  285.     /** 
  286.      * Holds the singleton instance of this class 
  287.      * @since 2.3.3 
  288.      * @var Jetpack 
  289.      */ 
  290.     static $instance = false; 
  291.  
  292.     /** 
  293.      * Singleton 
  294.      * @static 
  295.      */ 
  296.     public static function init() { 
  297.         if ( ! self::$instance ) { 
  298.             self::$instance = new Jetpack; 
  299.  
  300.             self::$instance->plugin_upgrade(); 
  301.         } 
  302.  
  303.         return self::$instance; 
  304.     } 
  305.  
  306.     /** 
  307.      * Must never be called statically 
  308.      */ 
  309.     function plugin_upgrade() { 
  310.         if ( Jetpack::is_active() ) { 
  311.             list( $version ) = explode( ':', Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'version' ) ); 
  312.             if ( JETPACK__VERSION != $version ) { 
  313.  
  314.                 // check which active modules actually exist and remove others from active_modules list 
  315.                 $unfiltered_modules = Jetpack::get_active_modules(); 
  316.                 $modules = array_filter( $unfiltered_modules, array( 'Jetpack', 'is_module' ) ); 
  317.                 if ( array_diff( $unfiltered_modules, $modules ) ) { 
  318.                     Jetpack::update_active_modules( $modules ); 
  319.                 } 
  320.  
  321.                 add_action( 'init', array( __CLASS__, 'activate_new_modules' ) ); 
  322.  
  323.                 // Upgrade to 4.3.0 
  324.                 if ( Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'identity_crisis_whitelist' ) ) { 
  325.                     Jetpack_Options::delete_option( 'identity_crisis_whitelist' ); 
  326.                 } 
  327.  
  328.                 // Make sure Markdown for posts gets turned back on 
  329.                 if ( ! get_option( 'wpcom_publish_posts_with_markdown' ) ) { 
  330.                     update_option( 'wpcom_publish_posts_with_markdown', true ); 
  331.                 } 
  332.  
  333.                 if ( did_action( 'wp_loaded' ) ) { 
  334.                     self::upgrade_on_load(); 
  335.                 } else { 
  336.                     add_action( 
  337.                         'wp_loaded',  
  338.                         array( __CLASS__, 'upgrade_on_load' ) 
  339.  ); 
  340.                 } 
  341.             } 
  342.         } 
  343.     } 
  344.  
  345.     /** 
  346.      * Runs upgrade routines that need to have modules loaded. 
  347.      */ 
  348.     static function upgrade_on_load() { 
  349.  
  350.         // Not attempting any upgrades if jetpack_modules_loaded did not fire. 
  351.         // This can happen in case Jetpack has been just upgraded and is 
  352.         // being initialized late during the page load. In this case we wait 
  353.         // until the next proper admin page load with Jetpack active. 
  354.         if ( ! did_action( 'jetpack_modules_loaded' ) ) { 
  355.             return; 
  356.         } 
  357.  
  358.         Jetpack::maybe_set_version_option(); 
  359.  
  360.         if ( class_exists( 'Jetpack_Widget_Conditions' ) ) { 
  361.             Jetpack_Widget_Conditions::migrate_post_type_rules(); 
  362.         } 
  363.     } 
  364.  
  365.     static function activate_manage( ) { 
  366.         if ( did_action( 'init' ) || current_filter() == 'init' ) { 
  367.             self::activate_module( 'manage', false, false ); 
  368.         } else if ( !  has_action( 'init' , array( __CLASS__, 'activate_manage' ) ) ) { 
  369.             add_action( 'init', array( __CLASS__, 'activate_manage' ) ); 
  370.         } 
  371.     } 
  372.  
  373.     static function update_active_modules( $modules ) { 
  374.         $current_modules = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'active_modules', array() ); 
  375.  
  376.         $success = Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'active_modules', array_unique( $modules ) ); 
  377.  
  378.         if ( is_array( $modules ) && is_array( $current_modules ) ) { 
  379.             $new_active_modules = array_diff( $modules, $current_modules ); 
  380.             foreach( $new_active_modules as $module ) { 
  381.                 /** 
  382.                  * Fires when a specific module is activated. 
  383.                  * 
  384.                  * @since 1.9.0 
  385.                  * 
  386.                  * @param string $module Module slug. 
  387.                  * @param boolean $success whether the module was activated. @since 4.2 
  388.                  */ 
  389.                 do_action( 'jetpack_activate_module', $module, $success ); 
  390.  
  391.                 /** 
  392.                  * Fires when a module is activated. 
  393.                  * The dynamic part of the filter, $module, is the module slug. 
  394.                  * 
  395.                  * @since 1.9.0 
  396.                  * 
  397.                  * @param string $module Module slug. 
  398.                  */ 
  399.                 do_action( "jetpack_activate_module_$module", $module ); 
  400.             } 
  401.  
  402.             $new_deactive_modules = array_diff( $current_modules, $modules ); 
  403.             foreach( $new_deactive_modules as $module ) { 
  404.                 /** 
  405.                  * Fired after a module has been deactivated. 
  406.                  * 
  407.                  * @since 4.2.0 
  408.                  * 
  409.                  * @param string $module Module slug. 
  410.                  * @param boolean $success whether the module was deactivated. 
  411.                  */ 
  412.                 do_action( 'jetpack_deactivate_module', $module, $success ); 
  413.                 /** 
  414.                  * Fires when a module is deactivated. 
  415.                  * The dynamic part of the filter, $module, is the module slug. 
  416.                  * 
  417.                  * @since 1.9.0 
  418.                  * 
  419.                  * @param string $module Module slug. 
  420.                  */ 
  421.                 do_action( "jetpack_deactivate_module_$module", $module ); 
  422.             } 
  423.         } 
  424.  
  425.         return $success; 
  426.     } 
  427.  
  428.     static function delete_active_modules() { 
  429.         self::update_active_modules( array() ); 
  430.     } 
  431.  
  432.     /** 
  433.      * Constructor.  Initializes WordPress hooks 
  434.      */ 
  435.     private function __construct() { 
  436.         /** 
  437.          * Check for and alert any deprecated hooks 
  438.          */ 
  439.         add_action( 'init', array( $this, 'deprecated_hooks' ) ); 
  440.  
  441.         /** 
  442.          * Load things that should only be in Network Admin. 
  443.          * 
  444.          * For now blow away everything else until a more full 
  445.          * understanding of what is needed at the network level is 
  446.          * available 
  447.          */ 
  448.         if( is_multisite() ) { 
  449.             Jetpack_Network::init(); 
  450.         } 
  451.  
  452.         add_action( 'set_user_role', array( $this, 'maybe_clear_other_linked_admins_transient' ), 10, 3 ); 
  453.  
  454.         // Unlink user before deleting the user from .com 
  455.         add_action( 'deleted_user', array( $this, 'unlink_user' ), 10, 1 ); 
  456.         add_action( 'remove_user_from_blog', array( $this, 'unlink_user' ), 10, 1 ); 
  457.  
  458.         if ( defined( 'XMLRPC_REQUEST' ) && XMLRPC_REQUEST && isset( $_GET['for'] ) && 'jetpack' == $_GET['for'] ) { 
  459.             @ini_set( 'display_errors', false ); // Display errors can cause the XML to be not well formed. 
  460.  
  461.             require_once JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'class.jetpack-xmlrpc-server.php'; 
  462.             $this->xmlrpc_server = new Jetpack_XMLRPC_Server(); 
  463.  
  464.             $this->require_jetpack_authentication(); 
  465.  
  466.             if ( Jetpack::is_active() ) { 
  467.                 // Hack to preserve $HTTP_RAW_POST_DATA 
  468.                 add_filter( 'xmlrpc_methods', array( $this, 'xmlrpc_methods' ) ); 
  469.  
  470.                 $signed = $this->verify_xml_rpc_signature(); 
  471.                 if ( $signed && ! is_wp_error( $signed ) ) { 
  472.                     // The actual API methods. 
  473.                     add_filter( 'xmlrpc_methods', array( $this->xmlrpc_server, 'xmlrpc_methods' ) ); 
  474.                 } else { 
  475.                     // The jetpack.authorize method should be available for unauthenticated users on a site with an 
  476.                     // active Jetpack connection, so that additional users can link their account. 
  477.                     add_filter( 'xmlrpc_methods', array( $this->xmlrpc_server, 'authorize_xmlrpc_methods' ) ); 
  478.                 } 
  479.             } else { 
  480.                 // The bootstrap API methods. 
  481.                 add_filter( 'xmlrpc_methods', array( $this->xmlrpc_server, 'bootstrap_xmlrpc_methods' ) ); 
  482.             } 
  483.  
  484.             // Now that no one can authenticate, and we're whitelisting all XML-RPC methods, force enable_xmlrpc on. 
  485.             add_filter( 'pre_option_enable_xmlrpc', '__return_true' ); 
  486.         } elseif ( 
  487.             is_admin() && 
  488.             isset( $_POST['action'] ) && ( 
  489.                 'jetpack_upload_file' == $_POST['action'] || 
  490.                 'jetpack_update_file' == $_POST['action'] 
  491.  ) 
  492.  ) { 
  493.             $this->require_jetpack_authentication(); 
  494.             $this->add_remote_request_handlers(); 
  495.         } else { 
  496.             if ( Jetpack::is_active() ) { 
  497.                 add_action( 'login_form_jetpack_json_api_authorization', array( &$this, 'login_form_json_api_authorization' ) ); 
  498.                 add_filter( 'xmlrpc_methods', array( $this, 'public_xmlrpc_methods' ) ); 
  499.             } 
  500.         } 
  501.  
  502.         if ( Jetpack::is_active() ) { 
  503.             Jetpack_Heartbeat::init(); 
  504.         } 
  505.  
  506.         add_filter( 'determine_current_user', array( $this, 'wp_rest_authenticate' ) ); 
  507.         add_filter( 'rest_authentication_errors', array( $this, 'wp_rest_authentication_errors' ) ); 
  508.  
  509.         add_action( 'jetpack_clean_nonces', array( 'Jetpack', 'clean_nonces' ) ); 
  510.         if ( ! wp_next_scheduled( 'jetpack_clean_nonces' ) ) { 
  511.             wp_schedule_event( time(), 'hourly', 'jetpack_clean_nonces' ); 
  512.         } 
  513.  
  514.         add_filter( 'xmlrpc_blog_options', array( $this, 'xmlrpc_options' ) ); 
  515.  
  516.         add_action( 'admin_init', array( $this, 'admin_init' ) ); 
  517.         add_action( 'admin_init', array( $this, 'dismiss_jetpack_notice' ) ); 
  518.  
  519.         add_filter( 'admin_body_class', array( $this, 'admin_body_class' ) ); 
  520.  
  521.         add_action( 'wp_dashboard_setup', array( $this, 'wp_dashboard_setup' ) ); 
  522.         // Filter the dashboard meta box order to swap the new one in in place of the old one. 
  523.         add_filter( 'get_user_option_meta-box-order_dashboard', array( $this, 'get_user_option_meta_box_order_dashboard' ) ); 
  524.  
  525.         // returns HTTPS support status 
  526.         add_action( 'wp_ajax_jetpack-recheck-ssl', array( $this, 'ajax_recheck_ssl' ) ); 
  527.  
  528.         // If any module option is updated before Jump Start is dismissed, hide Jump Start. 
  529.         add_action( 'update_option', array( $this, 'jumpstart_has_updated_module_option' ) ); 
  530.  
  531.         // JITM AJAX callback function 
  532.         add_action( 'wp_ajax_jitm_ajax', array( $this, 'jetpack_jitm_ajax_callback' ) ); 
  533.  
  534.         // Universal ajax callback for all tracking events triggered via js 
  535.         add_action( 'wp_ajax_jetpack_tracks', array( $this, 'jetpack_admin_ajax_tracks_callback' ) ); 
  536.  
  537.         add_action( 'wp_loaded', array( $this, 'register_assets' ) ); 
  538.         add_action( 'wp_enqueue_scripts', array( $this, 'devicepx' ) ); 
  539.         add_action( 'customize_controls_enqueue_scripts', array( $this, 'devicepx' ) ); 
  540.         add_action( 'admin_enqueue_scripts', array( $this, 'devicepx' ) ); 
  541.  
  542.         add_action( 'plugins_loaded', array( $this, 'extra_oembed_providers' ), 100 ); 
  543.  
  544.         /** 
  545.          * These actions run checks to load additional files. 
  546.          * They check for external files or plugins, so they need to run as late as possible. 
  547.          */ 
  548.         add_action( 'wp_head', array( $this, 'check_open_graph' ), 1 ); 
  549.         add_action( 'plugins_loaded', array( $this, 'check_twitter_tags' ), 999 ); 
  550.         add_action( 'plugins_loaded', array( $this, 'check_rest_api_compat' ), 1000 ); 
  551.  
  552.         add_filter( 'plugins_url', array( 'Jetpack', 'maybe_min_asset' ), 1, 3 ); 
  553.         add_filter( 'style_loader_tag', array( 'Jetpack', 'maybe_inline_style' ), 10, 2 ); 
  554.  
  555.         add_filter( 'map_meta_cap', array( $this, 'jetpack_custom_caps' ), 1, 4 ); 
  556.  
  557.         add_filter( 'jetpack_get_default_modules', array( $this, 'filter_default_modules' ) ); 
  558.         add_filter( 'jetpack_get_default_modules', array( $this, 'handle_deprecated_modules' ), 99 ); 
  559.  
  560.         // A filter to control all just in time messages 
  561.         add_filter( 'jetpack_just_in_time_msgs', '__return_true' ); 
  562.  
  563.         // Update the Jetpack plan from API on heartbeats 
  564.         add_action( 'jetpack_heartbeat', array( $this, 'refresh_active_plan_from_wpcom' ) ); 
  565.  
  566.         /** 
  567.          * This is the hack to concatinate all css files into one. 
  568.          * For description and reasoning see the implode_frontend_css method 
  569.          * 
  570.          * Super late priority so we catch all the registered styles 
  571.          */ 
  572.         if( !is_admin() ) { 
  573.             add_action( 'wp_print_styles', array( $this, 'implode_frontend_css' ), -1 ); // Run first 
  574.             add_action( 'wp_print_footer_scripts', array( $this, 'implode_frontend_css' ), -1 ); // Run first to trigger before `print_late_styles` 
  575.         } 
  576.     } 
  577.  
  578.     function jetpack_admin_ajax_tracks_callback() { 
  579.         // Check for nonce 
  580.         if ( ! isset( $_REQUEST['tracksNonce'] ) || ! wp_verify_nonce( $_REQUEST['tracksNonce'], 'jp-tracks-ajax-nonce' ) ) { 
  581.             wp_die( 'Permissions check failed.' ); 
  582.         } 
  583.  
  584.         if ( ! isset( $_REQUEST['tracksEventName'] ) || ! isset( $_REQUEST['tracksEventType'] ) ) { 
  585.             wp_die( 'No valid event name or type.' ); 
  586.         } 
  587.  
  588.         $tracks_data = array(); 
  589.         if ( 'click' === $_REQUEST['tracksEventType'] && isset( $_REQUEST['tracksEventProp'] ) ) { 
  590.             $tracks_data = array( 'clicked' => $_REQUEST['tracksEventProp'] ); 
  591.         } 
  592.  
  593.         JetpackTracking::record_user_event( $_REQUEST['tracksEventName'], $tracks_data ); 
  594.         wp_send_json_success(); 
  595.         wp_die(); 
  596.     } 
  597.  
  598.     /** 
  599.      * The callback for the JITM ajax requests. 
  600.      */ 
  601.     function jetpack_jitm_ajax_callback() { 
  602.         // Check for nonce 
  603.         if ( ! isset( $_REQUEST['jitmNonce'] ) || ! wp_verify_nonce( $_REQUEST['jitmNonce'], 'jetpack-jitm-nonce' ) ) { 
  604.             wp_die( 'Module activation failed due to lack of appropriate permissions' ); 
  605.         } 
  606.         if ( isset( $_REQUEST['jitmActionToTake'] ) && 'activate' == $_REQUEST['jitmActionToTake'] ) { 
  607.             $module_slug = $_REQUEST['jitmModule']; 
  608.             Jetpack::log( 'activate', $module_slug ); 
  609.             Jetpack::activate_module( $module_slug, false, false ); 
  610.             Jetpack::state( 'message', 'no_message' ); 
  611.  
  612.             //A Jetpack module is being activated through a JITM, track it 
  613.             $this->stat( 'jitm', $module_slug.'-activated-' . JETPACK__VERSION ); 
  614.             $this->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  615.  
  616.             wp_send_json_success(); 
  617.         } 
  618.         if ( isset( $_REQUEST['jitmActionToTake'] ) && 'dismiss' == $_REQUEST['jitmActionToTake'] ) { 
  619.             // get the hide_jitm options array 
  620.             $jetpack_hide_jitm = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'hide_jitm' ); 
  621.             $module_slug = $_REQUEST['jitmModule']; 
  622.  
  623.             if( ! $jetpack_hide_jitm ) { 
  624.                 $jetpack_hide_jitm = array( 
  625.                     $module_slug => 'hide' 
  626.  ); 
  627.             } else { 
  628.                 $jetpack_hide_jitm[$module_slug] = 'hide'; 
  629.             } 
  630.  
  631.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'hide_jitm', $jetpack_hide_jitm ); 
  632.  
  633.             //jitm is being dismissed forever, track it 
  634.             $this->stat( 'jitm', $module_slug.'-dismissed-' . JETPACK__VERSION ); 
  635.             $this->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  636.  
  637.             wp_send_json_success(); 
  638.         } 
  639.         if ( isset( $_REQUEST['jitmActionToTake'] ) && 'launch' == $_REQUEST['jitmActionToTake'] ) { 
  640.             $module_slug = $_REQUEST['jitmModule']; 
  641.  
  642.             // User went to WordPress.com, track this 
  643.             $this->stat( 'jitm', $module_slug.'-wordpress-tools-' . JETPACK__VERSION ); 
  644.             $this->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  645.  
  646.             wp_send_json_success(); 
  647.         } 
  648.         if ( isset( $_REQUEST['jitmActionToTake'] ) && 'viewed' == $_REQUEST['jitmActionToTake'] ) { 
  649.             $track = $_REQUEST['jitmModule']; 
  650.  
  651.             // User is viewing JITM, track it. 
  652.             $this->stat( 'jitm', $track . '-viewed-' . JETPACK__VERSION ); 
  653.             $this->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  654.  
  655.             wp_send_json_success(); 
  656.         } 
  657.     } 
  658.  
  659.     /** 
  660.      * If there are any stats that need to be pushed, but haven't been, push them now. 
  661.      */ 
  662.     function __destruct() { 
  663.         if ( ! empty( $this->stats ) ) { 
  664.             $this->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  665.         } 
  666.     } 
  667.  
  668.     function jetpack_custom_caps( $caps, $cap, $user_id, $args ) { 
  669.         switch( $cap ) { 
  670.             case 'jetpack_connect' : 
  671.             case 'jetpack_reconnect' : 
  672.                 if ( Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) { 
  673.                     $caps = array( 'do_not_allow' ); 
  674.                     break; 
  675.                 } 
  676.                 /** 
  677.                  * Pass through. If it's not development mode, these should match disconnect. 
  678.                  * Let users disconnect if it's development mode, just in case things glitch. 
  679.                  */ 
  680.             case 'jetpack_disconnect' : 
  681.                 /** 
  682.                  * In multisite, can individual site admins manage their own connection? 
  683.                  * 
  684.                  * Ideally, this should be extracted out to a separate filter in the Jetpack_Network class. 
  685.                  */ 
  686.                 if ( is_multisite() && ! is_super_admin() && is_plugin_active_for_network( 'jetpack/jetpack.php' ) ) { 
  687.                     if ( ! Jetpack_Network::init()->get_option( 'sub-site-connection-override' ) ) { 
  688.                         /** 
  689.                          * We need to update the option name -- it's terribly unclear which 
  690.                          * direction the override goes. 
  691.                          * 
  692.                          * @todo: Update the option name to `sub-sites-can-manage-own-connections` 
  693.                          */ 
  694.                         $caps = array( 'do_not_allow' ); 
  695.                         break; 
  696.                     } 
  697.                 } 
  698.  
  699.                 $caps = array( 'manage_options' ); 
  700.                 break; 
  701.             case 'jetpack_manage_modules' : 
  702.             case 'jetpack_activate_modules' : 
  703.             case 'jetpack_deactivate_modules' : 
  704.                 $caps = array( 'manage_options' ); 
  705.                 break; 
  706.             case 'jetpack_configure_modules' : 
  707.                 $caps = array( 'manage_options' ); 
  708.                 break; 
  709.             case 'jetpack_network_admin_page': 
  710.             case 'jetpack_network_settings_page': 
  711.                 $caps = array( 'manage_network_plugins' ); 
  712.                 break; 
  713.             case 'jetpack_network_sites_page': 
  714.                 $caps = array( 'manage_sites' ); 
  715.                 break; 
  716.             case 'jetpack_admin_page' : 
  717.                 if ( Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) { 
  718.                     $caps = array( 'manage_options' ); 
  719.                     break; 
  720.                 } else { 
  721.                     $caps = array( 'read' ); 
  722.                 } 
  723.                 break; 
  724.             case 'jetpack_connect_user' : 
  725.                 if ( Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) { 
  726.                     $caps = array( 'do_not_allow' ); 
  727.                     break; 
  728.                 } 
  729.                 $caps = array( 'read' ); 
  730.                 break; 
  731.         } 
  732.         return $caps; 
  733.     } 
  734.  
  735.     function require_jetpack_authentication() { 
  736.         // Don't let anyone authenticate 
  737.         $_COOKIE = array(); 
  738.         remove_all_filters( 'authenticate' ); 
  739.         remove_all_actions( 'wp_login_failed' ); 
  740.  
  741.         if ( Jetpack::is_active() ) { 
  742.             // Allow Jetpack authentication 
  743.             add_filter( 'authenticate', array( $this, 'authenticate_jetpack' ), 10, 3 ); 
  744.         } 
  745.     }

  747.     /** 
  748.      * Load language files 
  749.      * @action plugins_loaded 
  750.      */ 
  751.     public static function plugin_textdomain() { 
  752.         // Note to self, the third argument must not be hardcoded, to account for relocated folders. 
  753.         load_plugin_textdomain( 'jetpack', false, dirname( plugin_basename( JETPACK__PLUGIN_FILE ) ) . '/languages/' ); 
  754.     }

  756.     /** 
  757.      * Register assets for use in various modules and the Jetpack admin page. 
  758.      * 
  759.      * @uses wp_script_is, wp_register_script, plugins_url 
  760.      * @action wp_loaded 
  761.      * @return null 
  762.      */ 
  763.     public function register_assets() { 
  764.         if ( ! wp_script_is( 'spin', 'registered' ) ) { 
  765.             wp_register_script( 'spin', plugins_url( '_inc/spin.js', JETPACK__PLUGIN_FILE ), false, '1.3' ); 
  766.         } 
  767.  
  768.         if ( ! wp_script_is( 'jquery.spin', 'registered' ) ) { 
  769.             wp_register_script( 'jquery.spin', plugins_url( '_inc/jquery.spin.js', JETPACK__PLUGIN_FILE ) , array( 'jquery', 'spin' ), '1.3' ); 
  770.         } 
  771.  
  772.         if ( ! wp_script_is( 'jetpack-gallery-settings', 'registered' ) ) { 
  773.             wp_register_script( 'jetpack-gallery-settings', plugins_url( '_inc/gallery-settings.js', JETPACK__PLUGIN_FILE ), array( 'media-views' ), '20121225' ); 
  774.         } 
  775.  
  776.         if ( ! wp_script_is( 'jetpack-twitter-timeline', 'registered' ) ) { 
  777.             wp_register_script( 'jetpack-twitter-timeline', plugins_url( '_inc/twitter-timeline.js', JETPACK__PLUGIN_FILE ) , array( 'jquery' ), '4.0.0', true ); 
  778.         } 
  779.  
  780.         if ( ! wp_script_is( 'jetpack-facebook-embed', 'registered' ) ) { 
  781.             wp_register_script( 'jetpack-facebook-embed', plugins_url( '_inc/facebook-embed.js', __FILE__ ), array( 'jquery' ), null, true ); 
  782.  
  783.             /** This filter is documented in modules/sharedaddy/sharing-sources.php */ 
  784.             $fb_app_id = apply_filters( 'jetpack_sharing_facebook_app_id', '249643311490' ); 
  785.             if ( ! is_numeric( $fb_app_id ) ) { 
  786.                 $fb_app_id = ''; 
  787.             } 
  788.             wp_localize_script( 
  789.                 'jetpack-facebook-embed',  
  790.                 'jpfbembed',  
  791.                 array( 
  792.                     'appid' => $fb_app_id,  
  793.                     'locale' => $this->get_locale(),  
  794.  ) 
  795.  ); 
  796.         } 
  797.  
  798.         /** 
  799.          * As jetpack_register_genericons is by default fired off a hook,  
  800.          * the hook may have already fired by this point. 
  801.          * So, let's just trigger it manually. 
  802.          */ 
  803.         require_once( JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . '_inc/genericons.php' ); 
  804.         jetpack_register_genericons(); 
  805.  
  806.         /** 
  807.          * Register the social logos 
  808.          */ 
  809.         require_once( JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . '_inc/social-logos.php' ); 
  810.         jetpack_register_social_logos(); 
  811.  
  812.         if ( ! wp_style_is( 'jetpack-icons', 'registered' ) ) 
  813.             wp_register_style( 'jetpack-icons', plugins_url( 'css/jetpack-icons.min.css', JETPACK__PLUGIN_FILE ), false, JETPACK__VERSION ); 
  814.     } 
  815.  
  816.     /** 
  817.      * Guess locale from language code. 
  818.      * 
  819.      * @param string $lang Language code. 
  820.      * @return string|bool 
  821.      */ 
  822.     function guess_locale_from_lang( $lang ) { 
  823.         if ( 'en' === $lang || 'en_US' === $lang || ! $lang ) { 
  824.             return 'en_US'; 
  825.         } 
  826.  
  827.         if ( ! class_exists( 'GP_Locales' ) ) { 
  828.             if ( ! defined( 'JETPACK__GLOTPRESS_LOCALES_PATH' ) || ! file_exists( JETPACK__GLOTPRESS_LOCALES_PATH ) ) { 
  829.                 return false; 
  830.             } 
  831.  
  832.             require JETPACK__GLOTPRESS_LOCALES_PATH; 
  833.         } 
  834.  
  835.         if ( defined( 'IS_WPCOM' ) && IS_WPCOM ) { 
  836.             // WP.com: get_locale() returns 'it' 
  837.             $locale = GP_Locales::by_slug( $lang ); 
  838.         } else { 
  839.             // Jetpack: get_locale() returns 'it_IT'; 
  840.             $locale = GP_Locales::by_field( 'facebook_locale', $lang ); 
  841.         } 
  842.  
  843.         if ( ! $locale ) { 
  844.             return false; 
  845.         } 
  846.  
  847.         if ( empty( $locale->facebook_locale ) ) { 
  848.             if ( empty( $locale->wp_locale ) ) { 
  849.                 return false; 
  850.             } else { 
  851.                 // Facebook SDK is smart enough to fall back to en_US if a 
  852.                 // locale isn't supported. Since supported Facebook locales 
  853.                 // can fall out of sync, we'll attempt to use the known 
  854.                 // wp_locale value and rely on said fallback. 
  855.                 return $locale->wp_locale; 
  856.             } 
  857.         } 
  858.  
  859.         return $locale->facebook_locale; 
  860.     } 
  861.  
  862.     /** 
  863.      * Get the locale. 
  864.      * 
  865.      * @return string|bool 
  866.      */ 
  867.     function get_locale() { 
  868.         $locale = $this->guess_locale_from_lang( get_locale() ); 
  869.  
  870.         if ( ! $locale ) { 
  871.             $locale = 'en_US'; 
  872.         } 
  873.  
  874.         return $locale; 
  875.     }

  877.     /** 
  878.      * Device Pixels support 
  879.      * This improves the resolution of gravatars and wordpress.com uploads on hi-res and zoomed browsers. 
  880.      */ 
  881.     function devicepx() { 
  882.         if ( Jetpack::is_active() ) { 
  883.             wp_enqueue_script( 'devicepx', 'https://s0.wp.com/wp-content/js/devicepx-jetpack.js', array(), gmdate( 'oW' ), true ); 
  884.         } 
  885.     }

  902.     /** 
  903.      * Does the network allow new user and site registrations. 
  904.      * @return string

  906.     static function network_allow_new_registrations( $option = null ) { 
  907.         return ( in_array( get_site_option( 'registration' ), array('none', 'user', 'blog', 'all' ) ) ? get_site_option( 'registration') : 'none' ); 
  908.     }

  913.     static function network_add_new_users( $option = null ) {

  915.     } 
  916.     /**

  918.      *  -1 means NO LIMIT.

  921.     static function network_site_upload_space( $option = null ) { 
  922.         // value in MB

  943.     /**

  946.      */ 
  947.     static function network_enable_administration_menus( $option = null ) {

  949.     } 
  950.  
  951.     /** 
  952.      * If a user has been promoted to or demoted from admin, we need to clear the 
  953.      * jetpack_other_linked_admins transient. 
  954.      * 
  955.      * @since 4.3.2 
  956.      * @since 4.4.0  $old_roles is null by default and if it's not passed, the transient is cleared. 
  957.      * 
  958.      * @param int    $user_id   The user ID whose role changed. 
  959.      * @param string $role      The new role. 
  960.      * @param array  $old_roles An array of the user's previous roles. 
  961.      */ 
  962.     function maybe_clear_other_linked_admins_transient( $user_id, $role, $old_roles = null ) { 
  963.         if ( 'administrator' == $role 
  964.             || ( is_array( $old_roles ) && in_array( 'administrator', $old_roles ) ) 
  965.             || is_null( $old_roles ) 
  966.  ) { 
  967.             delete_transient( 'jetpack_other_linked_admins' ); 
  968.         } 
  969.     } 
  970.  
  971.     /** 
  972.      * Checks to see if there are any other users available to become primary 
  973.      * Users must both: 
  974.      * - Be linked to wpcom 
  975.      * - Be an admin 
  976.      * 
  977.      * @return mixed False if no other users are linked, Int if there are. 
  978.      */ 
  979.     static function get_other_linked_admins() { 
  980.         $other_linked_users = get_transient( 'jetpack_other_linked_admins' ); 
  981.  
  982.         if ( false === $other_linked_users ) { 
  983.             $admins = get_users( array( 'role' => 'administrator' ) ); 
  984.             if ( count( $admins ) > 1 ) { 
  985.                 $available = array(); 
  986.                 foreach ( $admins as $admin ) { 
  987.                     if ( Jetpack::is_user_connected( $admin->ID ) ) { 
  988.                         $available[] = $admin->ID; 
  989.                     } 
  990.                 } 
  991.  
  992.                 $count_connected_admins = count( $available ); 
  993.                 if ( count( $available ) > 1 ) { 
  994.                     $other_linked_users = $count_connected_admins; 
  995.                 } else { 
  996.                     $other_linked_users = 0; 
  997.                 } 
  998.             } else { 
  999.                 $other_linked_users = 0; 
  1000.             } 
  1001.  
  1002.             set_transient( 'jetpack_other_linked_admins', $other_linked_users, HOUR_IN_SECONDS ); 
  1003.         } 
  1004.  
  1005.         return ( 0 === $other_linked_users ) ? false : $other_linked_users; 
  1006.     }

  1008.     /** 
  1009.      * Return whether we are dealing with a multi network setup or not. 
  1010.      * The reason we are type casting this is because we want to avoid the situation where 
  1011.      * the result is false since when is_main_network_option return false it cases 
  1012.      * the rest the get_option( 'jetpack_is_multi_network' ); to return the value that is set in the 
  1013.      * database which could be set to anything as opposed to what this function returns. 
  1014.      * @param  bool  $option 
  1015.      * 
  1016.      * @return boolean 
  1017.      */ 
  1018.     public function is_main_network_option( $option ) { 
  1019.         // return '1' or '' 
  1020.         return (string) (bool) Jetpack::is_multi_network(); 
  1021.     }

  1024.      * Return true if we are with multi-site or multi-network false if we are dealing with single site.

  1033.     /** 
  1034.      * Implemented since there is no core is multi network function 
  1035.      * Right now there is no way to tell if we which network is the dominant network on the system 
  1036.      * 
  1037.      * @since  3.3 
  1038.      * @return boolean 
  1039.      */ 
  1040.     public static function is_multi_network() { 
  1041.         global  $wpdb; 
  1042.  
  1043.         // if we don't have a multi site setup no need to do any more 
  1044.         if ( ! is_multisite() ) { 
  1045.             return false; 
  1046.         } 
  1047.  
  1048.         $num_sites = $wpdb->get_var( "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM {$wpdb->site}" ); 
  1049.         if ( $num_sites > 1 ) { 
  1050.             return true; 
  1051.         } else { 
  1052.             return false; 
  1053.         } 
  1054.     }

  1072.     /** 
  1073.      * Get back if the current site is single user site. 
  1074.      * 
  1075.      * @return bool 
  1076.      */ 
  1077.     public static function is_single_user_site() { 
  1078.         global $wpdb; 
  1079.  
  1080.         if ( false === ( $some_users = get_transient( 'jetpack_is_single_user' ) ) ) { 
  1081.             $some_users = $wpdb->get_var( "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM (SELECT user_id FROM $wpdb->usermeta WHERE meta_key = '{$wpdb->prefix}capabilities' LIMIT 2) AS someusers" ); 
  1082.             set_transient( 'jetpack_is_single_user', (int) $some_users, 12 * HOUR_IN_SECONDS ); 
  1083.         } 
  1084.         return 1 === (int) $some_users; 
  1085.     }

  1087.     /** 
  1088.      * Returns true if the site has file write access false otherwise. 
  1089.      * @return string ( '1' | '0' ) 
  1090.      **/ 
  1091.     public static function file_system_write_access() { 
  1092.         if ( ! function_exists( 'get_filesystem_method' ) ) { 
  1093.             require_once( ABSPATH . 'wp-admin/includes/file.php' ); 
  1094.         } 
  1095.  
  1096.         require_once( ABSPATH . 'wp-admin/includes/template.php' ); 
  1097.  
  1098.         $filesystem_method = get_filesystem_method(); 
  1099.         if ( $filesystem_method === 'direct' ) { 
  1100.             return 1; 
  1101.         } 
  1102.  
  1103.         ob_start(); 
  1104.         $filesystem_credentials_are_stored = request_filesystem_credentials( self_admin_url() ); 
  1105.         ob_end_clean(); 
  1106.         if ( $filesystem_credentials_are_stored ) { 
  1107.             return 1; 
  1108.         } 
  1109.         return 0; 
  1110.     }

  1150.     /** 
  1151.      * jetpack_updates is saved in the following schema: 
  1152.      * 
  1153.      * array ( 
  1154.      *      'plugins' => (int) Number of plugin updates available. 
  1155.      *      'themes' => (int) Number of theme updates available. 
  1156.      *      'wordpress' => (int) Number of WordPress core updates available. 
  1157.      *      'translations' => (int) Number of translation updates available. 
  1158.      *      'total' => (int) Total of all available updates. 
  1159.      *      'wp_update_version' => (string) The latest available version of WordPress, only present if a WordPress update is needed. 
  1160.      * ) 
  1161.      * @return array 
  1162.      */ 
  1163.     public static function get_updates() { 
  1164.         $update_data = wp_get_update_data(); 
  1165.  
  1166.         // Stores the individual update counts as well as the total count. 
  1167.         if ( isset( $update_data['counts'] ) ) { 
  1168.             $updates = $update_data['counts']; 
  1169.         } 
  1170.  
  1171.         // If we need to update WordPress core, let's find the latest version number. 
  1172.         if ( ! empty( $updates['wordpress'] ) ) { 
  1173.             $cur = get_preferred_from_update_core(); 
  1174.             if ( isset( $cur->response ) && 'upgrade' === $cur->response ) { 
  1175.                 $updates['wp_update_version'] = $cur->current; 
  1176.             } 
  1177.         } 
  1178.         return isset( $updates ) ? $updates : array(); 
  1179.     } 
  1180.  
  1181.     public static function get_update_details() {

  1183.             'update_core' => get_site_transient( 'update_core' ),  
  1184.             'update_plugins' => get_site_transient( 'update_plugins' ),  
  1185.             'update_themes' => get_site_transient( 'update_themes' ),  
  1186.  ); 
  1187.         return $update_details; 
  1188.     }

  1206.     /** 
  1207.      * Make an API call to WordPress.com for plan status 
  1208.      * 
  1209.      * @uses Jetpack_Options::get_option() 
  1210.      * @uses Jetpack_Client::wpcom_json_api_request_as_blog() 
  1211.      * @uses update_option() 
  1212.      * 
  1213.      * @access public 
  1214.      * @static 
  1215.      * 
  1216.      * @return bool True if plan is updated, false if no update 
  1217.      */ 
  1218.     public static function refresh_active_plan_from_wpcom() { 
  1219.         // Make the API request 
  1220.         $request = sprintf( '/sites/%d', Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'id' ) ); 
  1221.         $response = Jetpack_Client::wpcom_json_api_request_as_blog( $request, '1.1' ); 
  1222.  
  1223.         // Bail if there was an error or malformed response 
  1224.         if ( is_wp_error( $response ) || ! is_array( $response ) || ! isset( $response['body'] ) ) { 
  1225.             return false; 
  1226.         } 
  1227.  
  1228.         // Decode the results 
  1229.         $results = json_decode( $response['body'], true ); 
  1230.  
  1231.         // Bail if there were no results or plan details returned 
  1232.         if ( ! is_array( $results ) || ! isset( $results['plan'] ) ) { 
  1233.             return false; 
  1234.         } 
  1235.  
  1236.         // Store the option and return true if updated 
  1237.         return update_option( 'jetpack_active_plan', $results['plan'] ); 
  1238.     } 
  1239.  
  1240.     /** 
  1241.      * Get the plan that this Jetpack site is currently using 
  1242.      * 
  1243.      * @uses get_option() 
  1244.      * 
  1245.      * @access public 
  1246.      * @static 
  1247.      * 
  1248.      * @return array Active Jetpack plan details 
  1249.      */ 
  1250.     public static function get_active_plan() { 
  1251.         $plan = get_option( 'jetpack_active_plan' ); 
  1252.  
  1253.         // Set the default options 
  1254.         if ( ! $plan ) { 
  1255.             $plan = array( 
  1256.                 'product_slug' => 'jetpack_free',  
  1257.                 'supports' => array(),  
  1258.                 'class' => 'free',  
  1259.  ); 
  1260.         } 
  1261.  
  1262.         // Define what paid modules are supported by personal plans 
  1263.         $personal_plans = array( 
  1264.             'jetpack_personal',  
  1265.             'jetpack_personal_monthly',  
  1266.             'personal-bundle',  
  1267.  ); 
  1268.  
  1269.         if ( in_array( $plan['product_slug'], $personal_plans ) ) { 
  1270.             $plan['supports'] = array( 
  1271.                 'akismet',  
  1272.  ); 
  1273.             $plan['class'] = 'personal'; 
  1274.         } 
  1275.  
  1276.         // Define what paid modules are supported by premium plans 
  1277.         $premium_plans = array( 
  1278.             'jetpack_premium',  
  1279.             'jetpack_premium_monthly',  
  1280.             'value_bundle',  
  1281.  ); 
  1282.  
  1283.         if ( in_array( $plan['product_slug'], $premium_plans ) ) { 
  1284.             $plan['supports'] = array( 
  1285.                 'videopress',  
  1286.                 'akismet',  
  1287.                 'vaultpress',  
  1288.                 'wordads',  
  1289.  ); 
  1290.             $plan['class'] = 'premium'; 
  1291.         } 
  1292.  
  1293.         // Define what paid modules are supported by professional plans 
  1294.         $business_plans = array( 
  1295.             'jetpack_business',  
  1296.             'jetpack_business_monthly',  
  1297.             'business-bundle',  
  1298.  ); 
  1299.  
  1300.         if ( in_array( $plan['product_slug'], $business_plans ) ) { 
  1301.             $plan['supports'] = array( 
  1302.                 'videopress',  
  1303.                 'akismet',  
  1304.                 'vaultpress',  
  1305.                 'seo-tools',  
  1306.                 'google-analytics',  
  1307.                 'wordads',  
  1308.  ); 
  1309.             $plan['class'] = 'business'; 
  1310.         } 
  1311.  
  1312.         // Make sure we have an array here in the event database data is stale 
  1313.         if ( ! isset( $plan['supports'] ) ) { 
  1314.             $plan['supports'] = array(); 
  1315.         } 
  1316.  
  1317.         return $plan; 
  1318.     }

  1320.     /** 
  1321.      * Determine whether the active plan supports a particular feature

  1340.     /** 
  1341.      * Is Jetpack in development (offline) mode? 
  1342.      */ 
  1343.     public static function is_development_mode() { 
  1344.         $development_mode = false; 
  1345.  
  1346.         if ( defined( 'JETPACK_DEV_DEBUG' ) ) { 
  1347.             $development_mode = JETPACK_DEV_DEBUG; 
  1348.         } elseif ( $site_url = site_url() ) { 
  1349.             $development_mode = false === strpos( $site_url, '.' ); 
  1350.         } 
  1351.  
  1352.         /** 
  1353.          * Filters Jetpack's development mode. 
  1354.          * 
  1355.          * @see https://jetpack.com/support/development-mode/ 
  1356.          * 
  1357.          * @since 2.2.1 
  1358.          * 
  1359.          * @param bool $development_mode Is Jetpack's development mode active. 
  1360.          */ 
  1361.         return apply_filters( 'jetpack_development_mode', $development_mode ); 
  1362.     } 
  1363.  
  1364.     /** 
  1365.     * Get Jetpack development mode notice text and notice class. 
  1366.     * 
  1367.     * Mirrors the checks made in Jetpack::is_development_mode 
  1368.     * 
  1369.     */ 
  1370.     public static function show_development_mode_notice() { 
  1371.         if ( Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) { 
  1372.             if ( defined( 'JETPACK_DEV_DEBUG' ) && JETPACK_DEV_DEBUG ) { 
  1373.                 $notice = sprintf( 
  1374.                     /** translators: %s is a URL */ 
  1375.                     __( 'In <a href="%s" target="_blank">Development Mode</a>, via the JETPACK_DEV_DEBUG constant being defined in wp-config.php or elsewhere.', 'jetpack' ),  
  1376.                     'https://jetpack.com/support/development-mode/' 
  1377.  ); 
  1378.             } elseif ( site_url() && false === strpos( site_url(), '.' ) ) { 
  1379.                 $notice = sprintf( 
  1380.                     /** translators: %s is a URL */ 
  1381.                     __( 'In <a href="%s" target="_blank">Development Mode</a>, via site URL lacking a dot (e.g. http://localhost).', 'jetpack' ),  
  1382.                     'https://jetpack.com/support/development-mode/' 
  1383.  ); 
  1384.             } else { 
  1385.                 $notice = sprintf( 
  1386.                     /** translators: %s is a URL */ 
  1387.                     __( 'In <a href="%s" target="_blank">Development Mode</a>, via the jetpack_development_mode filter.', 'jetpack' ),  
  1388.                     'https://jetpack.com/support/development-mode/' 
  1389.  ); 
  1390.             } 
  1391.  
  1392.             echo '<div class="updated" style="border-color: #f0821e;"><p>' . $notice . '</p></div>'; 
  1393.         } 
  1394.  
  1395.         // Throw up a notice if using a development version and as for feedback. 
  1396.         if ( Jetpack::is_development_version() ) { 
  1397.             /** translators: %s is a URL */ 
  1398.             $notice = sprintf( __( 'You are currently running a development version of Jetpack. <a href="%s" target="_blank">Submit your feedback</a>', 'jetpack' ), 'https://jetpack.com/contact-support/beta-group/' ); 
  1399.  
  1400.             echo '<div class="updated" style="border-color: #f0821e;"><p>' . $notice . '</p></div>'; 
  1401.         } 
  1402.         // Throw up a notice if using staging mode 
  1403.         if ( Jetpack::is_staging_site() ) { 
  1404.             /** translators: %s is a URL */ 
  1405.             $notice = sprintf( __( 'You are running Jetpack on a <a href="%s" target="_blank">staging server</a>.', 'jetpack' ), 'https://jetpack.com/support/staging-sites/' ); 
  1406.  
  1407.             echo '<div class="updated" style="border-color: #f0821e;"><p>' . $notice . '</p></div>'; 
  1408.         } 
  1409.     } 
  1410.  
  1411.     /** 
  1412.      * Whether Jetpack's version maps to a public release, or a development version. 
  1413.      */ 
  1414.     public static function is_development_version() { 
  1415.         /** 
  1416.          * Allows filtering whether this is a development version of Jetpack. 
  1417.          * 
  1418.          * This filter is especially useful for tests. 
  1419.          * 
  1420.          * @since 4.3.0 
  1421.          * 
  1422.          * @param bool $development_version Is this a develoment version of Jetpack? 
  1423.          */ 
  1424.         return (bool) apply_filters( 
  1425.             'jetpack_development_version',  
  1426.             ! preg_match( '/^\d+(\.\d+)+$/', Jetpack_Constants::get_constant( 'JETPACK__VERSION' ) ) 
  1427.  ); 
  1428.     } 
  1429.  
  1430.     /** 
  1431.      * Is a given user (or the current user if none is specified) linked to a WordPress.com user? 
  1432.      */ 
  1433.     public static function is_user_connected( $user_id = false ) { 
  1434.         $user_id = false === $user_id ? get_current_user_id() : absint( $user_id ); 
  1435.         if ( ! $user_id ) { 
  1436.             return false; 
  1437.         } 
  1438.  
  1439.         return (bool) Jetpack_Data::get_access_token( $user_id ); 
  1440.     } 
  1441.  
  1442.     /** 
  1443.      * Get the wpcom user data of the current|specified connected user. 
  1444.      */ 
  1445.     public static function get_connected_user_data( $user_id = null ) { 
  1446.         if ( ! $user_id ) { 
  1447.             $user_id = get_current_user_id(); 
  1448.         } 
  1449.  
  1450.         $transient_key = "jetpack_connected_user_data_$user_id"; 
  1451.  
  1452.         if ( $cached_user_data = get_transient( $transient_key ) ) { 
  1453.             return $cached_user_data; 
  1454.         } 
  1455.  
  1456.         Jetpack::load_xml_rpc_client(); 
  1457.         $xml = new Jetpack_IXR_Client( array( 
  1458.             'user_id' => $user_id,  
  1459.  ) ); 
  1460.         $xml->query( 'wpcom.getUser' ); 
  1461.         if ( ! $xml->isError() ) { 
  1462.             $user_data = $xml->getResponse(); 
  1463.             set_transient( $transient_key, $xml->getResponse(), DAY_IN_SECONDS ); 
  1464.             return $user_data; 
  1465.         } 
  1466.  
  1467.         return false; 
  1468.     } 
  1469.  
  1470.     /** 
  1471.      * Get the wpcom email of the current|specified connected user. 
  1472.      */ 
  1473.     public static function get_connected_user_email( $user_id = null ) { 
  1474.         if ( ! $user_id ) { 
  1475.             $user_id = get_current_user_id(); 
  1476.         } 
  1477.         Jetpack::load_xml_rpc_client(); 
  1478.         $xml = new Jetpack_IXR_Client( array( 
  1479.             'user_id' => $user_id,  
  1480.  ) ); 
  1481.         $xml->query( 'wpcom.getUserEmail' ); 
  1482.         if ( ! $xml->isError() ) { 
  1483.             return $xml->getResponse(); 
  1484.         } 
  1485.         return false; 
  1486.     } 
  1487.  
  1488.     /**

  1490.      */

  1492.         $master_user_id = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'master_user' ); 
  1493.         if ( $master_user_id ) { 
  1494.             return self::get_connected_user_email( $master_user_id ); 
  1495.         } 
  1496.         return ''; 
  1497.     } 
  1498.  
  1499.     function current_user_is_connection_owner() { 
  1500.         $user_token = Jetpack_Data::get_access_token( JETPACK_MASTER_USER ); 
  1501.         return $user_token && is_object( $user_token ) && isset( $user_token->external_user_id ) && get_current_user_id() === $user_token->external_user_id; 
  1502.     }

  1504.     /** 
  1505.      * Add any extra oEmbed providers that we know about and use on wpcom for feature parity. 
  1506.      */ 
  1507.     function extra_oembed_providers() { 
  1508.         // Cloudup: https://dev.cloudup.com/#oembed 
  1509.         wp_oembed_add_provider( 'https://cloudup.com/*' , 'https://cloudup.com/oembed' ); 
  1510.         wp_oembed_add_provider( 'https://me.sh/*', 'https://me.sh/oembed?format=json' ); 
  1511.         wp_oembed_add_provider( '#https?://(www\.)?gfycat\.com/.*#i', 'https://api.gfycat.com/v1/oembed', true ); 
  1512.         wp_oembed_add_provider( '#https?://[^.]+\.(wistia\.com|wi\.st)/(medias|embed)/.*#', 'https://fast.wistia.com/oembed', true ); 
  1513.         wp_oembed_add_provider( '#https?://sketchfab\.com/.*#i', 'https://sketchfab.com/oembed', true ); 
  1514.         wp_oembed_add_provider( '#https?://(www\.)?icloud\.com/keynote/.*#i', 'https://iwmb.icloud.com/iwmb/oembed', true ); 
  1515.     }

  1524.  
  1525.     /** 
  1526.      * Loads the currently active modules. 
  1527.      */ 
  1528.     public static function load_modules() { 
  1529.         if ( ! self::is_active() && !self::is_development_mode() ) { 
  1530.             if ( ! is_multisite() || ! get_site_option( 'jetpack_protect_active' ) ) { 
  1531.                 return; 
  1532.             } 
  1533.         } 
  1534.  
  1535.         $version = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'version' ); 
  1536.         if ( ! $version ) { 
  1537.             $version = $old_version = JETPACK__VERSION . ':' . time(); 
  1538.             /** This action is documented in class.jetpack.php */ 
  1539.             do_action( 'updating_jetpack_version', $version, false ); 
  1540.             Jetpack_Options::update_options( compact( 'version', 'old_version' ) ); 
  1541.         } 
  1542.         list( $version ) = explode( ':', $version ); 
  1543.  
  1544.         $modules = array_filter( Jetpack::get_active_modules(), array( 'Jetpack', 'is_module' ) ); 
  1545.  
  1546.         $modules_data = array(); 
  1547.  
  1548.         // Don't load modules that have had "Major" changes since the stored version until they have been deactivated/reactivated through the lint check. 
  1549.         if ( version_compare( $version, JETPACK__VERSION, '<' ) ) { 
  1550.             $updated_modules = array(); 
  1551.             foreach ( $modules as $module ) { 
  1552.                 $modules_data[ $module ] = Jetpack::get_module( $module ); 
  1553.                 if ( ! isset( $modules_data[ $module ]['changed'] ) ) { 
  1554.                     continue; 
  1555.                 } 
  1556.  
  1557.                 if ( version_compare( $modules_data[ $module ]['changed'], $version, '<=' ) ) { 
  1558.                     continue; 
  1559.                 } 
  1560.  
  1561.                 $updated_modules[] = $module; 
  1562.             } 
  1563.  
  1564.             $modules = array_diff( $modules, $updated_modules ); 
  1565.         } 
  1566.  
  1567.         $is_development_mode = Jetpack::is_development_mode(); 
  1568.  
  1569.         foreach ( $modules as $index => $module ) { 
  1570.             // If we're in dev mode, disable modules requiring a connection 
  1571.             if ( $is_development_mode ) { 
  1572.                 // Prime the pump if we need to 
  1573.                 if ( empty( $modules_data[ $module ] ) ) { 
  1574.                     $modules_data[ $module ] = Jetpack::get_module( $module ); 
  1575.                 } 
  1576.                 // If the module requires a connection, but we're in local mode, don't include it. 
  1577.                 if ( $modules_data[ $module ]['requires_connection'] ) { 
  1578.                     continue; 
  1579.                 } 
  1580.             } 
  1581.  
  1582.             if ( did_action( 'jetpack_module_loaded_' . $module ) ) { 
  1583.                 continue; 
  1584.             } 
  1585.  
  1586.             if ( ! include_once( Jetpack::get_module_path( $module ) ) ) { 
  1587.                 unset( $modules[ $index ] ); 
  1588.                 self::update_active_modules( array_values( $modules ) ); 
  1589.                 continue; 
  1590.             } 
  1591.  
  1592.             /** 
  1593.              * Fires when a specific module is loaded. 
  1594.              * The dynamic part of the hook, $module, is the module slug. 
  1595.              * 
  1596.              * @since 1.1.0 
  1597.              */ 
  1598.             do_action( 'jetpack_module_loaded_' . $module ); 
  1599.         } 
  1600.  
  1601.         /** 
  1602.          * Fires when all the modules are loaded. 
  1603.          * 
  1604.          * @since 1.1.0 
  1605.          */ 
  1606.         do_action( 'jetpack_modules_loaded' ); 
  1607.  
  1608.         // Load module-specific code that is needed even when a module isn't active. Loaded here because code contained therein may need actions such as setup_theme. 
  1609.         if ( Jetpack::is_active() || Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) 
  1610.             require_once( JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'modules/module-extras.php' ); 
  1611.     } 
  1612.  
  1613.     /** 
  1614.      * Check if Jetpack's REST API compat file should be included 
  1615.      * @action plugins_loaded 
  1616.      * @return null 
  1617.      */ 
  1618.     public function check_rest_api_compat() { 
  1619.         /** 
  1620.          * Filters the list of REST API compat files to be included. 
  1621.          * 
  1622.          * @since 2.2.5 
  1623.          * 
  1624.          * @param array $args Array of REST API compat files to include. 
  1625.          */ 
  1626.         $_jetpack_rest_api_compat_includes = apply_filters( 'jetpack_rest_api_compat', array() ); 
  1627.  
  1628.         if ( function_exists( 'bbpress' ) ) 
  1629.             $_jetpack_rest_api_compat_includes[] = JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'class.jetpack-bbpress-json-api-compat.php'; 
  1630.  
  1631.         foreach ( $_jetpack_rest_api_compat_includes as $_jetpack_rest_api_compat_include ) 
  1632.             require_once $_jetpack_rest_api_compat_include; 
  1633.     } 
  1634.  
  1635.     /** 
  1636.      * Gets all plugins currently active in values, regardless of whether they're 
  1637.      * traditionally activated or network activated. 
  1638.      * 
  1639.      * @todo Store the result in core's object cache maybe? 
  1640.      */ 
  1641.     public static function get_active_plugins() { 
  1642.         $active_plugins = (array) get_option( 'active_plugins', array() ); 
  1643.  
  1644.         if ( is_multisite() ) { 
  1645.             // Due to legacy code, active_sitewide_plugins stores them in the keys,  
  1646.             // whereas active_plugins stores them in the values. 
  1647.             $network_plugins = array_keys( get_site_option( 'active_sitewide_plugins', array() ) ); 
  1648.             if ( $network_plugins ) { 
  1649.                 $active_plugins = array_merge( $active_plugins, $network_plugins ); 
  1650.             } 
  1651.         } 
  1652.  
  1653.         sort( $active_plugins ); 
  1654.  
  1655.         return array_unique( $active_plugins ); 
  1656.     } 
  1657.  
  1658.     /** 
  1659.      * Gets and parses additional plugin data to send with the heartbeat data 
  1660.      * 
  1661.      * @since 3.8.1 
  1662.      * 
  1663.      * @return array Array of plugin data 
  1664.      */ 
  1665.     public static function get_parsed_plugin_data() { 
  1666.         if ( ! function_exists( 'get_plugins' ) ) { 
  1667.             require_once( ABSPATH . 'wp-admin/includes/plugin.php' ); 
  1668.         } 
  1669.         /** This filter is documented in wp-admin/includes/class-wp-plugins-list-table.php */ 
  1670.         $all_plugins = apply_filters( 'all_plugins', get_plugins() ); 
  1671.         $active_plugins = Jetpack::get_active_plugins(); 
  1672.  
  1673.         $plugins = array(); 
  1674.         foreach ( $all_plugins as $path => $plugin_data ) { 
  1675.             $plugins[ $path ] = array( 
  1676.                     'is_active' => in_array( $path, $active_plugins ),  
  1677.                     'file' => $path,  
  1678.                     'name' => $plugin_data['Name'],  
  1679.                     'version' => $plugin_data['Version'],  
  1680.                     'author' => $plugin_data['Author'],  
  1681.  ); 
  1682.         } 
  1683.  
  1684.         return $plugins; 
  1685.     } 
  1686.  
  1687.     /** 
  1688.      * Gets and parses theme data to send with the heartbeat data 
  1689.      * 
  1690.      * @since 3.8.1 
  1691.      * 
  1692.      * @return array Array of theme data 
  1693.      */ 
  1694.     public static function get_parsed_theme_data() { 
  1695.         $all_themes = wp_get_themes( array( 'allowed' => true ) ); 
  1696.         $header_keys = array( 'Name', 'Author', 'Version', 'ThemeURI', 'AuthorURI', 'Status', 'Tags' ); 
  1697.  
  1698.         $themes = array(); 
  1699.         foreach ( $all_themes as $slug => $theme_data ) { 
  1700.             $theme_headers = array(); 
  1701.             foreach ( $header_keys as $header_key ) { 
  1702.                 $theme_headers[ $header_key ] = $theme_data->get( $header_key ); 
  1703.             } 
  1704.  
  1705.             $themes[ $slug ] = array( 
  1706.                     'is_active_theme' => $slug == wp_get_theme()->get_template(),  
  1707.                     'slug' => $slug,  
  1708.                     'theme_root' => $theme_data->get_theme_root_uri(),  
  1709.                     'parent' => $theme_data->parent(),  
  1710.                     'headers' => $theme_headers 
  1711.  ); 
  1712.         } 
  1713.  
  1714.         return $themes; 
  1715.     }

  1727.     /**

  1734.      */ 
  1735.     public function check_open_graph() {

  1737.             add_filter( 'jetpack_enable_open_graph', '__return_true', 0 );

  1744.                 if ( in_array( $plugin, $active_plugins ) ) { 
  1745.                     add_filter( 'jetpack_enable_open_graph', '__return_false', 99 ); 
  1746.                     break; 
  1747.                 } 
  1748.             } 
  1749.         }

  1813.     /** 
  1814.      * Returns the requested option.  Looks in jetpack_options or jetpack_$name as appropriate. 
  1815.       * 
  1816.      * @param string $name    Option name 
  1817.      * @param mixed  $default (optional) 
  1818.      */

  1821.     } 
  1822.  
  1823.     /** 
  1824.     * Stores two secrets and a timestamp so WordPress.com can make a request back and verify an action 
  1825.     * Does some extra verification so urls (such as those to public-api, register, etc) can't just be crafted 
  1826.     * $name must be a registered option name. 
  1827.     */ 
  1828.     public static function create_nonce( $name ) { 
  1829.         $secret = wp_generate_password( 32, false ) . ':' . wp_generate_password( 32, false ) . ':' . ( time() + 600 ); 
  1830.  
  1831.         Jetpack_Options::update_option( $name, $secret ); 
  1832.         @list( $secret_1, $secret_2, $eol ) = explode( ':', Jetpack_Options::get_option( $name ) ); 
  1833.         if ( empty( $secret_1 ) || empty( $secret_2 ) || $eol < time() ) 
  1834.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'missing_secrets' ); 
  1835.  
  1836.         return array( 
  1837.             'secret_1' => $secret_1,  
  1838.             'secret_2' => $secret_2,  
  1839.             'eol' => $eol,  
  1840.  ); 
  1841.     }
