  1877.  
  1878.     /** 
  1879.      * Enters a user token into the user_tokens option 
  1880.      * 
  1881.      * @param int $user_id 
  1882.      * @param string $token 
  1883.      * return bool 
  1884.      */ 
  1885.     public static function update_user_token( $user_id, $token, $is_master_user ) { 
  1886.         // not designed for concurrent updates 
  1887.         $user_tokens = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'user_tokens' ); 
  1888.         if ( ! is_array( $user_tokens ) ) 
  1889.             $user_tokens = array(); 
  1890.         $user_tokens[$user_id] = $token; 
  1891.         if ( $is_master_user ) { 
  1892.             $master_user = $user_id; 
  1893.             $options = compact( 'user_tokens', 'master_user' ); 
  1894.         } else { 
  1895.             $options = compact( 'user_tokens' ); 
  1896.         } 
  1897.         return Jetpack_Options::update_options( $options ); 
  1898.     } 
  1899.  
  1900.     /** 
  1901.      * Returns an array of all PHP files in the specified absolute path. 
  1902.      * Equivalent to glob( "$absolute_path/**.php" ). 
  1903.      * 
  1904.      * @param string $absolute_path The absolute path of the directory to search. 
  1905.      * @return array Array of absolute paths to the PHP files. 
  1906.      */ 
  1907.     public static function glob_php( $absolute_path ) { 
  1908.         if ( function_exists( 'glob' ) ) { 
  1909.             return glob( "$absolute_path/*.php" ); 
  1910.         } 
  1911.  
  1912.         $absolute_path = untrailingslashit( $absolute_path ); 
  1913.         $files = array(); 
  1914.         if ( ! $dir = @opendir( $absolute_path ) ) { 
  1915.             return $files; 
  1916.         } 
  1917.  
  1918.         while ( false !== $file = readdir( $dir ) ) { 
  1919.             if ( '.' == substr( $file, 0, 1 ) || '.php' != substr( $file, -4 ) ) { 
  1920.                 continue; 
  1921.             } 
  1922.  
  1923.             $file = "$absolute_path/$file"; 
  1924.  
  1925.             if ( ! is_file( $file ) ) { 
  1926.                 continue; 
  1927.             } 
  1928.  
  1929.             $files[] = $file; 
  1930.         } 
  1931.  
  1932.         closedir( $dir ); 
  1933.  
  1934.         return $files; 
  1935.     } 
  1936.  
  1937.     public static function activate_new_modules( $redirect = false ) { 
  1938.         if ( ! Jetpack::is_active() && ! Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) { 
  1939.             return; 
  1940.         } 
  1941.  
  1942.         $jetpack_old_version = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'version' ); // [sic] 
  1943.         if ( ! $jetpack_old_version ) { 
  1944.             $jetpack_old_version = $version = $old_version = '1.1:' . time(); 
  1945.             /** This action is documented in class.jetpack.php */ 
  1946.             do_action( 'updating_jetpack_version', $version, false ); 
  1947.             Jetpack_Options::update_options( compact( 'version', 'old_version' ) ); 
  1948.         } 
  1949.  
  1950.         list( $jetpack_version ) = explode( ':', $jetpack_old_version ); // [sic] 
  1951.  
  1952.         if ( version_compare( JETPACK__VERSION, $jetpack_version, '<=' ) ) { 
  1953.             return; 
  1954.         } 
  1955.  
  1956.         $active_modules = Jetpack::get_active_modules(); 
  1957.         $reactivate_modules = array(); 
  1958.         foreach ( $active_modules as $active_module ) { 
  1959.             $module = Jetpack::get_module( $active_module ); 
  1960.             if ( ! isset( $module['changed'] ) ) { 
  1961.                 continue; 
  1962.             } 
  1963.  
  1964.             if ( version_compare( $module['changed'], $jetpack_version, '<=' ) ) { 
  1965.                 continue; 
  1966.             } 
  1967.  
  1968.             $reactivate_modules[] = $active_module; 
  1969.             Jetpack::deactivate_module( $active_module ); 
  1970.         } 
  1971.  
  1972.         $new_version = JETPACK__VERSION . ':' . time(); 
  1973.         /** This action is documented in class.jetpack.php */ 
  1974.         do_action( 'updating_jetpack_version', $new_version, $jetpack_old_version ); 
  1975.         Jetpack_Options::update_options( 
  1976.             array( 
  1977.                 'version' => $new_version,  
  1978.                 'old_version' => $jetpack_old_version,  
  1979.  ) 
  1980.  ); 
  1981.  
  1982.         Jetpack::state( 'message', 'modules_activated' ); 
  1983.         Jetpack::activate_default_modules( $jetpack_version, JETPACK__VERSION, $reactivate_modules ); 
  1984.  
  1985.         if ( $redirect ) { 
  1986.             $page = 'jetpack'; // make sure we redirect to either settings or the jetpack page 
  1987.             if ( isset( $_GET['page'] ) && in_array( $_GET['page'], array( 'jetpack', 'jetpack_modules' ) ) ) { 
  1988.                 $page = $_GET['page']; 
  1989.             } 
  1990.  
  1991.             wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=' . $page ) ); 
  1992.             exit; 
  1993.         } 
  1994.     } 
  1995.  
  1996.     /** 
  1997.      * List available Jetpack modules. Simply lists .php files in /modules/. 
  1998.      * Make sure to tuck away module "library" files in a sub-directory. 
  1999.      */ 
  2000.     public static function get_available_modules( $min_version = false, $max_version = false ) { 
  2001.         static $modules = null; 
  2002.  
  2003.         if ( ! isset( $modules ) ) { 
  2004.             $available_modules_option = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'available_modules', array() ); 
  2005.             // Use the cache if we're on the front-end and it's available... 
  2006.             if ( ! is_admin() && ! empty( $available_modules_option[ JETPACK__VERSION ] ) ) { 
  2007.                 $modules = $available_modules_option[ JETPACK__VERSION ]; 
  2008.             } else { 
  2009.                 $files = Jetpack::glob_php( JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'modules' ); 
  2010.  
  2011.                 $modules = array(); 
  2012.  
  2013.                 foreach ( $files as $file ) { 
  2014.                     if ( ! $headers = Jetpack::get_module( $file ) ) { 
  2015.                         continue; 
  2016.                     } 
  2017.  
  2018.                     $modules[ Jetpack::get_module_slug( $file ) ] = $headers['introduced']; 
  2019.                 } 
  2020.  
  2021.                 Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'available_modules', array( 
  2022.                     JETPACK__VERSION => $modules,  
  2023.  ) ); 
  2024.             } 
  2025.         } 
  2026.  
  2027.         /** 
  2028.          * Filters the array of modules available to be activated. 
  2029.          * 
  2030.          * @since 2.4.0 
  2031.          * 
  2032.          * @param array $modules Array of available modules. 
  2033.          * @param string $min_version Minimum version number required to use modules. 
  2034.          * @param string $max_version Maximum version number required to use modules. 
  2035.          */ 
  2036.         $mods = apply_filters( 'jetpack_get_available_modules', $modules, $min_version, $max_version ); 
  2037.  
  2038.         if ( ! $min_version && ! $max_version ) { 
  2039.             return array_keys( $mods ); 
  2040.         } 
  2041.  
  2042.         $r = array(); 
  2043.         foreach ( $mods as $slug => $introduced ) { 
  2044.             if ( $min_version && version_compare( $min_version, $introduced, '>=' ) ) { 
  2045.                 continue; 
  2046.             } 
  2047.  
  2048.             if ( $max_version && version_compare( $max_version, $introduced, '<' ) ) { 
  2049.                 continue; 
  2050.             } 
  2051.  
  2052.             $r[] = $slug; 
  2053.         } 
  2054.  
  2055.         return $r; 
  2056.     } 
  2057.  
  2058.     /** 
  2059.      * Default modules loaded on activation. 
  2060.      */ 
  2061.     public static function get_default_modules( $min_version = false, $max_version = false ) { 
  2062.         $return = array(); 
  2063.  
  2064.         foreach ( Jetpack::get_available_modules( $min_version, $max_version ) as $module ) { 
  2065.             $module_data = Jetpack::get_module( $module ); 
  2066.  
  2067.             switch ( strtolower( $module_data['auto_activate'] ) ) { 
  2068.                 case 'yes' : 
  2069.                     $return[] = $module; 
  2070.                     break; 
  2071.                 case 'public' : 
  2072.                     if ( Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'public' ) ) { 
  2073.                         $return[] = $module; 
  2074.                     } 
  2075.                     break; 
  2076.                 case 'no' : 
  2077.                 default : 
  2078.                     break; 
  2079.             } 
  2080.         } 
  2081.         /** 
  2082.          * Filters the array of default modules. 
  2083.          * 
  2084.          * @since 2.5.0 
  2085.          * 
  2086.          * @param array $return Array of default modules. 
  2087.          * @param string $min_version Minimum version number required to use modules. 
  2088.          * @param string $max_version Maximum version number required to use modules. 
  2089.          */ 
  2090.         return apply_filters( 'jetpack_get_default_modules', $return, $min_version, $max_version ); 
  2091.     } 
  2092.  
  2093.     /** 
  2094.      * Checks activated modules during auto-activation to determine 
  2095.      * if any of those modules are being deprecated.  If so, close 
  2096.      * them out, and add any replacement modules. 
  2097.      * 
  2098.      * Runs at priority 99 by default. 
  2099.      * 
  2100.      * This is run late, so that it can still activate a module if 
  2101.      * the new module is a replacement for another that the user 
  2102.      * currently has active, even if something at the normal priority 
  2103.      * would kibosh everything. 
  2104.      * 
  2105.      * @since 2.6 
  2106.      * @uses jetpack_get_default_modules filter 
  2107.      * @param array $modules 
  2108.      * @return array 
  2109.      */ 
  2110.     function handle_deprecated_modules( $modules ) { 
  2111.         $deprecated_modules = array( 
  2112.             'debug' => null, // Closed out and moved to ./class.jetpack-debugger.php 
  2113.             'wpcc' => 'sso', // Closed out in 2.6 -- SSO provides the same functionality. 
  2114.             'gplus-authorship' => null, // Closed out in 3.2 -- Google dropped support. 
  2115.  ); 
  2116.  
  2117.         // Don't activate SSO if they never completed activating WPCC. 
  2118.         if ( Jetpack::is_module_active( 'wpcc' ) ) { 
  2119.             $wpcc_options = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'wpcc_options' ); 
  2120.             if ( empty( $wpcc_options ) || empty( $wpcc_options['client_id'] ) || empty( $wpcc_options['client_id'] ) ) { 
  2121.                 $deprecated_modules['wpcc'] = null; 
  2122.             } 
  2123.         } 
  2124.  
  2125.         foreach ( $deprecated_modules as $module => $replacement ) { 
  2126.             if ( Jetpack::is_module_active( $module ) ) { 
  2127.                 self::deactivate_module( $module ); 
  2128.                 if ( $replacement ) { 
  2129.                     $modules[] = $replacement; 
  2130.                 } 
  2131.             } 
  2132.         } 
  2133.  
  2134.         return array_unique( $modules ); 
  2135.     } 
  2136.  
  2137.     /** 
  2138.      * Checks activated plugins during auto-activation to determine 
  2139.      * if any of those plugins are in the list with a corresponding module 
  2140.      * that is not compatible with the plugin. The module will not be allowed 
  2141.      * to auto-activate. 
  2142.      * 
  2143.      * @since 2.6 
  2144.      * @uses jetpack_get_default_modules filter 
  2145.      * @param array $modules 
  2146.      * @return array 
  2147.      */ 
  2148.     function filter_default_modules( $modules ) { 
  2149.  
  2150.         $active_plugins = self::get_active_plugins(); 
  2151.  
  2152.         if ( ! empty( $active_plugins ) ) { 
  2153.  
  2154.             // For each module we'd like to auto-activate... 
  2155.             foreach ( $modules as $key => $module ) { 
  2156.                 // If there are potential conflicts for it... 
  2157.                 if ( ! empty( $this->conflicting_plugins[ $module ] ) ) { 
  2158.                     // For each potential conflict... 
  2159.                     foreach ( $this->conflicting_plugins[ $module ] as $title => $plugin ) { 
  2160.                         // If that conflicting plugin is active... 
  2161.                         if ( in_array( $plugin, $active_plugins ) ) { 
  2162.                             // Remove that item from being auto-activated. 
  2163.                             unset( $modules[ $key ] ); 
  2164.                         } 
  2165.                     } 
  2166.                 } 
  2167.             } 
  2168.         } 
  2169.  
  2170.         return $modules; 
  2171.     } 
  2172.  
  2173.     /** 
  2174.      * Extract a module's slug from its full path. 
  2175.      */ 
  2176.     public static function get_module_slug( $file ) { 
  2177.         return str_replace( '.php', '', basename( $file ) ); 
  2178.     } 
  2179.  
  2180.     /** 
  2181.      * Generate a module's path from its slug. 
  2182.      */ 
  2183.     public static function get_module_path( $slug ) { 
  2184.         return JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . "modules/$slug.php"; 
  2185.     } 
  2186.  
  2187.     /** 
  2188.      * Load module data from module file. Headers differ from WordPress 
  2189.      * plugin headers to avoid them being identified as standalone 
  2190.      * plugins on the WordPress plugins page. 
  2191.      */ 
  2192.     public static function get_module( $module ) { 
  2193.         $headers = array( 
  2194.             'name' => 'Module Name',  
  2195.             'description' => 'Module Description',  
  2196.             'jumpstart_desc' => 'Jumpstart Description',  
  2197.             'sort' => 'Sort Order',  
  2198.             'recommendation_order' => 'Recommendation Order',  
  2199.             'introduced' => 'First Introduced',  
  2200.             'changed' => 'Major Changes In',  
  2201.             'deactivate' => 'Deactivate',  
  2202.             'free' => 'Free',  
  2203.             'requires_connection' => 'Requires Connection',  
  2204.             'auto_activate' => 'Auto Activate',  
  2205.             'module_tags' => 'Module Tags',  
  2206.             'feature' => 'Feature',  
  2207.             'additional_search_queries' => 'Additional Search Queries',  
  2208.  ); 
  2209.  
  2210.         $file = Jetpack::get_module_path( Jetpack::get_module_slug( $module ) ); 
  2211.  
  2212.         $mod = Jetpack::get_file_data( $file, $headers ); 
  2213.         if ( empty( $mod['name'] ) ) { 
  2214.             return false; 
  2215.         } 
  2216.  
  2217.         $mod['sort'] = empty( $mod['sort'] ) ? 10 : (int) $mod['sort']; 
  2218.         $mod['recommendation_order'] = empty( $mod['recommendation_order'] ) ? 20 : (int) $mod['recommendation_order']; 
  2219.         $mod['deactivate'] = empty( $mod['deactivate'] ); 
  2220.         $mod['free'] = empty( $mod['free'] ); 
  2221.         $mod['requires_connection'] = ( ! empty( $mod['requires_connection'] ) && 'No' == $mod['requires_connection'] ) ? false : true; 
  2222.  
  2223.         if ( empty( $mod['auto_activate'] ) || ! in_array( strtolower( $mod['auto_activate'] ), array( 'yes', 'no', 'public' ) ) ) { 
  2224.             $mod['auto_activate'] = 'No'; 
  2225.         } else { 
  2226.             $mod['auto_activate'] = (string) $mod['auto_activate']; 
  2227.         } 
  2228.  
  2229.         if ( $mod['module_tags'] ) { 
  2230.             $mod['module_tags'] = explode( ', ', $mod['module_tags'] ); 
  2231.             $mod['module_tags'] = array_map( 'trim', $mod['module_tags'] ); 
  2232.             $mod['module_tags'] = array_map( array( __CLASS__, 'translate_module_tag' ), $mod['module_tags'] ); 
  2233.         } else { 
  2234.             $mod['module_tags'] = array( self::translate_module_tag( 'Other' ) ); 
  2235.         } 
  2236.  
  2237.         if ( $mod['feature'] ) { 
  2238.             $mod['feature'] = explode( ', ', $mod['feature'] ); 
  2239.             $mod['feature'] = array_map( 'trim', $mod['feature'] ); 
  2240.         } else { 
  2241.             $mod['feature'] = array( self::translate_module_tag( 'Other' ) ); 
  2242.         } 
  2243.  
  2244.         /** 
  2245.          * Filters the feature array on a module. 
  2246.          * 
  2247.          * This filter allows you to control where each module is filtered: Recommended,  
  2248.          * Jumpstart, and the default "Other" listing. 
  2249.          * 
  2250.          * @since 3.5.0 
  2251.          * 
  2252.          * @param array   $mod['feature'] The areas to feature this module: 
  2253.          *     'Jumpstart' adds to the "Jumpstart" option to activate many modules at once. 
  2254.          *     'Recommended' shows on the main Jetpack admin screen. 
  2255.          *     'Other' should be the default if no other value is in the array. 
  2256.          * @param string  $module The slug of the module, e.g. sharedaddy. 
  2257.          * @param array   $mod All the currently assembled module data. 
  2258.          */ 
  2259.         $mod['feature'] = apply_filters( 'jetpack_module_feature', $mod['feature'], $module, $mod ); 
  2260.  
  2261.         /** 
  2262.          * Filter the returned data about a module. 
  2263.          * 
  2264.          * This filter allows overriding any info about Jetpack modules. It is dangerous,  
  2265.          * so please be careful. 
  2266.          * 
  2267.          * @since 3.6.0 
  2268.          * 
  2269.          * @param array   $mod    The details of the requested module. 
  2270.          * @param string  $module The slug of the module, e.g. sharedaddy 
  2271.          * @param string  $file   The path to the module source file. 
  2272.          */ 
  2273.         return apply_filters( 'jetpack_get_module', $mod, $module, $file ); 
  2274.     } 
  2275.  
  2276.     /** 
  2277.      * Like core's get_file_data implementation, but caches the result. 
  2278.      */ 
  2279.     public static function get_file_data( $file, $headers ) { 
  2280.         //Get just the filename from $file (i.e. exclude full path) so that a consistent hash is generated 
  2281.         $file_name = basename( $file ); 
  2282.         $file_data_option = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'file_data', array() ); 
  2283.         $key = md5( $file_name . serialize( $headers ) ); 
  2284.         $refresh_cache = is_admin() && isset( $_GET['page'] ) && 'jetpack' === substr( $_GET['page'], 0, 7 ); 
  2285.  
  2286.         // If we don't need to refresh the cache, and already have the value, short-circuit! 
  2287.         if ( ! $refresh_cache && isset( $file_data_option[ JETPACK__VERSION ][ $key ] ) ) { 
  2288.             return $file_data_option[ JETPACK__VERSION ][ $key ]; 
  2289.         } 
  2290.  
  2291.         $data = get_file_data( $file, $headers ); 
  2292.  
  2293.         // Strip out any old Jetpack versions that are cluttering the option. 
  2294.         // 
  2295.         // We maintain the data for the current version of Jetpack plus the previous version 
  2296.         // to prevent repeated DB hits on large sites hosted with multiple web servers 
  2297.         // on a single database (since all web servers might not be updated simultaneously) 
  2298.  
  2299.         $file_data_option[ JETPACK__VERSION ][ $key ] = $data; 
  2300.  
  2301.         if ( count( $file_data_option ) > 2 ) { 
  2302.             $count = 0; 
  2303.             krsort( $file_data_option ); 
  2304.             foreach ( $file_data_option as $version => $values ) { 
  2305.                 $count++; 
  2306.                 if ( $count > 2 && JETPACK__VERSION != $version ) { 
  2307.                     unset( $file_data_option[ $version ] ); 
  2308.                 } 
  2309.             } 
  2310.         } 
  2311.  
  2312.         Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'file_data', $file_data_option ); 
  2313.  
  2314.         return $data; 
  2315.     } 
  2316.  
  2317.  
  2318.     /** 
  2319.      * Return translated module tag. 
  2320.      * 
  2321.      * @param string $tag Tag as it appears in each module heading. 
  2322.      * 
  2323.      * @return mixed 
  2324.      */ 
  2325.     public static function translate_module_tag( $tag ) { 
  2326.         return jetpack_get_module_i18n_tag( $tag ); 
  2327.     } 
  2328.  
  2329.     /** 
  2330.      * Return module name translation. Uses matching string created in modules/module-headings.php. 
  2331.      * 
  2332.      * @since 3.9.2 
  2333.      * 
  2334.      * @param array $modules 
  2335.      * 
  2336.      * @return string|void 
  2337.      */ 
  2338.     public static function get_translated_modules( $modules ) { 
  2339.         foreach ( $modules as $index => $module ) { 
  2340.             $i18n_module = jetpack_get_module_i18n( $module['module'] ); 
  2341.             if ( isset( $module['name'] ) ) { 
  2342.                 $modules[ $index ]['name'] = $i18n_module['name']; 
  2343.             } 
  2344.             if ( isset( $module['description'] ) ) { 
  2345.                 $modules[ $index ]['description'] = $i18n_module['description']; 
  2346.                 $modules[ $index ]['short_description'] = $i18n_module['description']; 
  2347.             } 
  2348.         } 
  2349.         return $modules; 
  2350.     } 
  2351.  
  2352.     /** 
  2353.      * Get a list of activated modules as an array of module slugs. 
  2354.      */ 
  2355.     public static function get_active_modules() { 
  2356.         $active = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'active_modules' ); 
  2357.  
  2358.         if ( ! is_array( $active ) ) { 
  2359.             $active = array(); 
  2360.         } 
  2361.  
  2362.         if ( class_exists( 'VaultPress' ) || function_exists( 'vaultpress_contact_service' ) ) { 
  2363.             $active[] = 'vaultpress'; 
  2364.         } else { 
  2365.             $active = array_diff( $active, array( 'vaultpress' ) ); 
  2366.         } 
  2367.  
  2368.         //If protect is active on the main site of a multisite, it should be active on all sites. 
  2369.         if ( ! in_array( 'protect', $active ) && is_multisite() && get_site_option( 'jetpack_protect_active' ) ) { 
  2370.             $active[] = 'protect'; 
  2371.         } 
  2372.  
  2373.         return array_unique( $active ); 
  2374.     }

  2376.     /**

  2384.     public static function is_module_active( $module ) {

  2387.  
  2388.     public static function is_module( $module ) { 
  2389.         return ! empty( $module ) && ! validate_file( $module, Jetpack::get_available_modules() ); 
  2390.     } 
  2391.  
  2392.     /** 
  2393.      * Catches PHP errors.  Must be used in conjunction with output buffering. 
  2394.      * 
  2395.      * @param bool $catch True to start catching, False to stop. 
  2396.      * 
  2397.      * @static 
  2398.      */ 
  2399.     public static function catch_errors( $catch ) { 
  2400.         static $display_errors, $error_reporting; 
  2401.  
  2402.         if ( $catch ) { 
  2403.             $display_errors = @ini_set( 'display_errors', 1 ); 
  2404.             $error_reporting = @error_reporting( E_ALL ); 
  2405.             add_action( 'shutdown', array( 'Jetpack', 'catch_errors_on_shutdown' ), 0 ); 
  2406.         } else { 
  2407.             @ini_set( 'display_errors', $display_errors ); 
  2408.             @error_reporting( $error_reporting ); 
  2409.             remove_action( 'shutdown', array( 'Jetpack', 'catch_errors_on_shutdown' ), 0 ); 
  2410.         } 
  2411.     } 
  2412.  
  2413.     /** 
  2414.      * Saves any generated PHP errors in ::state( 'php_errors', {errors} ) 
  2415.      */ 
  2416.     public static function catch_errors_on_shutdown() { 
  2417.         Jetpack::state( 'php_errors', self::alias_directories( ob_get_clean() ) ); 
  2418.     } 
  2419.  
  2420.     /** 
  2421.      * Rewrite any string to make paths easier to read. 
  2422.      * 
  2423.      * Rewrites ABSPATH (eg `/home/jetpack/wordpress/`) to ABSPATH, and if WP_CONTENT_DIR 
  2424.      * is located outside of ABSPATH, rewrites that to WP_CONTENT_DIR. 
  2425.      * 
  2426.      * @param $string 
  2427.      * @return mixed 
  2428.      */ 
  2429.     public static function alias_directories( $string ) { 
  2430.         // ABSPATH has a trailing slash. 
  2431.         $string = str_replace( ABSPATH, 'ABSPATH/', $string ); 
  2432.         // WP_CONTENT_DIR does not have a trailing slash. 
  2433.         $string = str_replace( WP_CONTENT_DIR, 'WP_CONTENT_DIR', $string ); 
  2434.  
  2435.         return $string; 
  2436.     } 
  2437.  
  2438.     public static function activate_default_modules( $min_version = false, $max_version = false, $other_modules = array(), $redirect = true ) { 
  2439.         $jetpack = Jetpack::init(); 
  2440.  
  2441.         $modules = Jetpack::get_default_modules( $min_version, $max_version ); 
  2442.         $modules = array_merge( $other_modules, $modules ); 
  2443.  
  2444.         // Look for standalone plugins and disable if active. 
  2445.  
  2446.         $to_deactivate = array(); 
  2447.         foreach ( $modules as $module ) { 
  2448.             if ( isset( $jetpack->plugins_to_deactivate[$module] ) ) { 
  2449.                 $to_deactivate[$module] = $jetpack->plugins_to_deactivate[$module]; 
  2450.             } 
  2451.         } 
  2452.  
  2453.         $deactivated = array(); 
  2454.         foreach ( $to_deactivate as $module => $deactivate_me ) { 
  2455.             list( $probable_file, $probable_title ) = $deactivate_me; 
  2456.             if ( Jetpack_Client_Server::deactivate_plugin( $probable_file, $probable_title ) ) { 
  2457.                 $deactivated[] = $module; 
  2458.             } 
  2459.         } 
  2460.  
  2461.         if ( $deactivated && $redirect ) { 
  2462.             Jetpack::state( 'deactivated_plugins', join( ', ', $deactivated ) ); 
  2463.  
  2464.             $url = add_query_arg( 
  2465.                 array( 
  2466.                     'action' => 'activate_default_modules',  
  2467.                     '_wpnonce' => wp_create_nonce( 'activate_default_modules' ),  
  2468.  ),  
  2469.                 add_query_arg( compact( 'min_version', 'max_version', 'other_modules' ), Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=jetpack' ) ) 
  2470.  ); 
  2471.             wp_safe_redirect( $url ); 
  2472.             exit; 
  2473.         } 
  2474.  
  2475.         /** 
  2476.          * Fires before default modules are activated. 
  2477.          * 
  2478.          * @since 1.9.0 
  2479.          * 
  2480.          * @param string $min_version Minimum version number required to use modules. 
  2481.          * @param string $max_version Maximum version number required to use modules. 
  2482.          * @param array $other_modules Array of other modules to activate alongside the default modules. 
  2483.          */ 
  2484.         do_action( 'jetpack_before_activate_default_modules', $min_version, $max_version, $other_modules ); 
  2485.  
  2486.         // Check each module for fatal errors, a la wp-admin/plugins.php::activate before activating 
  2487.         Jetpack::restate(); 
  2488.         Jetpack::catch_errors( true ); 
  2489.  
  2490.         $active = Jetpack::get_active_modules(); 
  2491.  
  2492.         foreach ( $modules as $module ) { 
  2493.             if ( did_action( "jetpack_module_loaded_$module" ) ) { 
  2494.                 $active[] = $module; 
  2495.                 self::update_active_modules( $active ); 
  2496.                 continue; 
  2497.             } 
  2498.  
  2499.             if ( in_array( $module, $active ) ) { 
  2500.                 $module_info = Jetpack::get_module( $module ); 
  2501.                 if ( ! $module_info['deactivate'] ) { 
  2502.                     $state = in_array( $module, $other_modules ) ? 'reactivated_modules' : 'activated_modules'; 
  2503.                     if ( $active_state = Jetpack::state( $state ) ) { 
  2504.                         $active_state = explode( ', ', $active_state ); 
  2505.                     } else { 
  2506.                         $active_state = array(); 
  2507.                     } 
  2508.                     $active_state[] = $module; 
  2509.                     Jetpack::state( $state, implode( ', ', $active_state ) ); 
  2510.                 } 
  2511.                 continue; 
  2512.             } 
  2513.  
  2514.             $file = Jetpack::get_module_path( $module ); 
  2515.             if ( ! file_exists( $file ) ) { 
  2516.                 continue; 
  2517.             } 
  2518.  
  2519.             // we'll override this later if the plugin can be included without fatal error 
  2520.             if ( $redirect ) { 
  2521.                 wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=jetpack' ) ); 
  2522.             } 
  2523.             Jetpack::state( 'error', 'module_activation_failed' ); 
  2524.             Jetpack::state( 'module', $module ); 
  2525.             ob_start(); 
  2526.             require $file; 
  2527.  
  2528.             $active[] = $module; 
  2529.             $state = in_array( $module, $other_modules ) ? 'reactivated_modules' : 'activated_modules'; 
  2530.             if ( $active_state = Jetpack::state( $state ) ) { 
  2531.                 $active_state = explode( ', ', $active_state ); 
  2532.             } else { 
  2533.                 $active_state = array(); 
  2534.             } 
  2535.             $active_state[] = $module; 
  2536.             Jetpack::state( $state, implode( ', ', $active_state ) ); 
  2537.             Jetpack::update_active_modules( $active ); 
  2538.  
  2539.             ob_end_clean(); 
  2540.         } 
  2541.         Jetpack::state( 'error', false ); 
  2542.         Jetpack::state( 'module', false ); 
  2543.         Jetpack::catch_errors( false ); 
  2544.         /** 
  2545.          * Fires when default modules are activated. 
  2546.          * 
  2547.          * @since 1.9.0 
  2548.          * 
  2549.          * @param string $min_version Minimum version number required to use modules. 
  2550.          * @param string $max_version Maximum version number required to use modules. 
  2551.          * @param array $other_modules Array of other modules to activate alongside the default modules. 
  2552.          */ 
  2553.         do_action( 'jetpack_activate_default_modules', $min_version, $max_version, $other_modules ); 
  2554.     } 
  2555.  
  2556.     public static function activate_module( $module, $exit = true, $redirect = true ) { 
  2557.         /** 
  2558.          * Fires before a module is activated. 
  2559.          * 
  2560.          * @since 2.6.0 
  2561.          * 
  2562.          * @param string $module Module slug. 
  2563.          * @param bool $exit Should we exit after the module has been activated. Default to true. 
  2564.          * @param bool $redirect Should the user be redirected after module activation? Default to true. 
  2565.          */ 
  2566.         do_action( 'jetpack_pre_activate_module', $module, $exit, $redirect ); 
  2567.  
  2568.         $jetpack = Jetpack::init(); 
  2569.  
  2570.         if ( ! strlen( $module ) ) 
  2571.             return false; 
  2572.  
  2573.         if ( ! Jetpack::is_module( $module ) ) 
  2574.             return false; 
  2575.  
  2576.         // If it's already active, then don't do it again 
  2577.         $active = Jetpack::get_active_modules(); 
  2578.         foreach ( $active as $act ) { 
  2579.             if ( $act == $module ) 
  2580.                 return true; 
  2581.         } 
  2582.  
  2583.         $module_data = Jetpack::get_module( $module ); 
  2584.  
  2585.         if ( ! Jetpack::is_active() ) { 
  2586.             if ( !Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) 
  2587.                 return false; 
  2588.  
  2589.             // If we're not connected but in development mode, make sure the module doesn't require a connection 
  2590.             if ( Jetpack::is_development_mode() && $module_data['requires_connection'] ) 
  2591.                 return false; 
  2592.         } 
  2593.  
  2594.         // Check and see if the old plugin is active 
  2595.         if ( isset( $jetpack->plugins_to_deactivate[ $module ] ) ) { 
  2596.             // Deactivate the old plugin 
  2597.             if ( Jetpack_Client_Server::deactivate_plugin( $jetpack->plugins_to_deactivate[ $module ][0], $jetpack->plugins_to_deactivate[ $module ][1] ) ) { 
  2598.                 // If we deactivated the old plugin, remembere that with ::state() and redirect back to this page to activate the module 
  2599.                 // We can't activate the module on this page load since the newly deactivated old plugin is still loaded on this page load. 
  2600.                 Jetpack::state( 'deactivated_plugins', $module ); 
  2601.                 wp_safe_redirect( add_query_arg( 'jetpack_restate', 1 ) ); 
  2602.                 exit; 
  2603.             } 
  2604.         } 
  2605.  
  2606.         // Protect won't work with mis-configured IPs 
  2607.         if ( 'protect' === $module ) { 
  2608.             include_once JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'modules/protect/shared-functions.php'; 
  2609.             if ( ! jetpack_protect_get_ip() ) { 
  2610.                 Jetpack::state( 'message', 'protect_misconfigured_ip' ); 
  2611.                 return false; 
  2612.             } 
  2613.         } 
  2614.  
  2615.         // Check the file for fatal errors, a la wp-admin/plugins.php::activate 
  2616.         Jetpack::state( 'module', $module ); 
  2617.         Jetpack::state( 'error', 'module_activation_failed' ); // we'll override this later if the plugin can be included without fatal error 
  2618.  
  2619.         Jetpack::catch_errors( true ); 
  2620.         ob_start(); 
  2621.         require Jetpack::get_module_path( $module ); 
  2622.         /** This action is documented in class.jetpack.php */ 
  2623.         do_action( 'jetpack_activate_module', $module ); 
  2624.         $active[] = $module; 
  2625.         Jetpack::update_active_modules( $active ); 
  2626.  
  2627.         Jetpack::state( 'error', false ); // the override 
  2628.         ob_end_clean(); 
  2629.         Jetpack::catch_errors( false ); 
  2630.  
  2631.         // A flag for Jump Start so it's not shown again. Only set if it hasn't been yet. 
  2632.         if ( 'new_connection' === Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'jumpstart' ) ) { 
  2633.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'jumpstart', 'jetpack_action_taken' ); 
  2634.  
  2635.             //Jump start is being dismissed send data to MC Stats 
  2636.             $jetpack->stat( 'jumpstart', 'manual, '.$module ); 
  2637.  
  2638.             $jetpack->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  2639.         } 
  2640.  
  2641.         if ( $redirect ) { 
  2642.             wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=jetpack' ) ); 
  2643.         } 
  2644.         if ( $exit ) { 
  2645.             exit; 
  2646.         } 
  2647.         return true; 
  2648.     } 
  2649.  
  2650.     function activate_module_actions( $module ) { 
  2651.         _deprecated_function( __METHOD__, 'jeptack-4.2' ); 
  2652.     }

  2654.     public static function deactivate_module( $module ) { 
  2655.         /** 
  2656.          * Fires when a module is deactivated. 
  2657.          * 
  2658.          * @since 1.9.0 
  2659.          * 
  2660.          * @param string $module Module slug. 
  2661.          */ 
  2662.         do_action( 'jetpack_pre_deactivate_module', $module ); 
  2663.  
  2664.         $jetpack = Jetpack::init(); 
  2665.  
  2666.         $active = Jetpack::get_active_modules(); 
  2667.         $new = array_filter( array_diff( $active, (array) $module ) ); 
  2668.  
  2669.         // A flag for Jump Start so it's not shown again. 
  2670.         if ( 'new_connection' === Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'jumpstart' ) ) { 
  2671.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'jumpstart', 'jetpack_action_taken' ); 
  2672.  
  2673.             //Jump start is being dismissed send data to MC Stats 
  2674.             $jetpack->stat( 'jumpstart', 'manual, deactivated-'.$module ); 
  2675.  
  2676.             $jetpack->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  2677.         } 
  2678.  
  2679.         return self::update_active_modules( $new ); 
  2680.     }

  2714.     public static function bail_on_activation( $message, $deactivate = true ) { 
  2715. ?> 
  2716. <!doctype html> 
  2717. <html> 
  2718. <head> 
  2719. <meta charset="<?php bloginfo( 'charset' ); ?>"> 
  2720. <style> 
  2721. * { 
  2722.     text-align: center; 
  2723.     margin: 0; 
  2724.     padding: 0; 
  2725.     font-family: "Lucida Grande", Verdana, Arial, "Bitstream Vera Sans", sans-serif; 
  2726. } 
  2727. p { 
  2728.     margin-top: 1em; 
  2729.     font-size: 18px; 
  2730. } 
  2731. </style> 
  2732. <body> 
  2733. <p><?php echo esc_html( $message ); ?></p> 
  2734. </body> 
  2735. </html> 
  2736. <?php 
  2737.         if ( $deactivate ) { 
  2738.             $plugins = get_option( 'active_plugins' ); 
  2739.             $jetpack = plugin_basename( JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'jetpack.php' ); 
  2740.             $update = false; 
  2741.             foreach ( $plugins as $i => $plugin ) { 
  2742.                 if ( $plugin === $jetpack ) { 
  2743.                     $plugins[$i] = false; 
  2744.                     $update = true; 
  2745.                 } 
  2746.             } 
  2747.  
  2748.             if ( $update ) { 
  2749.                 update_option( 'active_plugins', array_filter( $plugins ) ); 
  2750.             } 
  2751.         } 
  2752.         exit; 
  2753.     } 
  2754.  
  2755.     /** 
  2756.      * Attached to activate_{ plugin_basename( __FILES__ ) } by register_activation_hook() 
  2757.      * @static 
  2758.      */ 
  2759.     public static function plugin_activation( $network_wide ) { 
  2760.         Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'activated', 1 ); 
  2761.  
  2762.         if ( version_compare( $GLOBALS['wp_version'], JETPACK__MINIMUM_WP_VERSION, '<' ) ) { 
  2763.             Jetpack::bail_on_activation( sprintf( __( 'Jetpack requires WordPress version %s or later.', 'jetpack' ), JETPACK__MINIMUM_WP_VERSION ) ); 
  2764.         } 
  2765.  
  2766.         if ( $network_wide ) 
  2767.             Jetpack::state( 'network_nag', true ); 
  2768.  
  2769.         // For firing one-off events (notices) immediately after activation 
  2770.         set_transient( 'activated_jetpack', true, .1 * MINUTE_IN_SECONDS ); 
  2771.  
  2772.         Jetpack::plugin_initialize(); 
  2773.     } 
  2774.     /** 
  2775.      * Runs before bumping version numbers up to a new version 
  2776.      * @param  (string) $version    Version:timestamp 
  2777.      * @param  (string) $old_version Old Version:timestamp or false if not set yet. 
  2778.      * @return null              [description] 
  2779.      */ 
  2780.     public static function do_version_bump( $version, $old_version ) { 
  2781.  
  2782.         if ( ! $old_version ) { // For new sites 
  2783.             // Setting up jetpack manage 
  2784.             Jetpack::activate_manage(); 
  2785.         } 
  2786.     }

  2788.     /** 
  2789.      * Sets the internal version number and activation state. 
  2790.      * @static 
  2791.      */ 
  2792.     public static function plugin_initialize() { 
  2793.         if ( ! Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'activated' ) ) { 
  2794.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'activated', 2 ); 
  2795.         } 
  2796.  
  2797.         if ( ! Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'version' ) ) { 
  2798.             $version = $old_version = JETPACK__VERSION . ':' . time(); 
  2799.             /** This action is documented in class.jetpack.php */ 
  2800.             do_action( 'updating_jetpack_version', $version, false ); 
  2801.             Jetpack_Options::update_options( compact( 'version', 'old_version' ) ); 
  2802.         } 
  2803.  
  2804.         Jetpack::load_modules(); 
  2805.  
  2806.         Jetpack_Options::delete_option( 'do_activate' ); 
  2807.     }

  2809.     /** 
  2810.      * Removes all connection options 
  2811.      * @static 
  2812.      */ 
  2813.     public static function plugin_deactivation( ) { 
  2814.         require_once( ABSPATH . '/wp-admin/includes/plugin.php' ); 
  2815.         if( is_plugin_active_for_network( 'jetpack/jetpack.php' ) ) { 
  2816.             Jetpack_Network::init()->deactivate(); 
  2817.         } else { 
  2818.             Jetpack::disconnect( false ); 
  2819.             //Jetpack_Heartbeat::init()->deactivate(); 
  2820.         } 
  2821.     } 
  2822.  
  2823.     /** 
  2824.      * Disconnects from the Jetpack servers. 
  2825.      * Forgets all connection details and tells the Jetpack servers to do the same. 
  2826.      * @static 
  2827.      */ 
  2828.     public static function disconnect( $update_activated_state = true ) { 
  2829.         wp_clear_scheduled_hook( 'jetpack_clean_nonces' ); 
  2830.         Jetpack::clean_nonces( true ); 
  2831.  
  2832.         // If the site is in an IDC because sync is not allowed,  
  2833.         // let's make sure to not disconnect the production site. 
  2834.         if ( ! self::validate_sync_error_idc_option() ) { 
  2835.             JetpackTracking::record_user_event( 'disconnect_site', array() ); 
  2836.             Jetpack::load_xml_rpc_client(); 
  2837.             $xml = new Jetpack_IXR_Client(); 
  2838.             $xml->query( 'jetpack.deregister' ); 
  2839.         } 
  2840.  
  2841.         Jetpack_Options::delete_option( 
  2842.             array( 
  2843.                 'register',  
  2844.                 'blog_token',  
  2845.                 'user_token',  
  2846.                 'user_tokens',  
  2847.                 'master_user',  
  2848.                 'time_diff',  
  2849.                 'fallback_no_verify_ssl_certs',  
  2850.  ) 
  2851.  ); 
  2852.  
  2853.         Jetpack_IDC::clear_all_idc_options(); 
  2854.  
  2855.         if ( $update_activated_state ) { 
  2856.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'activated', 4 ); 
  2857.         } 
  2858.  
  2859.         if ( $jetpack_unique_connection = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'unique_connection' ) ) { 
  2860.             // Check then record unique disconnection if site has never been disconnected previously 
  2861.             if ( - 1 == $jetpack_unique_connection['disconnected'] ) { 
  2862.                 $jetpack_unique_connection['disconnected'] = 1; 
  2863.             } else { 
  2864.                 if ( 0 == $jetpack_unique_connection['disconnected'] ) { 
  2865.                     //track unique disconnect 
  2866.                     $jetpack = Jetpack::init(); 
  2867.  
  2868.                     $jetpack->stat( 'connections', 'unique-disconnect' ); 
  2869.                     $jetpack->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  2870.                 } 
  2871.                 // increment number of times disconnected 
  2872.                 $jetpack_unique_connection['disconnected'] += 1; 
  2873.             } 
  2874.  
  2875.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'unique_connection', $jetpack_unique_connection ); 
  2876.         } 
  2877.  
  2878.         // Delete cached connected user data 
  2879.         $transient_key = "jetpack_connected_user_data_" . get_current_user_id(); 
  2880.         delete_transient( $transient_key ); 
  2881.  
  2882.         // Delete all the sync related data. Since it could be taking up space. 
  2883.         require_once JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'sync/class.jetpack-sync-sender.php'; 
  2884.         Jetpack_Sync_Sender::get_instance()->uninstall(); 
  2885.  
  2886.         // Disable the Heartbeat cron 
  2887.         Jetpack_Heartbeat::init()->deactivate(); 
  2888.     }

  2890.     /** 
  2891.      * Unlinks the current user from the linked WordPress.com user 
  2892.      */ 
  2893.     public static function unlink_user( $user_id = null ) { 
  2894.         if ( ! $tokens = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'user_tokens' ) ) 
  2895.             return false; 
  2896.  
  2897.         $user_id = empty( $user_id ) ? get_current_user_id() : intval( $user_id ); 
  2898.  
  2899.         if ( Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'master_user' ) == $user_id ) 
  2900.             return false; 
  2901.  
  2902.         if ( ! isset( $tokens[ $user_id ] ) ) 
  2903.             return false; 
  2904.  
  2905.         Jetpack::load_xml_rpc_client(); 
  2906.         $xml = new Jetpack_IXR_Client( compact( 'user_id' ) ); 
  2907.         $xml->query( 'jetpack.unlink_user', $user_id ); 
  2908.  
  2909.         unset( $tokens[ $user_id ] ); 
  2910.  
  2911.         Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'user_tokens', $tokens ); 
  2912.  
  2913.         /** 
  2914.          * Fires after the current user has been unlinked from WordPress.com. 
  2915.          * 
  2916.          * @since 4.1.0 
  2917.          * 
  2918.          * @param int $user_id The current user's ID. 
  2919.          */ 
  2920.         do_action( 'jetpack_unlinked_user', $user_id ); 
  2921.  
  2922.         return true; 
  2923.     } 
  2924.  
  2925.     /** 
  2926.      * Attempts Jetpack registration.  If it fail, a state flag is set: @see ::admin_page_load() 
  2927.      */ 
  2928.     public static function try_registration() { 
  2929.         // Let's get some testing in beta versions and such. 
  2930.         if ( self::is_development_version() && defined( 'PHP_URL_HOST' ) ) { 
  2931.             // Before attempting to connect, let's make sure that the domains are viable. 
  2932.             $domains_to_check = array_unique( array( 
  2933.                 'siteurl' => parse_url( get_site_url(), PHP_URL_HOST ),  
  2934.                 'homeurl' => parse_url( get_home_url(), PHP_URL_HOST ),  
  2935.  ) ); 
  2936.             foreach ( $domains_to_check as $domain ) { 
  2937.                 $result = Jetpack_Data::is_usable_domain( $domain ); 
  2938.                 if ( is_wp_error( $result ) ) { 
  2939.                     return $result; 
  2940.                 } 
  2941.             } 
  2942.         } 
  2943.  
  2944.         $result = Jetpack::register(); 
  2945.  
  2946.         // If there was an error with registration and the site was not registered, record this so we can show a message. 
  2947.         if ( ! $result || is_wp_error( $result ) ) { 
  2948.             return $result; 
  2949.         } else { 
  2950.             return true; 
  2951.         } 
  2952.     } 
  2953.  
  2954.     /** 
  2955.      * Tracking an internal event log. Try not to put too much chaff in here. 
  2956.      * 
  2957.      * [Everyone Loves a Log!](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2C7mNr5WMjA) 
  2958.      */ 
  2959.     public static function log( $code, $data = null ) { 
  2960.         // only grab the latest 200 entries 
  2961.         $log = array_slice( Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'log', array() ), -199, 199 ); 
  2962.  
  2963.         // Append our event to the log 
  2964.         $log_entry = array( 
  2965.             'time' => time(),  
  2966.             'user_id' => get_current_user_id(),  
  2967.             'blog_id' => Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'id' ),  
  2968.             'code' => $code,  
  2969.  ); 
  2970.         // Don't bother storing it unless we've got some. 
  2971.         if ( ! is_null( $data ) ) { 
  2972.             $log_entry['data'] = $data; 
  2973.         } 
  2974.         $log[] = $log_entry; 
  2975.  
  2976.         // Try add_option first, to make sure it's not autoloaded. 
  2977.         // @todo: Add an add_option method to Jetpack_Options 
  2978.         if ( ! add_option( 'jetpack_log', $log, null, 'no' ) ) { 
  2979.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'log', $log ); 
  2980.         } 
  2981.  
  2982.         /** 
  2983.          * Fires when Jetpack logs an internal event. 
  2984.          * 
  2985.          * @since 3.0.0 
  2986.          * 
  2987.          * @param array $log_entry { 
  2988.          *    Array of details about the log entry. 
  2989.          * 
  2990.          *    @param string time Time of the event. 
  2991.          *    @param int user_id ID of the user who trigerred the event. 
  2992.          *    @param int blog_id Jetpack Blog ID. 
  2993.          *    @param string code Unique name for the event. 
  2994.          *    @param string data Data about the event. 
  2995.          * } 
  2996.          */ 
  2997.         do_action( 'jetpack_log_entry', $log_entry ); 
  2998.     } 
  2999.  
  3000.     /** 
  3001.      * Get the internal event log. 
  3002.      * 
  3003.      * @param $event (string) - only return the specific log events 
  3004.      * @param $num   (int)    - get specific number of latest results, limited to 200 
  3005.      * 
  3006.      * @return array of log events || WP_Error for invalid params 
  3007.      */ 
  3008.     public static function get_log( $event = false, $num = false ) { 
  3009.         if ( $event && ! is_string( $event ) ) { 
  3010.             return new WP_Error( __( 'First param must be string or empty', 'jetpack' ) ); 
  3011.         } 
  3012.  
  3013.         if ( $num && ! is_numeric( $num ) ) { 
  3014.             return new WP_Error( __( 'Second param must be numeric or empty', 'jetpack' ) ); 
  3015.         } 
  3016.  
  3017.         $entire_log = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'log', array() ); 
  3018.  
  3019.         // If nothing set - act as it did before, otherwise let's start customizing the output 
  3020.         if ( ! $num && ! $event ) { 
  3021.             return $entire_log; 
  3022.         } else { 
  3023.             $entire_log = array_reverse( $entire_log ); 
  3024.         } 
  3025.  
  3026.         $custom_log_output = array(); 
  3027.  
  3028.         if ( $event ) { 
  3029.             foreach ( $entire_log as $log_event ) { 
  3030.                 if ( $event == $log_event[ 'code' ] ) { 
  3031.                     $custom_log_output[] = $log_event; 
  3032.                 } 
  3033.             } 
  3034.         } else { 
  3035.             $custom_log_output = $entire_log; 
  3036.         } 
  3037.  
  3038.         if ( $num ) { 
  3039.             $custom_log_output = array_slice( $custom_log_output, 0, $num ); 
  3040.         } 
  3041.  
  3042.         return $custom_log_output; 
  3043.     }

  3079.         $return["{$prefix}plugins-extra"] = Jetpack::get_parsed_plugin_data(); 
  3080.         $return["{$prefix}users"] = (int) Jetpack::get_site_user_count(); 
  3081.         $return["{$prefix}site-count"] = 0;

  3088.  
  3089.     private static function get_site_user_count() { 
  3090.         global $wpdb; 
  3091.  
  3092.         if ( function_exists( 'wp_is_large_network' ) ) { 
  3093.             if ( wp_is_large_network( 'users' ) ) { 
  3094.                 return -1; // Not a real value but should tell us that we are dealing with a large network. 
  3095.             } 
  3096.         } 
  3097.         if ( false === ( $user_count = get_transient( 'jetpack_site_user_count' ) ) ) { 
  3098.             // It wasn't there, so regenerate the data and save the transient 
  3099.             $user_count = $wpdb->get_var( "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM $wpdb->usermeta WHERE meta_key = '{$wpdb->prefix}capabilities'" ); 
  3100.             set_transient( 'jetpack_site_user_count', $user_count, DAY_IN_SECONDS ); 
  3101.         } 
  3102.         return $user_count; 
  3103.     }

  3107.     function admin_init() { 
  3108.         // If the plugin is not connected, display a connect message. 
  3109.         if ( 
  3110.             // the plugin was auto-activated and needs its candy 
  3111.             Jetpack_Options::get_option_and_ensure_autoload( 'do_activate', '0' ) 
  3112.         || 
  3113.             // the plugin is active, but was never activated.  Probably came from a site-wide network activation 
  3114.             ! Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'activated' ) 
  3115.  ) { 
  3116.             Jetpack::plugin_initialize(); 
  3117.         } 
  3118.  
  3119.         if ( ! Jetpack::is_active() && ! Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) { 
  3120.             Jetpack_Connection_Banner::init(); 
  3121.         } elseif ( false === Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'fallback_no_verify_ssl_certs' ) ) { 
  3122.             // Upgrade: 1.1 -> 1.1.1 
  3123.             // Check and see if host can verify the Jetpack servers' SSL certificate 
  3124.             $args = array(); 
  3125.             Jetpack_Client::_wp_remote_request( 
  3126.                 Jetpack::fix_url_for_bad_hosts( Jetpack::api_url( 'test' ) ),  
  3127.                 $args,  
  3128.                 true 
  3129.  ); 
  3130.         } else if ( $this->can_display_jetpack_manage_notice() && ! Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'dismissed_manage_banner' ) ) { 
  3131.             // Show the notice on the Dashboard only for now 
  3132.             add_action( 'load-index.php', array( $this, 'prepare_manage_jetpack_notice' ) ); 
  3133.         } 
  3134.  
  3135.         if ( current_user_can( 'manage_options' ) && 'AUTO' == JETPACK_CLIENT__HTTPS && ! self::permit_ssl() ) { 
  3136.             add_action( 'jetpack_notices', array( $this, 'alert_auto_ssl_fail' ) ); 
  3137.         } 
  3138.  
  3139.         add_action( 'load-plugins.php', array( $this, 'intercept_plugin_error_scrape_init' ) ); 
  3140.         add_action( 'admin_enqueue_scripts', array( $this, 'admin_menu_css' ) ); 
  3141.         add_filter( 'plugin_action_links_' . plugin_basename( JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'jetpack.php' ), array( $this, 'plugin_action_links' ) ); 
  3142.  
  3143.         if ( Jetpack::is_active() || Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) { 
  3144.             // Artificially throw errors in certain whitelisted cases during plugin activation 
  3145.             add_action( 'activate_plugin', array( $this, 'throw_error_on_activate_plugin' ) ); 
  3146.         } 
  3147.  
  3148.         // Jetpack Manage Activation Screen from .com 
  3149.         Jetpack::module_configuration_activation_screen( 'manage', array( $this, 'manage_activate_screen' ) ); 
  3150.  
  3151.         // Add custom column in wp-admin/users.php to show whether user is linked. 
  3152.         add_filter( 'manage_users_columns', array( $this, 'jetpack_icon_user_connected' ) ); 
  3153.         add_action( 'manage_users_custom_column', array( $this, 'jetpack_show_user_connected_icon' ), 10, 3 ); 
  3154.         add_action( 'admin_print_styles', array( $this, 'jetpack_user_col_style' ) ); 
  3155.     }

  3184.     /** 
  3185.      * Sometimes a plugin can activate without causing errors, but it will cause errors on the next page load. 
  3186.      * This function artificially throws errors for such cases (whitelisted). 
  3187.      * 
  3188.      * @param string $plugin The activated plugin. 
  3189.      */ 
  3190.     function throw_error_on_activate_plugin( $plugin ) { 
  3191.         $active_modules = Jetpack::get_active_modules(); 
  3192.  
  3193.         // The Shortlinks module and the Stats plugin conflict, but won't cause errors on activation because of some function_exists() checks. 
  3194.         if ( function_exists( 'stats_get_api_key' ) && in_array( 'shortlinks', $active_modules ) ) { 
  3195.             $throw = false; 
  3196.  
  3197.             // Try and make sure it really was the stats plugin 
  3198.             if ( ! class_exists( 'ReflectionFunction' ) ) { 
  3199.                 if ( 'stats.php' == basename( $plugin ) ) { 
  3200.                     $throw = true; 
  3201.                 } 
  3202.             } else { 
  3203.                 $reflection = new ReflectionFunction( 'stats_get_api_key' ); 
  3204.                 if ( basename( $plugin ) == basename( $reflection->getFileName() ) ) { 
  3205.                     $throw = true; 
  3206.                 } 
  3207.             } 
  3208.  
  3209.             if ( $throw ) { 
  3210.                 trigger_error( sprintf( __( 'Jetpack contains the most recent version of the old “%1$s” plugin.', 'jetpack' ), 'WordPress.com Stats' ), E_USER_ERROR ); 
  3211.             } 
  3212.         } 
  3213.     } 
  3214.  
  3215.     function intercept_plugin_error_scrape_init() { 
  3216.         add_action( 'check_admin_referer', array( $this, 'intercept_plugin_error_scrape' ), 10, 2 ); 
  3217.     } 
  3218.  
  3219.     function intercept_plugin_error_scrape( $action, $result ) { 
  3220.         if ( ! $result ) { 
  3221.             return; 
  3222.         } 
  3223.  
  3224.         foreach ( $this->plugins_to_deactivate as $deactivate_me ) { 
  3225.             if ( "plugin-activation-error_{$deactivate_me[0]}" == $action ) { 
  3226.                 Jetpack::bail_on_activation( sprintf( __( 'Jetpack contains the most recent version of the old “%1$s” plugin.', 'jetpack' ), $deactivate_me[1] ), false ); 
  3227.             } 
  3228.         } 
  3229.     } 
  3230.  
  3231.     function add_remote_request_handlers() { 
  3232.         add_action( 'wp_ajax_nopriv_jetpack_upload_file', array( $this, 'remote_request_handlers' ) ); 
  3233.         add_action( 'wp_ajax_nopriv_jetpack_update_file', array( $this, 'remote_request_handlers' ) ); 
  3234.     } 
  3235.  
  3236.     function remote_request_handlers() { 
  3237.         $action = current_filter(); 
  3238.  
  3239.         switch ( current_filter() ) { 
  3240.         case 'wp_ajax_nopriv_jetpack_upload_file' : 
  3241.             $response = $this->upload_handler(); 
  3242.             break; 
  3243.  
  3244.         case 'wp_ajax_nopriv_jetpack_update_file' : 
  3245.             $response = $this->upload_handler( true ); 
  3246.             break; 
  3247.         default : 
  3248.             $response = new Jetpack_Error( 'unknown_handler', 'Unknown Handler', 400 ); 
  3249.             break; 
  3250.         } 
  3251.  
  3252.         if ( ! $response ) { 
  3253.             $response = new Jetpack_Error( 'unknown_error', 'Unknown Error', 400 ); 
  3254.         } 
  3255.  
  3256.         if ( is_wp_error( $response ) ) { 
  3257.             $status_code = $response->get_error_data(); 
  3258.             $error = $response->get_error_code(); 
  3259.             $error_description = $response->get_error_message(); 
  3260.  
  3261.             if ( ! is_int( $status_code ) ) { 
  3262.                 $status_code = 400; 
  3263.             } 
  3264.  
  3265.             status_header( $status_code ); 
  3266.             die( json_encode( (object) compact( 'error', 'error_description' ) ) ); 
  3267.         } 
  3268.  
  3269.         status_header( 200 ); 
  3270.         if ( true === $response ) { 
  3271.             exit; 
  3272.         } 
  3273.  
  3274.         die( json_encode( (object) $response ) ); 
  3275.     } 
  3276.  
  3277.     /** 
  3278.      * Uploads a file gotten from the global $_FILES. 
  3279.      * If `$update_media_item` is true and `post_id` is defined 
  3280.      * the attachment file of the media item (gotten through of the post_id) 
  3281.      * will be updated instead of add a new one. 
  3282.      * 
  3283.      * @param  boolean $update_media_item - update media attachment 
  3284.      * @return array - An array describing the uploadind files process 
  3285.      */ 
  3286.     function upload_handler( $update_media_item = false ) { 
  3287.         if ( 'POST' !== strtoupper( $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] ) ) { 
  3288.             return new Jetpack_Error( 405, get_status_header_desc( 405 ), 405 ); 
  3289.         } 
  3290.  
  3291.         $user = wp_authenticate( '', '' ); 
  3292.         if ( ! $user || is_wp_error( $user ) ) { 
  3293.             return new Jetpack_Error( 403, get_status_header_desc( 403 ), 403 ); 
  3294.         } 
  3295.  
  3296.         wp_set_current_user( $user->ID ); 
  3297.  
  3298.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'upload_files' ) ) { 
  3299.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'cannot_upload_files', 'User does not have permission to upload files', 403 ); 
  3300.         } 
  3301.  
  3302.         if ( empty( $_FILES ) ) { 
  3303.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'no_files_uploaded', 'No files were uploaded: nothing to process', 400 ); 
  3304.         } 
  3305.  
  3306.         foreach ( array_keys( $_FILES ) as $files_key ) { 
  3307.             if ( ! isset( $_POST["_jetpack_file_hmac_{$files_key}"] ) ) { 
  3308.                 return new Jetpack_Error( 'missing_hmac', 'An HMAC for one or more files is missing', 400 ); 
  3309.             } 
  3310.         } 
  3311.  
  3312.         $media_keys = array_keys( $_FILES['media'] ); 
  3313.  
  3314.         $token = Jetpack_Data::get_access_token( get_current_user_id() ); 
  3315.         if ( ! $token || is_wp_error( $token ) ) { 
  3316.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'unknown_token', 'Unknown Jetpack token', 403 ); 
  3317.         } 
  3318.  
  3319.         $uploaded_files = array(); 
  3320.         $global_post = isset( $GLOBALS['post'] ) ? $GLOBALS['post'] : null; 
  3321.         unset( $GLOBALS['post'] ); 
  3322.         foreach ( $_FILES['media']['name'] as $index => $name ) { 
  3323.             $file = array(); 
  3324.             foreach ( $media_keys as $media_key ) { 
  3325.                 $file[$media_key] = $_FILES['media'][$media_key][$index]; 
  3326.             } 
  3327.  
  3328.             list( $hmac_provided, $salt ) = explode( ':', $_POST['_jetpack_file_hmac_media'][$index] ); 
  3329.  
  3330.             $hmac_file = hash_hmac_file( 'sha1', $file['tmp_name'], $salt . $token->secret ); 
  3331.             if ( $hmac_provided !== $hmac_file ) { 
  3332.                 $uploaded_files[$index] = (object) array( 'error' => 'invalid_hmac', 'error_description' => 'The corresponding HMAC for this file does not match' ); 
  3333.                 continue; 
  3334.             } 
  3335.  
  3336.             $_FILES['.jetpack.upload.'] = $file; 
  3337.             $post_id = isset( $_POST['post_id'][$index] ) ? absint( $_POST['post_id'][$index] ) : 0; 
  3338.             if ( ! current_user_can( 'edit_post', $post_id ) ) { 
  3339.                 $post_id = 0; 
  3340.             } 
  3341.  
  3342.             if ( $update_media_item ) { 
  3343.                 if ( ! isset( $post_id ) || $post_id === 0 ) { 
  3344.                     return new Jetpack_Error( 'invalid_input', 'Media ID must be defined.', 400 ); 
  3345.                 } 
  3346.  
  3347.                 $media_array = $_FILES['media']; 
  3348.  
  3349.                 $file_array['name'] = $media_array['name'][0]; 
  3350.                 $file_array['type'] = $media_array['type'][0]; 
  3351.                 $file_array['tmp_name'] = $media_array['tmp_name'][0]; 
  3352.                 $file_array['error'] = $media_array['error'][0]; 
  3353.                 $file_array['size'] = $media_array['size'][0]; 
  3354.  
  3355.                 $edited_media_item = Jetpack_Media::edit_media_file( $post_id, $file_array ); 
  3356.  
  3357.                 if ( is_wp_error( $edited_media_item ) ) { 
  3358.                     return $edited_media_item; 
  3359.                 } 
  3360.  
  3361.                 $response = (object) array( 
  3362.                     'id' => (string) $post_id,  
  3363.                     'file' => (string) $edited_media_item->post_title,  
  3364.                     'url' => (string) wp_get_attachment_url( $post_id ),  
  3365.                     'type' => (string) $edited_media_item->post_mime_type,  
  3366.                     'meta' => (array) wp_get_attachment_metadata( $post_id ),  
  3367.  ); 
  3368.  
  3369.                 return (array) array( $response ); 
  3370.             } 
  3371.  
  3372.             $attachment_id = media_handle_upload( 
  3373.                 '.jetpack.upload.',  
  3374.                 $post_id,  
  3375.                 array(),  
  3376.                 array( 
  3377.                     'action' => 'jetpack_upload_file',  
  3378.  ) 
  3379.  ); 
  3380.  
  3381.             if ( ! $attachment_id ) { 
  3382.                 $uploaded_files[$index] = (object) array( 'error' => 'unknown', 'error_description' => 'An unknown problem occurred processing the upload on the Jetpack site' ); 
  3383.             } elseif ( is_wp_error( $attachment_id ) ) { 
  3384.                 $uploaded_files[$index] = (object) array( 'error' => 'attachment_' . $attachment_id->get_error_code(), 'error_description' => $attachment_id->get_error_message() ); 
  3385.             } else { 
  3386.                 $attachment = get_post( $attachment_id ); 
  3387.                 $uploaded_files[$index] = (object) array( 
  3388.                     'id' => (string) $attachment_id,  
  3389.                     'file' => $attachment->post_title,  
  3390.                     'url' => wp_get_attachment_url( $attachment_id ),  
  3391.                     'type' => $attachment->post_mime_type,  
  3392.                     'meta' => wp_get_attachment_metadata( $attachment_id ),  
  3393.  ); 
  3394.                 // Zip files uploads are not supported unless they are done for installation purposed 
  3395.                 // lets delete them in case something goes wrong in this whole process 
  3396.                 if ( 'application/zip' === $attachment->post_mime_type ) { 
  3397.                     // Schedule a cleanup for 2 hours from now in case of failed install. 
  3398.                     wp_schedule_single_event( time() + 2 * HOUR_IN_SECONDS, 'upgrader_scheduled_cleanup', array( $attachment_id ) ); 
  3399.                 } 
  3400.             } 
  3401.         } 
  3402.         if ( ! is_null( $global_post ) ) { 
  3403.             $GLOBALS['post'] = $global_post; 
  3404.         } 
  3405.  
  3406.         return $uploaded_files; 
  3407.     }

  3503.              JETPACK__VERSION . '-20121016'

  3505.         wp_style_add_data( 'jetpack', 'rtl', 'replace' ); 
  3506.         wp_style_add_data( 'jetpack', 'suffix', $min ); 
  3507.     } 
  3508.  
  3509.     function plugin_action_links( $actions ) { 
  3510.  
  3511.         $jetpack_home = array( 'jetpack-home' => sprintf( '<a href="%s">%s</a>', Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=jetpack' ), __( 'Jetpack', 'jetpack' ) ) ); 
  3512.  
  3513.         if( current_user_can( 'jetpack_manage_modules' ) && ( Jetpack::is_active() || Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) ) { 
  3514.             return array_merge( 
  3515.                 $jetpack_home,  
  3516.                 array( 'settings' => sprintf( '<a href="%s">%s</a>', Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=jetpack#/settings' ), __( 'Settings', 'jetpack' ) ) ),  
  3517.                 array( 'support' => sprintf( '<a href="%s">%s</a>', Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=jetpack-debugger '), __( 'Support', 'jetpack' ) ) ),  
  3518.                 $actions 
  3519.  ); 
  3520.             } 
  3521.  
  3522.         return array_merge( $jetpack_home, $actions ); 
  3523.     } 
  3524.  
  3525.     /** 
  3526.      * This is the first banner 
  3527.      * It should be visible only to user that can update the option 
  3528.      * Are not connected 
  3529.      * 
  3530.      * @return null 
  3531.      */ 
  3532.     function admin_jetpack_manage_notice() { 
  3533.         $screen = get_current_screen(); 
  3534.  
  3535.         // Don't show the connect notice on the jetpack settings page. 
  3536.         if ( ! in_array( $screen->base, array( 'dashboard' ) ) || $screen->is_network || $screen->action ) { 
  3537.             return; 
  3538.         }

  3541.         $opt_in_url = $this->opt_in_jetpack_manage_url(); 
  3542.         /**

  3544.          * for example if we show the notice on dashboard and a different one if we show it on Plugins screen

  3546.          */ 
  3547.  
  3548.         ?>

  3551.                 <div class="jp-banner__description-container">
