  3553.                     <p class="jp-banner__description"><?php printf( __( 'Manage multiple Jetpack enabled sites from one single dashboard at wordpress.com. Allows all existing, connected Administrators to modify your site.', 'jetpack' ), 'https://jetpack.com/support/site-management' ); ?></p> 
  3554.                     <p class="jp-banner__button-container"> 
  3555.                         <a href="<?php echo esc_url( $opt_in_url ); ?>" class="button button-primary" id="wpcom-connect"><?php _e( 'Activate Jetpack Manage', 'jetpack' ); ?></a> 
  3556.                         <a href="https://jetpack.com/support/site-management" class="button" target="_blank" title="<?php esc_attr_e( 'Learn more about Jetpack Manage on Jetpack.com', 'jetpack' ); ?>"><?php _e( 'Learn more', 'jetpack' ); ?></a> 
  3557.                     </p> 
  3558.                 </div> 
  3559.         </div> 
  3560.         <?php 
  3561.     } 
  3562.  
  3563.     /** 
  3564.      * Returns the url that the user clicks to remove the notice for the big banner 
  3565.      * @return (string) 
  3566.      */ 
  3567.     function opt_out_jetpack_manage_url() { 
  3568.         $referer = '&_wp_http_referer=' . add_query_arg( '_wp_http_referer', null ); 
  3569.         return wp_nonce_url( Jetpack::admin_url( 'jetpack-notice=jetpack-manage-opt-out' . $referer ), 'jetpack_manage_banner_opt_out' ); 
  3570.     } 
  3571.     /** 
  3572.      * Returns the url that the user clicks to opt in to Jetpack Manage 
  3573.      * @return (string) 
  3574.      */ 
  3575.     function opt_in_jetpack_manage_url() { 
  3576.         return wp_nonce_url( Jetpack::admin_url( 'jetpack-notice=jetpack-manage-opt-in' ), 'jetpack_manage_banner_opt_in' ); 
  3577.     } 
  3578.  
  3579.     function opt_in_jetpack_manage_notice() { 
  3580.         ?> 
  3581.         <div class="wrap"> 
  3582.             <div id="message" class="jetpack-message is-opt-in"> 
  3583.                 <?php echo sprintf( __( '<p><a href="%1$s" title="Opt in to WordPress.com Site Management" >Activate Site Management</a> to manage multiple sites from our centralized dashboard at wordpress.com/sites. <a href="%2$s" target="_blank">Learn more</a>.</p><a href="%1$s" class="jp-button">Activate Now</a>', 'jetpack' ), $this->opt_in_jetpack_manage_url(), 'https://jetpack.com/support/site-management' ); ?> 
  3584.             </div> 
  3585.         </div> 
  3586.         <?php 
  3587.  
  3588.     } 
  3589.     /** 
  3590.      * Determines whether to show the notice of not true = display notice 
  3591.      * @return (bool) 
  3592.      */ 
  3593.     function can_display_jetpack_manage_notice() { 
  3594.         // never display the notice to users that can't do anything about it anyways 
  3595.         if( ! current_user_can( 'jetpack_manage_modules' ) ) 
  3596.             return false; 
  3597.  
  3598.         // don't display if we are in development more 
  3599.         if( Jetpack::is_development_mode() ) { 
  3600.             return false; 
  3601.         } 
  3602.         // don't display if the site is private 
  3603.         if(  ! Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'public' ) ) 
  3604.             return false; 
  3605.  
  3606.         /** 
  3607.          * Should the Jetpack Remote Site Management notice be displayed. 
  3608.          * 
  3609.          * @since 3.3.0 
  3610.          * 
  3611.          * @param bool ! self::is_module_active( 'manage' ) Is the Manage module inactive. 
  3612.          */ 
  3613.         return apply_filters( 'can_display_jetpack_manage_notice', ! self::is_module_active( 'manage' ) ); 
  3614.     } 
  3615.  
  3616.     /** 
  3617.      * Registration flow: 
  3618.      * 1 - ::admin_page_load() action=register 
  3619.      * 2 - ::try_registration() 
  3620.      * 3 - ::register() 
  3621.      *     - Creates jetpack_register option containing two secrets and a timestamp 
  3622.      *     - Calls https://jetpack.wordpress.com/jetpack.register/1/ with 
  3623.      *       siteurl, home, gmt_offset, timezone_string, site_name, secret_1, secret_2, site_lang, timeout, stats_id 
  3624.      *     - That request to jetpack.wordpress.com does not immediately respond.  It first makes a request BACK to this site's 
  3625.      *       xmlrpc.php?for=jetpack: RPC method: jetpack.verifyRegistration, Parameters: secret_1 
  3626.      *     - The XML-RPC request verifies secret_1, deletes both secrets and responds with: secret_2 
  3627.      *     - https://jetpack.wordpress.com/jetpack.register/1/ verifies that XML-RPC response (secret_2) then finally responds itself with 
  3628.      *       jetpack_id, jetpack_secret, jetpack_public 
  3629.      *     - ::register() then stores jetpack_options: id => jetpack_id, blog_token => jetpack_secret 
  3630.      * 4 - redirect to https://wordpress.com/start/jetpack-connect 
  3631.      * 5 - user logs in with WP.com account 
  3632.      * 6 - remote request to this site's xmlrpc.php with action remoteAuthorize, Jetpack_XMLRPC_Server->remote_authorize 
  3633.      *        - Jetpack_Client_Server::authorize() 
  3634.      *        - Jetpack_Client_Server::get_token() 
  3635.      *        - GET https://jetpack.wordpress.com/jetpack.token/1/ with 
  3636.      *        client_id, client_secret, grant_type, code, redirect_uri:action=authorize, state, scope, user_email, user_login 
  3637.      *            - which responds with access_token, token_type, scope 
  3638.      *        - Jetpack_Client_Server::authorize() stores jetpack_options: user_token => access_token.$user_id 
  3639.      *        - Jetpack::activate_default_modules() 
  3640.      *             - Deactivates deprecated plugins 
  3641.      *             - Activates all default modules 
  3642.      *        - Responds with either error, or 'connected' for new connection, or 'linked' for additional linked users 
  3643.      * 7 - For a new connection, user selects a Jetpack plan on wordpress.com 
  3644.      * 8 - User is redirected back to wp-admin/index.php?page=jetpack with state:message=authorized 
  3645.      *     Done! 
  3646.      */ 
  3647.  
  3648.     /** 
  3649.      * Handles the page load events for the Jetpack admin page 
  3650.      */ 
  3651.     function admin_page_load() { 
  3652.         $error = false; 
  3653.  
  3654.         // Make sure we have the right body class to hook stylings for subpages off of. 
  3655.         add_filter( 'admin_body_class', array( __CLASS__, 'add_jetpack_pagestyles' ) ); 
  3656.  
  3657.         if ( ! empty( $_GET['jetpack_restate'] ) ) { 
  3658.             // Should only be used in intermediate redirects to preserve state across redirects 
  3659.             Jetpack::restate(); 
  3660.         } 
  3661.  
  3662.         if ( isset( $_GET['connect_url_redirect'] ) ) { 
  3663.             // User clicked in the iframe to link their accounts 
  3664.             if ( ! Jetpack::is_user_connected() ) { 
  3665.                 $connect_url = $this->build_connect_url( true, false, 'iframe' ); 
  3666.                 if ( isset( $_GET['notes_iframe'] ) ) 
  3667.                     $connect_url .= '¬es_iframe'; 
  3668.                 wp_redirect( $connect_url ); 
  3669.                 exit; 
  3670.             } else { 
  3671.                 if ( ! isset( $_GET['calypso_env'] ) ) { 
  3672.                     Jetpack::state( 'message', 'already_authorized' ); 
  3673.                     wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url() ); 
  3674.                 } else { 
  3675.                     $connect_url = $this->build_connect_url( true, false, 'iframe' ); 
  3676.                     $connect_url .= '&already_authorized=true'; 
  3677.                     wp_redirect( $connect_url ); 
  3678.                 } 
  3679.             } 
  3680.         } 
  3681.  
  3682.  
  3683.         if ( isset( $_GET['action'] ) ) { 
  3684.             switch ( $_GET['action'] ) { 
  3685.             case 'authorize': 
  3686.                 if ( Jetpack::is_active() && Jetpack::is_user_connected() ) { 
  3687.                     Jetpack::state( 'message', 'already_authorized' ); 
  3688.                     wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url() ); 
  3689.                     exit; 
  3690.                 } 
  3691.                 Jetpack::log( 'authorize' ); 
  3692.                 $client_server = new Jetpack_Client_Server; 
  3693.                 $client_server->client_authorize(); 
  3694.                 exit; 
  3695.             case 'register' : 
  3696.                 if ( ! current_user_can( 'jetpack_connect' ) ) { 
  3697.                     $error = 'cheatin'; 
  3698.                     break; 
  3699.                 } 
  3700.                 check_admin_referer( 'jetpack-register' ); 
  3701.                 Jetpack::log( 'register' ); 
  3702.                 Jetpack::maybe_set_version_option(); 
  3703.                 $registered = Jetpack::try_registration(); 
  3704.                 if ( is_wp_error( $registered ) ) { 
  3705.                     $error = $registered->get_error_code(); 
  3706.                     Jetpack::state( 'error', $error ); 
  3707.                     Jetpack::state( 'error', $registered->get_error_message() ); 
  3708.                     break; 
  3709.                 } 
  3710.  
  3711.                 $from = isset( $_GET['from'] ) ? $_GET['from'] : false; 
  3712.  
  3713.                 wp_redirect( $this->build_connect_url( true, false, $from ) ); 
  3714.                 exit; 
  3715.             case 'activate' : 
  3716.                 if ( ! current_user_can( 'jetpack_activate_modules' ) ) { 
  3717.                     $error = 'cheatin'; 
  3718.                     break; 
  3719.                 } 
  3720.  
  3721.                 $module = stripslashes( $_GET['module'] ); 
  3722.                 check_admin_referer( "jetpack_activate-$module" ); 
  3723.                 Jetpack::log( 'activate', $module ); 
  3724.                 Jetpack::activate_module( $module ); 
  3725.                 // The following two lines will rarely happen, as Jetpack::activate_module normally exits at the end. 
  3726.                 wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=jetpack' ) ); 
  3727.                 exit; 
  3728.             case 'activate_default_modules' : 
  3729.                 check_admin_referer( 'activate_default_modules' ); 
  3730.                 Jetpack::log( 'activate_default_modules' ); 
  3731.                 Jetpack::restate(); 
  3732.                 $min_version = isset( $_GET['min_version'] ) ? $_GET['min_version'] : false; 
  3733.                 $max_version = isset( $_GET['max_version'] ) ? $_GET['max_version'] : false; 
  3734.                 $other_modules = isset( $_GET['other_modules'] ) && is_array( $_GET['other_modules'] ) ? $_GET['other_modules'] : array(); 
  3735.                 Jetpack::activate_default_modules( $min_version, $max_version, $other_modules ); 
  3736.                 wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=jetpack' ) ); 
  3737.                 exit; 
  3738.             case 'disconnect' : 
  3739.                 if ( ! current_user_can( 'jetpack_disconnect' ) ) { 
  3740.                     $error = 'cheatin'; 
  3741.                     break; 
  3742.                 } 
  3743.  
  3744.                 check_admin_referer( 'jetpack-disconnect' ); 
  3745.                 Jetpack::log( 'disconnect' ); 
  3746.                 Jetpack::disconnect(); 
  3747.                 wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url( 'disconnected=true' ) ); 
  3748.                 exit; 
  3749.             case 'reconnect' : 
  3750.                 if ( ! current_user_can( 'jetpack_reconnect' ) ) { 
  3751.                     $error = 'cheatin'; 
  3752.                     break; 
  3753.                 } 
  3754.  
  3755.                 check_admin_referer( 'jetpack-reconnect' ); 
  3756.                 Jetpack::log( 'reconnect' ); 
  3757.                 $this->disconnect(); 
  3758.                 wp_redirect( $this->build_connect_url( true, false, 'reconnect' ) ); 
  3759.                 exit; 
  3760.             case 'deactivate' : 
  3761.                 if ( ! current_user_can( 'jetpack_deactivate_modules' ) ) { 
  3762.                     $error = 'cheatin'; 
  3763.                     break; 
  3764.                 } 
  3765.  
  3766.                 $modules = stripslashes( $_GET['module'] ); 
  3767.                 check_admin_referer( "jetpack_deactivate-$modules" ); 
  3768.                 foreach ( explode( ', ', $modules ) as $module ) { 
  3769.                     Jetpack::log( 'deactivate', $module ); 
  3770.                     Jetpack::deactivate_module( $module ); 
  3771.                     Jetpack::state( 'message', 'module_deactivated' ); 
  3772.                 } 
  3773.                 Jetpack::state( 'module', $modules ); 
  3774.                 wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url( 'page=jetpack' ) ); 
  3775.                 exit; 
  3776.             case 'unlink' : 
  3777.                 $redirect = isset( $_GET['redirect'] ) ? $_GET['redirect'] : ''; 
  3778.                 check_admin_referer( 'jetpack-unlink' ); 
  3779.                 Jetpack::log( 'unlink' ); 
  3780.                 $this->unlink_user(); 
  3781.                 Jetpack::state( 'message', 'unlinked' ); 
  3782.                 if ( 'sub-unlink' == $redirect ) { 
  3783.                     wp_safe_redirect( admin_url() ); 
  3784.                 } else { 
  3785.                     wp_safe_redirect( Jetpack::admin_url( array( 'page' => $redirect ) ) ); 
  3786.                 } 
  3787.                 exit; 
  3788.             default: 
  3789.                 /** 
  3790.                  * Fires when a Jetpack admin page is loaded with an unrecognized parameter. 
  3791.                  * 
  3792.                  * @since 2.6.0 
  3793.                  * 
  3794.                  * @param string sanitize_key( $_GET['action'] ) Unrecognized URL parameter. 
  3795.                  */ 
  3796.                 do_action( 'jetpack_unrecognized_action', sanitize_key( $_GET['action'] ) ); 
  3797.             } 
  3798.         } 
  3799.  
  3800.         if ( ! $error = $error ? $error : Jetpack::state( 'error' ) ) { 
  3801.             self::activate_new_modules( true ); 
  3802.         } 
  3803.  
  3804.         $message_code = Jetpack::state( 'message' ); 
  3805.         if ( Jetpack::state( 'optin-manage' ) ) { 
  3806.             $activated_manage = $message_code; 
  3807.             $message_code = 'jetpack-manage'; 
  3808.         } 
  3809.  
  3810.         switch ( $message_code ) { 
  3811.         case 'jetpack-manage': 
  3812.             $this->message = '<strong>' . sprintf( __( 'You are all set! Your site can now be managed from <a href="%s" target="_blank">wordpress.com/sites</a>.', 'jetpack' ), 'https://wordpress.com/sites' ) . '</strong>'; 
  3813.             if ( $activated_manage ) { 
  3814.                 $this->message .= '<br /><strong>' . __( 'Manage has been activated for you!', 'jetpack' ) . '</strong>'; 
  3815.             } 
  3816.             break; 
  3817.  
  3818.         } 
  3819.  
  3820.         $deactivated_plugins = Jetpack::state( 'deactivated_plugins' ); 
  3821.  
  3822.         if ( ! empty( $deactivated_plugins ) ) { 
  3823.             $deactivated_plugins = explode( ', ', $deactivated_plugins ); 
  3824.             $deactivated_titles = array(); 
  3825.             foreach ( $deactivated_plugins as $deactivated_plugin ) { 
  3826.                 if ( ! isset( $this->plugins_to_deactivate[$deactivated_plugin] ) ) { 
  3827.                     continue; 
  3828.                 } 
  3829.  
  3830.                 $deactivated_titles[] = '<strong>' . str_replace( ' ', ' ', $this->plugins_to_deactivate[$deactivated_plugin][1] ) . '</strong>'; 
  3831.             } 
  3832.  
  3833.             if ( $deactivated_titles ) { 
  3834.                 if ( $this->message ) { 
  3835.                     $this->message .= "<br /><br />\n"; 
  3836.                 } 
  3837.  
  3838.                 $this->message .= wp_sprintf( 
  3839.                     _n( 
  3840.                         'Jetpack contains the most recent version of the old %l plugin.',  
  3841.                         'Jetpack contains the most recent versions of the old %l plugins.',  
  3842.                         count( $deactivated_titles ),  
  3843.                         'jetpack' 
  3844.  ),  
  3845.                     $deactivated_titles 
  3846.  ); 
  3847.  
  3848.                 $this->message .= "<br />\n"; 
  3849.  
  3850.                 $this->message .= _n( 
  3851.                     'The old version has been deactivated and can be removed from your site.',  
  3852.                     'The old versions have been deactivated and can be removed from your site.',  
  3853.                     count( $deactivated_titles ),  
  3854.                     'jetpack' 
  3855.  ); 
  3856.             } 
  3857.         } 
  3858.  
  3859.         $this->privacy_checks = Jetpack::state( 'privacy_checks' ); 
  3860.  
  3861.         if ( $this->message || $this->error || $this->privacy_checks || $this->can_display_jetpack_manage_notice() ) { 
  3862.             add_action( 'jetpack_notices', array( $this, 'admin_notices' ) ); 
  3863.         } 
  3864.  
  3865.         if ( isset( $_GET['configure'] ) && Jetpack::is_module( $_GET['configure'] ) && current_user_can( 'manage_options' ) ) { 
  3866.             /** 
  3867.              * Fires when a module configuration page is loaded. 
  3868.              * The dynamic part of the hook is the configure parameter from the URL. 
  3869.              * 
  3870.              * @since 1.1.0 
  3871.              */ 
  3872.             do_action( 'jetpack_module_configuration_load_' . $_GET['configure'] ); 
  3873.         } 
  3874.  
  3875.         add_filter( 'jetpack_short_module_description', 'wptexturize' ); 
  3876.     } 
  3877.  
  3878.     function admin_notices() { 
  3879.  
  3880.         if ( $this->error ) { 
  3881. ?> 
  3882. <div id="message" class="jetpack-message jetpack-err"> 
  3883.     <div class="squeezer"> 
  3884.         <h2><?php echo wp_kses( $this->error, array( 'a' => array( 'href' => array() ), 'small' => true, 'code' => true, 'strong' => true, 'br' => true, 'b' => true ) ); ?></h2> 
  3885. <?php    if ( $desc = Jetpack::state( 'error_description' ) ) : ?> 
  3886.         <p><?php echo esc_html( stripslashes( $desc ) ); ?></p> 
  3887. <?php    endif; ?> 
  3888.     </div> 
  3889. </div> 
  3890. <?php 
  3891.         } 
  3892.  
  3893.         if ( $this->message ) { 
  3894. ?> 
  3895. <div id="message" class="jetpack-message"> 
  3896.     <div class="squeezer"> 
  3897.         <h2><?php echo wp_kses( $this->message, array( 'strong' => array(), 'a' => array( 'href' => true ), 'br' => true ) ); ?></h2> 
  3898.     </div> 
  3899. </div> 
  3900. <?php 
  3901.         } 
  3902.  
  3903.         if ( $this->privacy_checks ) : 
  3904.             $module_names = $module_slugs = array(); 
  3905.  
  3906.             $privacy_checks = explode( ', ', $this->privacy_checks ); 
  3907.             $privacy_checks = array_filter( $privacy_checks, array( 'Jetpack', 'is_module' ) ); 
  3908.             foreach ( $privacy_checks as $module_slug ) { 
  3909.                 $module = Jetpack::get_module( $module_slug ); 
  3910.                 if ( ! $module ) { 
  3911.                     continue; 
  3912.                 } 
  3913.  
  3914.                 $module_slugs[] = $module_slug; 
  3915.                 $module_names[] = "<strong>{$module['name']}</strong>"; 
  3916.             } 
  3917.  
  3918.             $module_slugs = join( ', ', $module_slugs ); 
  3919. ?> 
  3920. <div id="message" class="jetpack-message jetpack-err"> 
  3921.     <div class="squeezer"> 
  3922.         <h2><strong><?php esc_html_e( 'Is this site private?', 'jetpack' ); ?></strong></h2><br /> 
  3923.         <p><?php 
  3924.             echo wp_kses( 
  3925.                 wptexturize( 
  3926.                     wp_sprintf( 
  3927.                         _nx( 
  3928.                             "Like your site's RSS feeds, %l allows access to your posts and other content to third parties.",  
  3929.                             "Like your site's RSS feeds, %l allow access to your posts and other content to third parties.",  
  3930.                             count( $privacy_checks ),  
  3931.                             '%l = list of Jetpack module/feature names',  
  3932.                             'jetpack' 
  3933.  ),  
  3934.                         $module_names 
  3935.  ) 
  3936.  ),  
  3937.                 array( 'strong' => true ) 
  3938.  ); 
  3939.  
  3940.             echo "\n<br />\n"; 
  3941.  
  3942.             echo wp_kses( 
  3943.                 sprintf( 
  3944.                     _nx( 
  3945.                         'If your site is not publicly accessible, consider <a href="%1$s" title="%2$s">deactivating this feature</a>.',  
  3946.                         'If your site is not publicly accessible, consider <a href="%1$s" title="%2$s">deactivating these features</a>.',  
  3947.                         count( $privacy_checks ),  
  3948.                         '%1$s = deactivation URL, %2$s = "Deactivate {list of Jetpack module/feature names}',  
  3949.                         'jetpack' 
  3950.  ),  
  3951.                     wp_nonce_url( 
  3952.                         Jetpack::admin_url( 
  3953.                             array( 
  3954.                                 'page' => 'jetpack',  
  3955.                                 'action' => 'deactivate',  
  3956.                                 'module' => urlencode( $module_slugs ),  
  3957.  ) 
  3958.  ),  
  3959.                         "jetpack_deactivate-$module_slugs" 
  3960.  ),

  3976.     /** 
  3977.      * Record a stat for later output.  This will only currently output in the admin_footer. 
  3978.      */ 
  3979.     function stat( $group, $detail ) { 
  3980.         if ( ! isset( $this->stats[ $group ] ) ) 
  3981.             $this->stats[ $group ] = array(); 
  3982.         $this->stats[ $group ][] = $detail; 
  3983.     } 
  3984.  
  3985.     /** 
  3986.      * Load stats pixels. $group is auto-prefixed with "x_jetpack-" 
  3987.      */ 
  3988.     function do_stats( $method = '' ) { 
  3989.         if ( is_array( $this->stats ) && count( $this->stats ) ) { 
  3990.             foreach ( $this->stats as $group => $stats ) { 
  3991.                 if ( is_array( $stats ) && count( $stats ) ) { 
  3992.                     $args = array( "x_jetpack-{$group}" => implode( ', ', $stats ) ); 
  3993.                     if ( 'server_side' === $method ) { 
  3994.                         self::do_server_side_stat( $args ); 
  3995.                     } else { 
  3996.                         echo '<img src="' . esc_url( self::build_stats_url( $args ) ) . '" width="1" height="1" style="display:none;" />'; 
  3997.                     } 
  3998.                 } 
  3999.                 unset( $this->stats[ $group ] ); 
  4000.             } 
  4001.         } 
  4002.     } 
  4003.  
  4004.     /** 
  4005.      * Runs stats code for a one-off, server-side. 
  4006.      * 
  4007.      * @param $args array|string The arguments to append to the URL. Should include `x_jetpack-{$group}={$stats}` or whatever we want to store. 
  4008.      * 
  4009.      * @return bool If it worked. 
  4010.      */ 
  4011.     static function do_server_side_stat( $args ) { 
  4012.         $response = wp_remote_get( esc_url_raw( self::build_stats_url( $args ) ) ); 
  4013.         if ( is_wp_error( $response ) ) 
  4014.             return false; 
  4015.  
  4016.         if ( 200 !== wp_remote_retrieve_response_code( $response ) ) 
  4017.             return false; 
  4018.  
  4019.         return true; 
  4020.     } 
  4021.  
  4022.     /** 
  4023.      * Builds the stats url. 
  4024.      * 
  4025.      * @param $args array|string The arguments to append to the URL. 
  4026.      * 
  4027.      * @return string The URL to be pinged. 
  4028.      */ 
  4029.     static function build_stats_url( $args ) { 
  4030.         $defaults = array( 
  4031.             'v' => 'wpcom2',  
  4032.             'rand' => md5( mt_rand( 0, 999 ) . time() ),  
  4033.  ); 
  4034.         $args = wp_parse_args( $args, $defaults ); 
  4035.         /** 
  4036.          * Filter the URL used as the Stats tracking pixel. 
  4037.          * 
  4038.          * @since 2.3.2 
  4039.          * 
  4040.          * @param string $url Base URL used as the Stats tracking pixel. 
  4041.          */ 
  4042.         $base_url = apply_filters( 
  4043.             'jetpack_stats_base_url',  
  4044.             'https://pixel.wp.com/g.gif' 
  4045.  ); 
  4046.         $url = add_query_arg( $args, $base_url ); 
  4047.         return $url; 
  4048.     }

  4050.     static function translate_current_user_to_role() { 
  4051.         foreach ( self::$capability_translations as $role => $cap ) { 
  4052.             if ( current_user_can( $role ) || current_user_can( $cap ) ) { 
  4053.                 return $role; 
  4054.             } 
  4055.         } 
  4056.  
  4057.         return false; 
  4058.     } 
  4059.  
  4060.     static function translate_role_to_cap( $role ) { 
  4061.         if ( ! isset( self::$capability_translations[$role] ) ) { 
  4062.             return false; 
  4063.         } 
  4064.  
  4065.         return self::$capability_translations[$role]; 
  4066.     } 
  4067.  
  4068.     static function sign_role( $role ) { 
  4069.         if ( ! $user_id = (int) get_current_user_id() ) { 
  4070.             return false; 
  4071.         } 
  4072.  
  4073.         $token = Jetpack_Data::get_access_token(); 
  4074.         if ( ! $token || is_wp_error( $token ) ) { 
  4075.             return false; 
  4076.         } 
  4077.  
  4078.         return $role . ':' . hash_hmac( 'md5', "{$role}|{$user_id}", $token->secret ); 
  4079.     }

  4081.  
  4082.     /** 
  4083.      * Builds a URL to the Jetpack connection auth page 
  4084.      * 
  4085.      * @since 3.9.5 
  4086.      * 
  4087.      * @param bool $raw If true, URL will not be escaped. 
  4088.      * @param bool|string $redirect If true, will redirect back to Jetpack wp-admin landing page after connection. 
  4089.      *                              If string, will be a custom redirect. 
  4090.      * @param bool|string $from If not false, adds 'from=$from' param to the connect URL. 
  4091.      * 
  4092.      * @return string Connect URL 
  4093.      */ 
  4094.     function build_connect_url( $raw = false, $redirect = false, $from = false ) { 
  4095.         if ( ! Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'blog_token' ) || ! Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'id' ) ) { 
  4096.             $url = Jetpack::nonce_url_no_esc( Jetpack::admin_url( 'action=register' ), 'jetpack-register' ); 
  4097.             if( is_network_admin() ) { 
  4098.                 $url = add_query_arg( 'is_multisite', network_admin_url( 'admin.php?page=jetpack-settings' ), $url ); 
  4099.             } 
  4100.         } else { 
  4101.             if ( defined( 'JETPACK__GLOTPRESS_LOCALES_PATH' ) && include_once JETPACK__GLOTPRESS_LOCALES_PATH ) { 
  4102.                 $gp_locale = GP_Locales::by_field( 'wp_locale', get_locale() ); 
  4103.             } 
  4104.  
  4105.             $role = self::translate_current_user_to_role(); 
  4106.             $signed_role = self::sign_role( $role ); 
  4107.  
  4108.             $user = wp_get_current_user(); 
  4109.  
  4110.             $jetpack_admin_page = esc_url_raw( admin_url( 'admin.php?page=jetpack' ) ); 
  4111.             $redirect = $redirect 
  4112.                 ? wp_validate_redirect( esc_url_raw( $redirect ), $jetpack_admin_page ) 
  4113.                 : $jetpack_admin_page; 
  4114.  
  4115.             if( isset( $_REQUEST['is_multisite'] ) ) { 
  4116.                 $redirect = Jetpack_Network::init()->get_url( 'network_admin_page' ); 
  4117.             } 
  4118.  
  4119.             $secrets = Jetpack::init()->generate_secrets( 'authorize' ); 
  4120.             @list( $secret ) = explode( ':', $secrets ); 
  4121.  
  4122.             $site_icon = ( function_exists( 'has_site_icon') && has_site_icon() ) 
  4123.                 ? get_site_icon_url() 
  4124.                 : false; 
  4125.  
  4126.             /** 
  4127.              * Filter the type of authorization. 
  4128.              * 'calypso' completes authorization on wordpress.com/jetpack/connect 
  4129.              * while 'jetpack' ( or any other value ) completes the authorization at jetpack.wordpress.com. 
  4130.              * 
  4131.              * @since 4.3.3 
  4132.              * 
  4133.              * @param string $auth_type Defaults to 'calypso', can also be 'jetpack'. 
  4134.              */ 
  4135.             $auth_type = apply_filters( 'jetpack_auth_type', 'calypso' ); 
  4136.  
  4137.             $args = urlencode_deep( 
  4138.                 array( 
  4139.                     'response_type' => 'code',  
  4140.                     'client_id' => Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'id' ),  
  4141.                     'redirect_uri' => add_query_arg( 
  4142.                         array( 
  4143.                             'action' => 'authorize',  
  4144.                             '_wpnonce' => wp_create_nonce( "jetpack-authorize_{$role}_{$redirect}" ),  
  4145.                             'redirect' => urlencode( $redirect ),  
  4146.  ),  
  4147.                         esc_url( admin_url( 'admin.php?page=jetpack' ) ) 
  4148.  ),  
  4149.                     'state' => $user->ID,  
  4150.                     'scope' => $signed_role,  
  4151.                     'user_email' => $user->user_email,  
  4152.                     'user_login' => $user->user_login,  
  4153.                     'is_active' => Jetpack::is_active(),  
  4154.                     'jp_version' => JETPACK__VERSION,  
  4155.                     'auth_type' => $auth_type,  
  4156.                     'secret' => $secret,  
  4157.                     'locale' => ( isset( $gp_locale ) && isset( $gp_locale->slug ) ) ? $gp_locale->slug : '',  
  4158.                     'blogname' => get_option( 'blogname' ),  
  4159.                     'site_url' => site_url(),  
  4160.                     'home_url' => home_url(),  
  4161.                     'site_icon' => $site_icon,  
  4162.  ) 
  4163.  ); 
  4164.  
  4165.             $url = add_query_arg( $args, Jetpack::api_url( 'authorize' ) ); 
  4166.         } 
  4167.  
  4168.         if ( $from ) { 
  4169.             $url = add_query_arg( 'from', $from, $url ); 
  4170.         } 
  4171.  
  4172.         if ( isset( $_GET['calypso_env'] ) ) { 
  4173.             $url = add_query_arg( 'calypso_env', sanitize_key( $_GET['calypso_env'] ), $url ); 
  4174.         } 
  4175.  
  4176.         return $raw ? $url : esc_url( $url ); 
  4177.     }

  4195.     function dismiss_jetpack_notice() { 
  4196.  
  4197.         if ( ! isset( $_GET['jetpack-notice'] ) ) { 
  4198.             return; 
  4199.         } 
  4200.  
  4201.         switch( $_GET['jetpack-notice'] ) { 
  4202.             case 'dismiss': 
  4203.                 if ( check_admin_referer( 'jetpack-deactivate' ) && ! is_plugin_active_for_network( plugin_basename( JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'jetpack.php' ) ) ) { 
  4204.  
  4205.                     require_once ABSPATH . 'wp-admin/includes/plugin.php'; 
  4206.                     deactivate_plugins( JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'jetpack.php', false, false ); 
  4207.                     wp_safe_redirect( admin_url() . 'plugins.php?deactivate=true&plugin_status=all&paged=1&s=' ); 
  4208.                 } 
  4209.                 break; 
  4210.             case 'jetpack-manage-opt-out': 
  4211.  
  4212.                 if ( check_admin_referer( 'jetpack_manage_banner_opt_out' ) ) { 
  4213.                     // Don't show the banner again 
  4214.  
  4215.                     Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'dismissed_manage_banner', true ); 
  4216.                     // redirect back to the page that had the notice 
  4217.                     if ( wp_get_referer() ) { 
  4218.                         wp_safe_redirect( wp_get_referer() ); 
  4219.                     } else { 
  4220.                         // Take me to Jetpack 
  4221.                         wp_safe_redirect( admin_url( 'admin.php?page=jetpack' ) ); 
  4222.                     } 
  4223.                 } 
  4224.                 break; 
  4225.             case 'jetpack-protect-multisite-opt-out': 
  4226.  
  4227.                 if ( check_admin_referer( 'jetpack_protect_multisite_banner_opt_out' ) ) { 
  4228.                     // Don't show the banner again 
  4229.  
  4230.                     update_site_option( 'jetpack_dismissed_protect_multisite_banner', true ); 
  4231.                     // redirect back to the page that had the notice 
  4232.                     if ( wp_get_referer() ) { 
  4233.                         wp_safe_redirect( wp_get_referer() ); 
  4234.                     } else { 
  4235.                         // Take me to Jetpack 
  4236.                         wp_safe_redirect( admin_url( 'admin.php?page=jetpack' ) ); 
  4237.                     } 
  4238.                 } 
  4239.                 break; 
  4240.             case 'jetpack-manage-opt-in': 
  4241.                 if ( check_admin_referer( 'jetpack_manage_banner_opt_in' ) ) { 
  4242.                     // This makes sure that we are redirect to jetpack home so that we can see the Success Message. 
  4243.  
  4244.                     $redirection_url = Jetpack::admin_url(); 
  4245.                     remove_action( 'jetpack_pre_activate_module', array( Jetpack_Admin::init(), 'fix_redirect' ) ); 
  4246.  
  4247.                     // Don't redirect form the Jetpack Setting Page 
  4248.                     $referer_parsed = parse_url ( wp_get_referer() ); 
  4249.                     // check that we do have a wp_get_referer and the query paramater is set orderwise go to the Jetpack Home 
  4250.                     if ( isset( $referer_parsed['query'] ) && false !== strpos( $referer_parsed['query'], 'page=jetpack_modules' ) ) { 
  4251.                         // Take the user to Jetpack home except when on the setting page 
  4252.                         $redirection_url = wp_get_referer(); 
  4253.                         add_action( 'jetpack_pre_activate_module', array( Jetpack_Admin::init(), 'fix_redirect' ) ); 
  4254.                     } 
  4255.                     // Also update the JSON API FULL MANAGEMENT Option 
  4256.                     Jetpack::activate_module( 'manage', false, false ); 
  4257.  
  4258.                     // Special Message when option in. 
  4259.                     Jetpack::state( 'optin-manage', 'true' ); 
  4260.                     // Activate the Module if not activated already 
  4261.  
  4262.                     // Redirect properly 
  4263.                     wp_safe_redirect( $redirection_url ); 
  4264.  
  4265.                 } 
  4266.                 break; 
  4267.         } 
  4268.     }

  4381.     public static function sort_modules( $a, $b ) { 
  4382.         if ( $a['sort'] == $b['sort'] ) 
  4383.             return 0; 
  4384.  
  4385.         return ( $a['sort'] < $b['sort'] ) ? -1 : 1; 
  4386.     }

  4388.     function ajax_recheck_ssl() { 
  4389.         check_ajax_referer( 'recheck-ssl', 'ajax-nonce' ); 
  4390.         $result = Jetpack::permit_ssl( true ); 
  4391.         wp_send_json( array( 
  4392.             'enabled' => $result,  
  4393.             'message' => get_transient( 'jetpack_https_test_message' ) 
  4394.  ) ); 
  4395.     }

  4399.     /** 
  4400.      * Returns the requested Jetpack API URL 
  4401.      * 
  4402.      * @return string 
  4403.      */ 
  4404.     public static function api_url( $relative_url ) { 
  4405.         return trailingslashit( JETPACK__API_BASE . $relative_url ) . JETPACK__API_VERSION . '/'; 
  4406.     } 
  4407.  
  4408.     /** 
  4409.      * Some hosts disable the OpenSSL extension and so cannot make outgoing HTTPS requsets 
  4410.      */ 
  4411.     public static function fix_url_for_bad_hosts( $url ) { 
  4412.         if ( 0 !== strpos( $url, 'https://' ) ) { 
  4413.             return $url; 
  4414.         } 
  4415.  
  4416.         switch ( JETPACK_CLIENT__HTTPS ) { 
  4417.             case 'ALWAYS' : 
  4418.                 return $url; 
  4419.             case 'NEVER' : 
  4420.                 return set_url_scheme( $url, 'http' ); 
  4421.             // default : case 'AUTO' : 
  4422.         } 
  4423.  
  4424.         // we now return the unmodified SSL URL by default, as a security precaution 
  4425.         return $url; 
  4426.     } 
  4427.  
  4428.     /** 
  4429.      * Checks to see if the URL is using SSL to connect with Jetpack 
  4430.      * 
  4431.      * @since 2.3.3 
  4432.      * @return boolean 
  4433.      */ 
  4434.     public static function permit_ssl( $force_recheck = false ) { 
  4435.         // Do some fancy tests to see if ssl is being supported 
  4436.         if ( $force_recheck || false === ( $ssl = get_transient( 'jetpack_https_test' ) ) ) { 
  4437.             $message = ''; 
  4438.             if ( 'https' !== substr( JETPACK__API_BASE, 0, 5 ) ) { 
  4439.                 $ssl = 0; 
  4440.             } else { 
  4441.                 switch ( JETPACK_CLIENT__HTTPS ) { 
  4442.                     case 'NEVER': 
  4443.                         $ssl = 0; 
  4444.                         $message = __( 'JETPACK_CLIENT__HTTPS is set to NEVER', 'jetpack' ); 
  4445.                         break; 
  4446.                     case 'ALWAYS': 
  4447.                     case 'AUTO': 
  4448.                     default: 
  4449.                         $ssl = 1; 
  4450.                         break; 
  4451.                 } 
  4452.  
  4453.                 // If it's not 'NEVER', test to see 
  4454.                 if ( $ssl ) { 
  4455.                     if ( ! wp_http_supports( array( 'ssl' => true ) ) ) { 
  4456.                         $ssl = 0; 
  4457.                         $message = __( 'WordPress reports no SSL support', 'jetpack' ); 
  4458.                     } else { 
  4459.                         $response = wp_remote_get( JETPACK__API_BASE . 'test/1/' ); 
  4460.                         if ( is_wp_error( $response ) ) { 
  4461.                             $ssl = 0; 
  4462.                             $message = __( 'WordPress reports no SSL support', 'jetpack' ); 
  4463.                         } elseif ( 'OK' !== wp_remote_retrieve_body( $response ) ) { 
  4464.                             $ssl = 0; 
  4465.                             $message = __( 'Response was not OK: ', 'jetpack' ) . wp_remote_retrieve_body( $response ); 
  4466.                         } 
  4467.                     } 
  4468.                 } 
  4469.             } 
  4470.             set_transient( 'jetpack_https_test', $ssl, DAY_IN_SECONDS ); 
  4471.             set_transient( 'jetpack_https_test_message', $message, DAY_IN_SECONDS ); 
  4472.         } 
  4473.  
  4474.         return (bool) $ssl; 
  4475.     }

  4530.     /** 
  4531.      * Returns the Jetpack XML-RPC API 
  4532.      * 
  4533.      * @return string 
  4534.      */ 
  4535.     public static function xmlrpc_api_url() { 
  4536.         $base = preg_replace( '#(https?://[^?/]+)(/?.*)?$#', '\\1', JETPACK__API_BASE ); 
  4537.         return untrailingslashit( $base ) . '/xmlrpc.php'; 
  4538.     } 
  4539.  
  4540.     /** 
  4541.      * Creates two secret tokens and the end of life timestamp for them. 
  4542.      * 
  4543.      * Note these tokens are unique per call, NOT static per site for connecting. 
  4544.      * 
  4545.      * @since 2.6 
  4546.      * @return array 
  4547.      */ 
  4548.     public function generate_secrets( $action, $exp = 600 ) { 
  4549.         $secret = wp_generate_password( 32, false ) // secret_1 
  4550.                 . ':' . wp_generate_password( 32, false ) // secret_2 
  4551.                 . ':' . ( time() + $exp ) // eol ( End of Life ) 
  4552.                 . ':' . get_current_user_id(); // ties the secrets to the current user 
  4553.         Jetpack_Options::update_option( $action, $secret ); 
  4554.         return Jetpack_Options::get_option( $action ); 
  4555.     } 
  4556.  
  4557.     /** 
  4558.      * Builds the timeout limit for queries talking with the wpcom servers. 
  4559.      * 
  4560.      * Based on local php max_execution_time in php.ini 
  4561.      * 
  4562.      * @since 2.6 
  4563.      * @return int 
  4564.      **/ 
  4565.     public function get_remote_query_timeout_limit() { 
  4566.         $timeout = (int) ini_get( 'max_execution_time' ); 
  4567.         if ( ! $timeout ) // Ensure exec time set in php.ini 
  4568.                 $timeout = 30; 
  4569.         return intval( $timeout / 2 ); 
  4570.     } 
  4571.  
  4572.  
  4573.     /** 
  4574.      * Takes the response from the Jetpack register new site endpoint and 
  4575.      * verifies it worked properly. 
  4576.      * 
  4577.      * @since 2.6 
  4578.      * @return string|Jetpack_Error A JSON object on success or Jetpack_Error on failures 
  4579.      **/ 
  4580.     public function validate_remote_register_response( $response ) { 
  4581.       if ( is_wp_error( $response ) ) { 
  4582.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'register_http_request_failed', $response->get_error_message() ); 
  4583.         } 
  4584.  
  4585.         $code = wp_remote_retrieve_response_code( $response ); 
  4586.         $entity = wp_remote_retrieve_body( $response ); 
  4587.         if ( $entity ) 
  4588.             $registration_response = json_decode( $entity ); 
  4589.         else 
  4590.             $registration_response = false; 
  4591.  
  4592.         $code_type = intval( $code / 100 ); 
  4593.         if ( 5 == $code_type ) { 
  4594.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'wpcom_5??', sprintf( __( 'Error Details: %s', 'jetpack' ), $code ), $code ); 
  4595.         } elseif ( 408 == $code ) { 
  4596.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'wpcom_408', sprintf( __( 'Error Details: %s', 'jetpack' ), $code ), $code ); 
  4597.         } elseif ( ! empty( $registration_response->error ) ) { 
  4598.             if ( 'xml_rpc-32700' == $registration_response->error && ! function_exists( 'xml_parser_create' ) ) { 
  4599.                 $error_description = __( "PHP's XML extension is not available. Jetpack requires the XML extension to communicate with WordPress.com. Please contact your hosting provider to enable PHP's XML extension.", 'jetpack' ); 
  4600.             } else { 
  4601.                 $error_description = isset( $registration_response->error_description ) ? sprintf( __( 'Error Details: %s', 'jetpack' ), (string) $registration_response->error_description ) : ''; 
  4602.             } 
  4603.  
  4604.             return new Jetpack_Error( (string) $registration_response->error, $error_description, $code ); 
  4605.         } elseif ( 200 != $code ) { 
  4606.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'wpcom_bad_response', sprintf( __( 'Error Details: %s', 'jetpack' ), $code ), $code ); 
  4607.         } 
  4608.  
  4609.         // Jetpack ID error block 
  4610.         if ( empty( $registration_response->jetpack_id ) ) { 
  4611.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'jetpack_id', sprintf( __( 'Error Details: Jetpack ID is empty. Do not publicly post this error message! %s', 'jetpack' ), $entity ), $entity ); 
  4612.         } elseif ( ! is_scalar( $registration_response->jetpack_id ) ) { 
  4613.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'jetpack_id', sprintf( __( 'Error Details: Jetpack ID is not a scalar. Do not publicly post this error message! %s', 'jetpack' ) , $entity ), $entity ); 
  4614.         } elseif ( preg_match( '/[^0-9]/', $registration_response->jetpack_id ) ) { 
  4615.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'jetpack_id', sprintf( __( 'Error Details: Jetpack ID begins with a numeral. Do not publicly post this error message! %s', 'jetpack' ) , $entity ), $entity ); 
  4616.         } 
  4617.  
  4618.         return $registration_response; 
  4619.     } 
  4620.     /** 
  4621.      * @return bool|WP_Error 
  4622.      */ 
  4623.     public static function register() { 
  4624.         add_action( 'pre_update_jetpack_option_register', array( 'Jetpack_Options', 'delete_option' ) ); 
  4625.         $secrets = Jetpack::init()->generate_secrets( 'register' ); 
  4626.  
  4627.         @list( $secret_1, $secret_2, $secret_eol ) = explode( ':', $secrets ); 
  4628.         if ( empty( $secret_1 ) || empty( $secret_2 ) || empty( $secret_eol ) || $secret_eol < time() ) { 
  4629.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'missing_secrets' ); 
  4630.         } 
  4631.  
  4632.         $timeout = Jetpack::init()->get_remote_query_timeout_limit(); 
  4633.  
  4634.         $gmt_offset = get_option( 'gmt_offset' ); 
  4635.         if ( ! $gmt_offset ) { 
  4636.             $gmt_offset = 0; 
  4637.         } 
  4638.  
  4639.         $stats_options = get_option( 'stats_options' ); 
  4640.         $stats_id = isset($stats_options['blog_id']) ? $stats_options['blog_id'] : null; 
  4641.  
  4642.         $args = array( 
  4643.             'method' => 'POST',  
  4644.             'body' => array( 
  4645.                 'siteurl' => site_url(),  
  4646.                 'home' => home_url(),  
  4647.                 'gmt_offset' => $gmt_offset,  
  4648.                 'timezone_string' => (string) get_option( 'timezone_string' ),  
  4649.                 'site_name' => (string) get_option( 'blogname' ),  
  4650.                 'secret_1' => $secret_1,  
  4651.                 'secret_2' => $secret_2,  
  4652.                 'site_lang' => get_locale(),  
  4653.                 'timeout' => $timeout,  
  4654.                 'stats_id' => $stats_id,  
  4655.                 'state' => get_current_user_id(),  
  4656.  ),  
  4657.             'headers' => array( 
  4658.                 'Accept' => 'application/json',  
  4659.  ),  
  4660.             'timeout' => $timeout,  
  4661.  ); 
  4662.         $response = Jetpack_Client::_wp_remote_request( Jetpack::fix_url_for_bad_hosts( Jetpack::api_url( 'register' ) ), $args, true ); 
  4663.  
  4664.         // Make sure the response is valid and does not contain any Jetpack errors 
  4665.         $registration_details = Jetpack::init()->validate_remote_register_response( $response ); 
  4666.         if ( is_wp_error( $registration_details ) ) { 
  4667.             return $registration_details; 
  4668.         } elseif ( ! $registration_details ) { 
  4669.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'unknown_error', __( 'Unknown error registering your Jetpack site', 'jetpack' ), wp_remote_retrieve_response_code( $response ) ); 
  4670.         } 
  4671.  
  4672.         if ( empty( $registration_details->jetpack_secret ) || ! is_string( $registration_details->jetpack_secret ) ) { 
  4673.             return new Jetpack_Error( 'jetpack_secret', '', wp_remote_retrieve_response_code( $response ) ); 
  4674.         } 
  4675.  
  4676.         if ( isset( $registration_details->jetpack_public ) ) { 
  4677.             $jetpack_public = (int) $registration_details->jetpack_public; 
  4678.         } else { 
  4679.             $jetpack_public = false; 
  4680.         } 
  4681.  
  4682.         Jetpack_Options::update_options( 
  4683.             array( 
  4684.                 'id' => (int)    $registration_details->jetpack_id,  
  4685.                 'blog_token' => (string) $registration_details->jetpack_secret,  
  4686.                 'public' => $jetpack_public,  
  4687.  ) 
  4688.  ); 
  4689.  
  4690.         /** 
  4691.          * Fires when a site is registered on WordPress.com. 
  4692.          * 
  4693.          * @since 3.7.0 
  4694.          * 
  4695.          * @param int $json->jetpack_id Jetpack Blog ID. 
  4696.          * @param string $json->jetpack_secret Jetpack Blog Token. 
  4697.          * @param int|bool $jetpack_public Is the site public. 
  4698.          */ 
  4699.         do_action( 'jetpack_site_registered', $registration_details->jetpack_id, $registration_details->jetpack_secret, $jetpack_public ); 
  4700.  
  4701.         // Initialize Jump Start for the first and only time. 
  4702.         if ( ! Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'jumpstart' ) ) { 
  4703.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'jumpstart', 'new_connection' ); 
  4704.  
  4705.             $jetpack = Jetpack::init(); 
  4706.  
  4707.             $jetpack->stat( 'jumpstart', 'unique-views' ); 
  4708.             $jetpack->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  4709.         }; 
  4710.  
  4711.         return true; 
  4712.     } 
  4713.  
  4714.     /** 
  4715.      * If the db version is showing something other that what we've got now, bump it to current. 
  4716.      * 
  4717.      * @return bool: True if the option was incorrect and updated, false if nothing happened. 
  4718.      */ 
  4719.     public static function maybe_set_version_option() { 
  4720.         list( $version ) = explode( ':', Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'version' ) ); 
  4721.         if ( JETPACK__VERSION != $version ) { 
  4722.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'version', JETPACK__VERSION . ':' . time() ); 
  4723.  
  4724.             if ( version_compare( JETPACK__VERSION, $version, '>' ) ) { 
  4725.                 /** This action is documented in class.jetpack.php */ 
  4726.                 do_action( 'updating_jetpack_version', JETPACK__VERSION, $version ); 
  4727.             } 
  4728.  
  4729.             return true; 
  4730.         } 
  4731.         return false; 
  4732.     }

  4743.  
  4744.     /** 
  4745.      * Resets the saved authentication state in between testing requests. 
  4746.      */ 
  4747.     public function reset_saved_auth_state() { 
  4748.         $this->xmlrpc_verification = null; 
  4749.         $this->rest_authentication_status = null; 
  4750.     } 
  4751.  
  4752.     function verify_xml_rpc_signature() { 
  4753.         if ( $this->xmlrpc_verification ) { 
  4754.             return $this->xmlrpc_verification; 
  4755.         } 
  4756.  
  4757.         // It's not for us 
  4758.         if ( ! isset( $_GET['token'] ) || empty( $_GET['signature'] ) ) { 
  4759.             return false; 
  4760.         } 
  4761.  
  4762.         @list( $token_key, $version, $user_id ) = explode( ':', $_GET['token'] ); 
  4763.         if ( 
  4764.             empty( $token_key ) 
  4765.         || 
  4766.             empty( $version ) || strval( JETPACK__API_VERSION ) !== $version 
  4767.  ) { 
  4768.             return false; 
  4769.         } 
  4770.  
  4771.         if ( '0' === $user_id ) { 
  4772.             $token_type = 'blog'; 
  4773.             $user_id = 0; 
  4774.         } else { 
  4775.             $token_type = 'user'; 
  4776.             if ( empty( $user_id ) || ! ctype_digit( $user_id ) ) { 
  4777.                 return false; 
  4778.             } 
  4779.             $user_id = (int) $user_id; 
  4780.  
  4781.             $user = new WP_User( $user_id ); 
  4782.             if ( ! $user || ! $user->exists() ) { 
  4783.                 return false; 
  4784.             } 
  4785.         } 
  4786.  
  4787.         $token = Jetpack_Data::get_access_token( $user_id ); 
  4788.         if ( ! $token ) { 
  4789.             return false; 
  4790.         } 
  4791.  
  4792.         $token_check = "$token_key."; 
  4793.         if ( ! hash_equals( substr( $token->secret, 0, strlen( $token_check ) ), $token_check ) ) { 
  4794.             return false; 
  4795.         } 
  4796.  
  4797.         require_once JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'class.jetpack-signature.php'; 
  4798.  
  4799.         $jetpack_signature = new Jetpack_Signature( $token->secret, (int) Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'time_diff' ) ); 
  4800.         if ( isset( $_POST['_jetpack_is_multipart'] ) ) { 
  4801.             $post_data = $_POST; 
  4802.             $file_hashes = array(); 
  4803.             foreach ( $post_data as $post_data_key => $post_data_value ) { 
  4804.                 if ( 0 !== strpos( $post_data_key, '_jetpack_file_hmac_' ) ) { 
  4805.                     continue; 
  4806.                 } 
  4807.                 $post_data_key = substr( $post_data_key, strlen( '_jetpack_file_hmac_' ) ); 
  4808.                 $file_hashes[$post_data_key] = $post_data_value; 
  4809.             } 
  4810.  
  4811.             foreach ( $file_hashes as $post_data_key => $post_data_value ) { 
  4812.                 unset( $post_data["_jetpack_file_hmac_{$post_data_key}"] ); 
  4813.                 $post_data[$post_data_key] = $post_data_value; 
  4814.             } 
  4815.  
  4816.             ksort( $post_data ); 
  4817.  
  4818.             $body = http_build_query( stripslashes_deep( $post_data ) ); 
  4819.         } elseif ( is_null( $this->HTTP_RAW_POST_DATA ) ) { 
  4820.             $body = file_get_contents( 'php://input' ); 
  4821.         } else { 
  4822.             $body = null; 
  4823.         } 
  4824.  
  4825.         $signature = $jetpack_signature->sign_current_request( 
  4826.             array( 'body' => is_null( $body ) ? $this->HTTP_RAW_POST_DATA : $body, ) 
  4827.  ); 
  4828.  
  4829.         if ( ! $signature ) { 
  4830.             return false; 
  4831.         } else if ( is_wp_error( $signature ) ) { 
  4832.             return $signature; 
  4833.         } else if ( ! hash_equals( $signature, $_GET['signature'] ) ) { 
  4834.             return false; 
  4835.         } 
  4836.  
  4837.         $timestamp = (int) $_GET['timestamp']; 
  4838.         $nonce = stripslashes( (string) $_GET['nonce'] ); 
  4839.  
  4840.         if ( ! $this->add_nonce( $timestamp, $nonce ) ) { 
  4841.             return false; 
  4842.         } 
  4843.  
  4844.         $this->xmlrpc_verification = array( 
  4845.             'type' => $token_type,  
  4846.             'user_id' => $token->external_user_id,  
  4847.  ); 
  4848.  
  4849.         return $this->xmlrpc_verification; 
  4850.     } 
  4851.  
  4852.     /** 
  4853.      * Authenticates XML-RPC and other requests from the Jetpack Server 
  4854.      */ 
  4855.     function authenticate_jetpack( $user, $username, $password ) { 
  4856.         if ( is_a( $user, 'WP_User' ) ) { 
  4857.             return $user; 
  4858.         } 
  4859.  
  4860.         $token_details = $this->verify_xml_rpc_signature(); 
  4861.  
  4862.         if ( ! $token_details || is_wp_error( $token_details ) ) { 
  4863.             return $user; 
  4864.         } 
  4865.  
  4866.         if ( 'user' !== $token_details['type'] ) { 
  4867.             return $user; 
  4868.         } 
  4869.  
  4870.         if ( ! $token_details['user_id'] ) { 
  4871.             return $user; 
  4872.         } 
  4873.  
  4874.         nocache_headers(); 
  4875.  
  4876.         return new WP_User( $token_details['user_id'] ); 
  4877.     } 
  4878.  
  4879.     // Authenticates requests from Jetpack server to WP REST API endpoints. 
  4880.     // Uses the existing XMLRPC request signing implementation. 
  4881.     function wp_rest_authenticate( $user ) { 
  4882.         if ( ! empty( $user ) ) { 
  4883.             // Another authentication method is in effect. 
  4884.             return $user; 
  4885.         } 
  4886.  
  4887.         if ( ! isset( $_GET['_for'] ) || $_GET['_for'] !== 'jetpack' ) { 
  4888.             // Nothing to do for this authentication method. 
  4889.             return null; 
  4890.         } 
  4891.  
  4892.         if ( ! isset( $_GET['token'] ) && ! isset( $_GET['signature'] ) ) { 
  4893.             // Nothing to do for this authentication method. 
  4894.             return null; 
  4895.         } 
  4896.  
  4897.         // Ensure that we always have the request body available.  At this 
  4898.         // point, the WP REST API code to determine the request body has not 
  4899.         // run yet.  That code may try to read from 'php://input' later, but 
  4900.         // this can only be done once per request in PHP versions prior to 5.6. 
  4901.         // So we will go ahead and perform this read now if needed, and save 
  4902.         // the request body where both the Jetpack signature verification code 
  4903.         // and the WP REST API code can see it. 
  4904.         if ( ! isset( $GLOBALS['HTTP_RAW_POST_DATA'] ) ) { 
  4905.             $GLOBALS['HTTP_RAW_POST_DATA'] = file_get_contents( 'php://input' ); 
  4906.         } 
  4907.         $this->HTTP_RAW_POST_DATA = $GLOBALS['HTTP_RAW_POST_DATA']; 
  4908.  
  4909.         // Only support specific request parameters that have been tested and 
  4910.         // are known to work with signature verification.  A different method 
  4911.         // can be passed to the WP REST API via the '?_method=' parameter if 
  4912.         // needed. 
  4913.         if ( $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] !== 'GET' && $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] !== 'POST' ) { 
  4914.             $this->rest_authentication_status = new WP_Error( 
  4915.                 'rest_invalid_request',  
  4916.                 __( 'This request method is not supported.', 'jetpack' ),  
  4917.                 array( 'status' => 400 ) 
  4918.  ); 
  4919.             return null; 
  4920.         } 
  4921.         if ( $_SERVER['REQUEST_METHOD'] !== 'POST' && ! empty( $this->HTTP_RAW_POST_DATA ) ) { 
  4922.             $this->rest_authentication_status = new WP_Error( 
  4923.                 'rest_invalid_request',  
  4924.                 __( 'This request method does not support body parameters.', 'jetpack' ),  
  4925.                 array( 'status' => 400 ) 
  4926.  ); 
  4927.             return null; 
  4928.         } 
  4929.  
  4930.         if ( ! empty( $_SERVER['CONTENT_TYPE'] ) ) { 
  4931.             $content_type = $_SERVER['CONTENT_TYPE']; 
  4932.         } elseif ( ! empty( $_SERVER['HTTP_CONTENT_TYPE'] ) ) { 
  4933.             $content_type = $_SERVER['HTTP_CONTENT_TYPE']; 
  4934.         } 
  4935.  
  4936.         if ( 
  4937.             isset( $content_type ) && 
  4938.             $content_type !== 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' && 
  4939.             $content_type !== 'application/json' 
  4940.  ) { 
  4941.             $this->rest_authentication_status = new WP_Error( 
  4942.                 'rest_invalid_request',  
  4943.                 __( 'This Content-Type is not supported.', 'jetpack' ),  
  4944.                 array( 'status' => 400 ) 
  4945.  ); 
  4946.             return null; 
  4947.         } 
  4948.  
  4949.         $verified = $this->verify_xml_rpc_signature(); 
  4950.  
  4951.         if ( is_wp_error( $verified ) ) { 
  4952.             $this->rest_authentication_status = $verified; 
  4953.             return null; 
  4954.         } 
  4955.  
  4956.         if ( 
  4957.             $verified && 
  4958.             isset( $verified['type'] ) && 
  4959.             'user' === $verified['type'] && 
  4960.             ! empty( $verified['user_id'] ) 
  4961.  ) { 
  4962.             // Authentication successful. 
  4963.             $this->rest_authentication_status = true; 
  4964.             return $verified['user_id']; 
  4965.         } 
  4966.  
  4967.         // Something else went wrong.  Probably a signature error. 
  4968.         $this->rest_authentication_status = new WP_Error( 
  4969.             'rest_invalid_signature',  
  4970.             __( 'The request is not signed correctly.', 'jetpack' ),  
  4971.             array( 'status' => 400 ) 
  4972.  ); 
  4973.         return null; 
  4974.     } 
  4975.  
  4976.     /** 
  4977.      * Report authentication status to the WP REST API. 
  4978.      * 
  4979.      * @param  WP_Error|mixed $result Error from another authentication handler, null if we should handle it, or another value if not 
  4980.      * @return WP_Error|boolean|null {@see WP_JSON_Server::check_authentication} 
  4981.      */ 
  4982.     public function wp_rest_authentication_errors( $value ) { 
  4983.         if ( $value !== null ) { 
  4984.             return $value; 
  4985.         } 
  4986.         return $this->rest_authentication_status; 
  4987.     } 
  4988.  
  4989.     function add_nonce( $timestamp, $nonce ) { 
  4990.         global $wpdb; 
  4991.         static $nonces_used_this_request = array(); 
  4992.  
  4993.         if ( isset( $nonces_used_this_request["$timestamp:$nonce"] ) ) { 
  4994.             return $nonces_used_this_request["$timestamp:$nonce"]; 
  4995.         } 
  4996.  
  4997.         // This should always have gone through Jetpack_Signature::sign_request() first to check $timestamp an $nonce 
  4998.         $timestamp = (int) $timestamp; 
  4999.         $nonce = esc_sql( $nonce ); 
  5000.  
  5001.         // Raw query so we can avoid races: add_option will also update 
  5002.         $show_errors = $wpdb->show_errors( false ); 
  5003.  
  5004.         $old_nonce = $wpdb->get_row( 
  5005.             $wpdb->prepare( "SELECT * FROM `$wpdb->options` WHERE option_name = %s", "jetpack_nonce_{$timestamp}_{$nonce}" ) 
  5006.  ); 
  5007.  
  5008.         if ( is_null( $old_nonce ) ) { 
  5009.             $return = $wpdb->query( 
  5010.                 $wpdb->prepare( 
  5011.                     "INSERT INTO `$wpdb->options` (`option_name`, `option_value`, `autoload`) VALUES (%s, %s, %s)",  
  5012.                     "jetpack_nonce_{$timestamp}_{$nonce}",  
  5013.                     time(),  
  5014.                     'no' 
  5015.  ) 
  5016.  ); 
  5017.         } else { 
  5018.             $return = false; 
  5019.         } 
  5020.  
  5021.         $wpdb->show_errors( $show_errors ); 
  5022.  
  5023.         $nonces_used_this_request["$timestamp:$nonce"] = $return; 
  5024.  
  5025.         return $return; 
  5026.     } 
  5027.  
  5028.     /** 
  5029.      * In some setups, $HTTP_RAW_POST_DATA can be emptied during some IXR_Server paths since it is passed by reference to various methods. 
  5030.      * Capture it here so we can verify the signature later. 
  5031.      */ 
  5032.     function xmlrpc_methods( $methods ) {

  5044.     function jetpack_getOptions( $args ) {

  5046.

  5048.  
  5049.         $username = $args[1]; 
  5050.         $password = $args[2]; 
  5051.

  5053.             return $wp_xmlrpc_server->error; 
  5054.         }

  5073.  );

  5104.     public static function clean_nonces( $all = false ) { 
  5105.         global $wpdb; 
  5106.  
  5107.         $sql = "DELETE FROM `$wpdb->options` WHERE `option_name` LIKE %s"; 
  5108.         $sql_args = array( $wpdb->esc_like( 'jetpack_nonce_' ) . '%' ); 
  5109.  
  5110.         if ( true !== $all ) { 
  5111.             $sql .= ' AND CAST( `option_value` AS UNSIGNED ) < %d'; 
  5112.             $sql_args[] = time() - 3600; 
  5113.         } 
  5114.  
  5115.         $sql .= ' ORDER BY `option_id` LIMIT 100'; 
  5116.  
  5117.         $sql = $wpdb->prepare( $sql, $sql_args ); 
  5118.  
  5119.         for ( $i = 0; $i < 1000; $i++ ) { 
  5120.             if ( ! $wpdb->query( $sql ) ) { 
  5121.                 break; 
  5122.             } 
  5123.         } 
  5124.     } 
  5125.  
  5126.     /** 
  5127.      * State is passed via cookies from one request to the next, but never to subsequent requests. 
  5128.      * SET: state( $key, $value ); 
  5129.      * GET: $value = state( $key ); 
  5130.      * 
  5131.      * @param string $key 
  5132.      * @param string $value 
  5133.      * @param bool $restate private 
  5134.      */ 
  5135.     public static function state( $key = null, $value = null, $restate = false ) { 
  5136.         static $state = array(); 
  5137.         static $path, $domain; 
  5138.         if ( ! isset( $path ) ) { 
  5139.             require_once( ABSPATH . 'wp-admin/includes/plugin.php' ); 
  5140.             $admin_url = Jetpack::admin_url(); 
  5141.             $bits = parse_url( $admin_url ); 
  5142.  
  5143.             if ( is_array( $bits ) ) { 
  5144.                 $path = ( isset( $bits['path'] ) ) ? dirname( $bits['path'] ) : null; 
  5145.                 $domain = ( isset( $bits['host'] ) ) ? $bits['host'] : null; 
  5146.             } else { 
  5147.                 $path = $domain = null; 
  5148.             } 
  5149.         } 
  5150.  
  5151.         // Extract state from cookies and delete cookies 
  5152.         if ( isset( $_COOKIE[ 'jetpackState' ] ) && is_array( $_COOKIE[ 'jetpackState' ] ) ) { 
  5153.             $yum = $_COOKIE[ 'jetpackState' ]; 
  5154.             unset( $_COOKIE[ 'jetpackState' ] ); 
  5155.             foreach ( $yum as $k => $v ) { 
  5156.                 if ( strlen( $v ) ) 
  5157.                     $state[ $k ] = $v; 
  5158.                 setcookie( "jetpackState[$k]", false, 0, $path, $domain ); 
  5159.             } 
  5160.         } 
  5161.  
  5162.         if ( $restate ) { 
  5163.             foreach ( $state as $k => $v ) { 
  5164.                 setcookie( "jetpackState[$k]", $v, 0, $path, $domain ); 
  5165.             } 
  5166.             return; 
  5167.         } 
  5168.  
  5169.         // Get a state variable 
  5170.         if ( isset( $key ) && ! isset( $value ) ) { 
  5171.             if ( array_key_exists( $key, $state ) ) 
  5172.                 return $state[ $key ]; 
  5173.             return null; 
  5174.         } 
  5175.  
  5176.         // Set a state variable 
  5177.         if ( isset ( $key ) && isset( $value ) ) { 
  5178.             if( is_array( $value ) && isset( $value[0] ) ) { 
  5179.                 $value = $value[0]; 
  5180.             } 
  5181.             $state[ $key ] = $value; 
  5182.             setcookie( "jetpackState[$key]", $value, 0, $path, $domain ); 
  5183.         } 
  5184.     } 
  5185.  
  5186.     public static function restate() { 
  5187.         Jetpack::state( null, null, true ); 
  5188.     } 
  5189.  
  5190.     public static function check_privacy( $file ) { 
  5191.         static $is_site_publicly_accessible = null; 
  5192.  
  5193.         if ( is_null( $is_site_publicly_accessible ) ) { 
  5194.             $is_site_publicly_accessible = false; 
  5195.  
  5196.             Jetpack::load_xml_rpc_client(); 
  5197.             $rpc = new Jetpack_IXR_Client(); 
  5198.  
  5199.             $success = $rpc->query( 'jetpack.isSitePubliclyAccessible', home_url() ); 
  5200.             if ( $success ) { 
  5201.                 $response = $rpc->getResponse(); 
  5202.                 if ( $response ) { 
  5203.                     $is_site_publicly_accessible = true; 
  5204.                 } 
  5205.             } 
  5206.  
  5207.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'public', (int) $is_site_publicly_accessible ); 
  5208.         } 
  5209.  
  5210.         if ( $is_site_publicly_accessible ) { 
  5211.             return; 
  5212.         } 
  5213.  
  5214.         $module_slug = self::get_module_slug( $file ); 
  5215.  
  5216.         $privacy_checks = Jetpack::state( 'privacy_checks' ); 
  5217.         if ( ! $privacy_checks ) { 
  5218.             $privacy_checks = $module_slug; 
  5219.         } else { 
  5220.             $privacy_checks .= ", $module_slug"; 
  5221.         } 
  5222.  
  5223.         Jetpack::state( 'privacy_checks', $privacy_checks ); 
  5224.     } 
  5225.  
  5226.     /** 
  5227.      * Helper method for multicall XMLRPC. 
  5228.      */ 
  5229.     public static function xmlrpc_async_call() { 
  5230.         global $blog_id; 
  5231.         static $clients = array(); 
  5232.  
  5233.         $client_blog_id = is_multisite() ? $blog_id : 0; 
  5234.  
  5235.         if ( ! isset( $clients[$client_blog_id] ) ) { 
  5236.             Jetpack::load_xml_rpc_client(); 
  5237.             $clients[$client_blog_id] = new Jetpack_IXR_ClientMulticall( array( 'user_id' => JETPACK_MASTER_USER, ) ); 
  5238.             if ( function_exists( 'ignore_user_abort' ) ) { 
  5239.                 ignore_user_abort( true ); 
  5240.             } 
  5241.             add_action( 'shutdown', array( 'Jetpack', 'xmlrpc_async_call' ) ); 
  5242.         } 
  5243.  
  5244.         $args = func_get_args(); 
  5245.  
  5246.         if ( ! empty( $args[0] ) ) { 
  5247.             call_user_func_array( array( $clients[$client_blog_id], 'addCall' ), $args ); 
  5248.         } elseif ( is_multisite() ) { 
  5249.             foreach ( $clients as $client_blog_id => $client ) { 
  5250.                 if ( ! $client_blog_id || empty( $client->calls ) ) { 
  5251.                     continue; 
  5252.                 } 
  5253.  
  5254.                 $switch_success = switch_to_blog( $client_blog_id, true ); 
  5255.                 if ( ! $switch_success ) { 
  5256.                     continue; 
  5257.                 } 
  5258.  
  5259.                 flush(); 
  5260.                 $client->query(); 
  5261.  
  5262.                 restore_current_blog(); 
  5263.             } 
  5264.         } else { 
  5265.             if ( isset( $clients[0] ) && ! empty( $clients[0]->calls ) ) { 
  5266.                 flush(); 
  5267.                 $clients[0]->query(); 
  5268.             } 
  5269.         } 
  5270.     } 
  5271.  
  5272.     public static function staticize_subdomain( $url ) { 
  5273.  
  5274.         // Extract hostname from URL 
  5275.         $host = parse_url( $url, PHP_URL_HOST ); 
  5276.  
  5277.         // Explode hostname on '.' 
  5278.         $exploded_host = explode( '.', $host ); 
  5279.  
  5280.         // Retrieve the name and TLD 
  5281.         if ( count( $exploded_host ) > 1 ) { 
  5282.             $name = $exploded_host[ count( $exploded_host ) - 2 ]; 
  5283.             $tld = $exploded_host[ count( $exploded_host ) - 1 ]; 
  5284.             // Rebuild domain excluding subdomains 
  5285.             $domain = $name . '.' . $tld; 
  5286.         } else { 
  5287.             $domain = $host; 
  5288.         } 
  5289.         // Array of Automattic domains 
  5290.         $domain_whitelist = array( 'wordpress.com', 'wp.com' ); 
  5291.  
  5292.         // Return $url if not an Automattic domain 
  5293.         if ( ! in_array( $domain, $domain_whitelist ) ) { 
  5294.             return $url; 
  5295.         } 
  5296.  
  5297.         if ( is_ssl() ) { 
  5298.             return preg_replace( '|https?://[^/]++/|', 'https://s-ssl.wordpress.com/', $url ); 
  5299.         } 
  5300.  
  5301.         srand( crc32( basename( $url ) ) ); 
  5302.         $static_counter = rand( 0, 2 ); 
  5303.         srand(); // this resets everything that relies on this, like array_rand() and shuffle() 
  5304.  
  5305.         return preg_replace( '|://[^/]+?/|', "://s$static_counter.wp.com/", $url ); 
  5306.     }
