  5310.     /** 
  5311.      * Handles the login action for Authorizing the JSON API 
  5312.      */ 
  5313.     function login_form_json_api_authorization() { 
  5314.         $this->verify_json_api_authorization_request(); 
  5315.  
  5316.         add_action( 'wp_login', array( &$this, 'store_json_api_authorization_token' ), 10, 2 ); 
  5317.  
  5318.         add_action( 'login_message', array( &$this, 'login_message_json_api_authorization' ) ); 
  5319.         add_action( 'login_form', array( &$this, 'preserve_action_in_login_form_for_json_api_authorization' ) ); 
  5320.         add_filter( 'site_url', array( &$this, 'post_login_form_to_signed_url' ), 10, 3 ); 
  5321.     } 
  5322.  
  5323.     // Make sure the login form is POSTed to the signed URL so we can reverify the request 
  5324.     function post_login_form_to_signed_url( $url, $path, $scheme ) { 
  5325.         if ( 'wp-login.php' !== $path || ( 'login_post' !== $scheme && 'login' !== $scheme ) ) { 
  5326.             return $url; 
  5327.         } 
  5328.  
  5329.         $parsed_url = parse_url( $url ); 
  5330.         $url = strtok( $url, '?' ); 
  5331.         $url = "$url?{$_SERVER['QUERY_STRING']}"; 
  5332.         if ( ! empty( $parsed_url['query'] ) ) 
  5333.             $url .= "&{$parsed_url['query']}"; 
  5334.  
  5335.         return $url; 
  5336.     } 
  5337.  
  5338.     // Make sure the POSTed request is handled by the same action 
  5339.     function preserve_action_in_login_form_for_json_api_authorization() { 
  5340.         echo "<input type='hidden' name='action' value='jetpack_json_api_authorization' />\n"; 
  5341.         echo "<input type='hidden' name='jetpack_json_api_original_query' value='" . esc_url( set_url_scheme( $_SERVER['HTTP_HOST'] . $_SERVER['REQUEST_URI'] ) ) . "' />\n"; 
  5342.     } 
  5343.  
  5344.     // If someone logs in to approve API access, store the Access Code in usermeta 
  5345.     function store_json_api_authorization_token( $user_login, $user ) { 
  5346.         add_filter( 'login_redirect', array( &$this, 'add_token_to_login_redirect_json_api_authorization' ), 10, 3 ); 
  5347.         add_filter( 'allowed_redirect_hosts', array( &$this, 'allow_wpcom_public_api_domain' ) ); 
  5348.         $token = wp_generate_password( 32, false ); 
  5349.         update_user_meta( $user->ID, 'jetpack_json_api_' . $this->json_api_authorization_request['client_id'], $token ); 
  5350.     } 
  5351.  
  5352.     // Add public-api.wordpress.com to the safe redirect whitelist - only added when someone allows API access 
  5353.     function allow_wpcom_public_api_domain( $domains ) { 
  5354.         $domains[] = 'public-api.wordpress.com'; 
  5355.         return $domains; 
  5356.     } 
  5357.  
  5358.     // Add the Access Code details to the public-api.wordpress.com redirect 
  5359.     function add_token_to_login_redirect_json_api_authorization( $redirect_to, $original_redirect_to, $user ) { 
  5360.         return add_query_arg( 
  5361.             urlencode_deep( 
  5362.                 array( 
  5363.                     'jetpack-code' => get_user_meta( $user->ID, 'jetpack_json_api_' . $this->json_api_authorization_request['client_id'], true ),  
  5364.                     'jetpack-user-id' => (int) $user->ID,  
  5365.                     'jetpack-state' => $this->json_api_authorization_request['state'],  
  5366.  ) 
  5367.  ),  
  5368.             $redirect_to 
  5369.  ); 
  5370.     } 
  5371.  
  5372.  
  5373.     /** 
  5374.      * Verifies the request by checking the signature 
  5375.      * 
  5376.      * @since 4.6.0 Method was updated to use `$_REQUEST` instead of `$_GET` and `$_POST`. Method also updated to allow 
  5377.      * passing in an `$environment` argument that overrides `$_REQUEST`. This was useful for integrating with SSO. 
  5378.      * 
  5379.      * @param null|array $environment 
  5380.      */ 
  5381.     function verify_json_api_authorization_request( $environment = null ) { 
  5382.         require_once JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'class.jetpack-signature.php'; 
  5383.  
  5384.         $environment = is_null( $environment ) 
  5385.             ? $_REQUEST 
  5386.             : $environment; 
  5387.  
  5388.         list( $envToken, $envVersion, $envUserId ) = explode( ':', $environment['token'] ); 
  5389.         $token = Jetpack_Data::get_access_token( $envUserId ); 
  5390.         if ( ! $token || empty( $token->secret ) ) { 
  5391.             wp_die( __( 'You must connect your Jetpack plugin to WordPress.com to use this feature.' , 'jetpack' ) ); 
  5392.         } 
  5393.  
  5394.         $die_error = __( 'Someone may be trying to trick you into giving them access to your site.  Or it could be you just encountered a bug :).  Either way, please close this window.', 'jetpack' ); 
  5395.  
  5396.         $jetpack_signature = new Jetpack_Signature( $token->secret, (int) Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'time_diff' ) ); 
  5397.  
  5398.         if ( isset( $environment['jetpack_json_api_original_query'] ) ) { 
  5399.             $signature = $jetpack_signature->sign_request( 
  5400.                 $environment['token'],  
  5401.                 $environment['timestamp'],  
  5402.                 $environment['nonce'],  
  5403.                 '',  
  5404.                 'GET',  
  5405.                 $environment['jetpack_json_api_original_query'],  
  5406.                 null,  
  5407.                 true 
  5408.  ); 
  5409.         } else { 
  5410.             $signature = $jetpack_signature->sign_current_request( array( 'body' => null, 'method' => 'GET' ) ); 
  5411.         } 
  5412.  
  5413.         if ( ! $signature ) { 
  5414.             wp_die( $die_error ); 
  5415.         } else if ( is_wp_error( $signature ) ) { 
  5416.             wp_die( $die_error ); 
  5417.         } else if ( ! hash_equals( $signature, $environment['signature'] ) ) { 
  5418.             if ( is_ssl() ) { 
  5419.                 // If we signed an HTTP request on the Jetpack Servers, but got redirected to HTTPS by the local blog, check the HTTP signature as well 
  5420.                 $signature = $jetpack_signature->sign_current_request( array( 'scheme' => 'http', 'body' => null, 'method' => 'GET' ) ); 
  5421.                 if ( ! $signature || is_wp_error( $signature ) || ! hash_equals( $signature, $environment['signature'] ) ) { 
  5422.                     wp_die( $die_error ); 
  5423.                 } 
  5424.             } else { 
  5425.                 wp_die( $die_error ); 
  5426.             } 
  5427.         } 
  5428.  
  5429.         $timestamp = (int) $environment['timestamp']; 
  5430.         $nonce = stripslashes( (string) $environment['nonce'] ); 
  5431.  
  5432.         if ( ! $this->add_nonce( $timestamp, $nonce ) ) { 
  5433.             // De-nonce the nonce, at least for 5 minutes. 
  5434.             // We have to reuse this nonce at least once (used the first time when the initial request is made, used a second time when the login form is POSTed) 
  5435.             $old_nonce_time = get_option( "jetpack_nonce_{$timestamp}_{$nonce}" ); 
  5436.             if ( $old_nonce_time < time() - 300 ) { 
  5437.                 wp_die( __( 'The authorization process expired.  Please go back and try again.' , 'jetpack' ) ); 
  5438.             } 
  5439.         } 
  5440.  
  5441.         $data = json_decode( base64_decode( stripslashes( $environment['data'] ) ) ); 
  5442.         $data_filters = array( 
  5443.             'state' => 'opaque',  
  5444.             'client_id' => 'int',  
  5445.             'client_title' => 'string',  
  5446.             'client_image' => 'url',  
  5447.  ); 
  5448.  
  5449.         foreach ( $data_filters as $key => $sanitation ) { 
  5450.             if ( ! isset( $data->$key ) ) { 
  5451.                 wp_die( $die_error ); 
  5452.             } 
  5453.  
  5454.             switch ( $sanitation ) { 
  5455.             case 'int' : 
  5456.                 $this->json_api_authorization_request[$key] = (int) $data->$key; 
  5457.                 break; 
  5458.             case 'opaque' : 
  5459.                 $this->json_api_authorization_request[$key] = (string) $data->$key; 
  5460.                 break; 
  5461.             case 'string' : 
  5462.                 $this->json_api_authorization_request[$key] = wp_kses( (string) $data->$key, array() ); 
  5463.                 break; 
  5464.             case 'url' : 
  5465.                 $this->json_api_authorization_request[$key] = esc_url_raw( (string) $data->$key ); 
  5466.                 break; 
  5467.             } 
  5468.         } 
  5469.  
  5470.         if ( empty( $this->json_api_authorization_request['client_id'] ) ) { 
  5471.             wp_die( $die_error ); 
  5472.         } 
  5473.     } 
  5474.  
  5475.     function login_message_json_api_authorization( $message ) { 
  5476.         return '<p class="message">' . sprintf( 
  5477.             esc_html__( '%s wants to access your site’s data.  Log in to authorize that access.' , 'jetpack' ),  
  5478.             '<strong>' . esc_html( $this->json_api_authorization_request['client_title'] ) . '</strong>' 
  5479.  ) . '<img src="' . esc_url( $this->json_api_authorization_request['client_image'] ) . '" /></p>'; 
  5480.     }

  5487.         /**

  5489.          *

  5491.          *

  5494.         return apply_filters( 'jetpack_content_width', $content_width ); 
  5495.     }

  5497.     /**

  5502.      * @return array An associative array of the option values as stored in the WordPress.com Mirror Site

  5504.     public function get_cloud_site_options( $option_names ) { 
  5505.         $option_names = array_filter( (array) $option_names, 'is_string' );

  5509.         $xml->query( 'jetpack.fetchSiteOptions', $option_names );

  5521.     /** 
  5522.      * Checks if the site is currently in an identity crisis. 
  5523.      * 
  5524.      * @return array|bool Array of options that are in a crisis, or false if everything is OK. 
  5525.      */ 
  5526.     public static function check_identity_crisis() { 
  5527.         if ( ! Jetpack::is_active() || Jetpack::is_development_mode() || ! self::validate_sync_error_idc_option() ) { 
  5528.             return false; 
  5529.         } 
  5530.  
  5531.         return Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'sync_error_idc' ); 
  5532.     } 
  5533.  
  5534.     /** 
  5535.      * Checks whether the home and siteurl specifically are whitelisted 
  5536.      * Written so that we don't have re-check $key and $value params every time 
  5537.      * we want to check if this site is whitelisted, for example in footer.php 
  5538.      * 
  5539.      * @since  3.8.0 
  5540.      * @return bool True = already whitelisted False = not whitelisted 
  5541.      */ 
  5542.     public static function is_staging_site() { 
  5543.         $is_staging = false; 
  5544.  
  5545.         $known_staging = array( 
  5546.             'urls' => array( 
  5547.                 '#\.staging\.wpengine\.com$#i', // WP Engine 
  5548.                 '#\.staging\.kinsta\.com$#i', // Kinsta.com 
  5549.  ),  
  5550.             'constants' => array( 
  5551.                 'IS_WPE_SNAPSHOT', // WP Engine 
  5552.                 'KINSTA_DEV_ENV', // Kinsta.com 
  5553.                 'WPSTAGECOACH_STAGING', // WP Stagecoach 
  5554.                 'JETPACK_STAGING_MODE', // Generic 
  5555.  ) 
  5556.  ); 
  5557.         /** 
  5558.          * Filters the flags of known staging sites. 
  5559.          * 
  5560.          * @since 3.9.0 
  5561.          * 
  5562.          * @param array $known_staging { 
  5563.          *     An array of arrays that each are used to check if the current site is staging. 
  5564.          *     @type array $urls      URLs of staging sites in regex to check against site_url. 
  5565.          *     @type array $constants PHP constants of known staging/developement environments. 
  5566.          *  } 
  5567.          */ 
  5568.         $known_staging = apply_filters( 'jetpack_known_staging', $known_staging ); 
  5569.  
  5570.         if ( isset( $known_staging['urls'] ) ) { 
  5571.             foreach ( $known_staging['urls'] as $url ) { 
  5572.                 if ( preg_match( $url, site_url() ) ) { 
  5573.                     $is_staging = true; 
  5574.                     break; 
  5575.                 } 
  5576.             } 
  5577.         } 
  5578.  
  5579.         if ( isset( $known_staging['constants'] ) ) { 
  5580.             foreach ( $known_staging['constants'] as $constant ) { 
  5581.                 if ( defined( $constant ) && constant( $constant ) ) { 
  5582.                     $is_staging = true; 
  5583.                 } 
  5584.             } 
  5585.         } 
  5586.  
  5587.         // Last, let's check if sync is erroring due to an IDC. If so, set the site to staging mode. 
  5588.         if ( ! $is_staging && self::validate_sync_error_idc_option() ) { 
  5589.             $is_staging = true; 
  5590.         } 
  5591.  
  5592.         /** 
  5593.          * Filters is_staging_site check. 
  5594.          * 
  5595.          * @since 3.9.0 
  5596.          * 
  5597.          * @param bool $is_staging If the current site is a staging site. 
  5598.          */ 
  5599.         return apply_filters( 'jetpack_is_staging_site', $is_staging ); 
  5600.     } 
  5601.  
  5602.     /** 
  5603.      * Checks whether the sync_error_idc option is valid or not, and if not, will do cleanup. 
  5604.      * 
  5605.      * @return bool 
  5606.      */ 
  5607.     public static function validate_sync_error_idc_option() { 
  5608.         $is_valid = false; 
  5609.  
  5610.         $idc_allowed = get_transient( 'jetpack_idc_allowed' ); 
  5611.         if ( false === $idc_allowed ) { 
  5612.             $response = wp_remote_get( 'https://jetpack.com/is-idc-allowed/' ); 
  5613.             if ( 200 === (int) wp_remote_retrieve_response_code( $response ) ) { 
  5614.                 $json = json_decode( wp_remote_retrieve_body( $response ) ); 
  5615.                 $idc_allowed = isset( $json, $json->result ) && $json->result ? '1' : '0'; 
  5616.                 $transient_duration = HOUR_IN_SECONDS; 
  5617.             } else { 
  5618.                 // If the request failed for some reason, then assume IDC is allowed and set shorter transient. 
  5619.                 $idc_allowed = '1'; 
  5620.                 $transient_duration = 5 * MINUTE_IN_SECONDS; 
  5621.             } 
  5622.  
  5623.             set_transient( 'jetpack_idc_allowed', $idc_allowed, $transient_duration ); 
  5624.         } 
  5625.  
  5626.         // Is the site opted in and does the stored sync_error_idc option match what we now generate? 
  5627.         $sync_error = Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'sync_error_idc' ); 
  5628.         $local_options = self::get_sync_error_idc_option(); 
  5629.         if ( $idc_allowed && $sync_error && self::sync_idc_optin() ) { 
  5630.             if ( $sync_error['home'] === $local_options['home'] && $sync_error['siteurl'] === $local_options['siteurl'] ) { 
  5631.                 $is_valid = true; 
  5632.             } 
  5633.         } 
  5634.  
  5635.         /** 
  5636.          * Filters whether the sync_error_idc option is valid. 
  5637.          * 
  5638.          * @since 4.4.0 
  5639.          * 
  5640.          * @param bool $is_valid If the sync_error_idc is valid or not. 
  5641.          */ 
  5642.         $is_valid = (bool) apply_filters( 'jetpack_sync_error_idc_validation', $is_valid ); 
  5643.  
  5644.         if ( ! $idc_allowed || ( ! $is_valid && $sync_error ) ) { 
  5645.             // Since the option exists, and did not validate, delete it 
  5646.             Jetpack_Options::delete_option( 'sync_error_idc' ); 
  5647.         } 
  5648.  
  5649.         return $is_valid; 
  5650.     } 
  5651.  
  5652.     /** 
  5653.      * Normalizes a url by doing three things: 
  5654.      *  - Strips protocol 
  5655.      *  - Strips www 
  5656.      *  - Adds a trailing slash 
  5657.      * 
  5658.      * @since 4.4.0 
  5659.      * @param string $url 
  5660.      * @return WP_Error|string 
  5661.      */ 
  5662.     public static function normalize_url_protocol_agnostic( $url ) { 
  5663.         $parsed_url = wp_parse_url( trailingslashit( esc_url_raw( $url ) ) ); 
  5664.         if ( ! $parsed_url ) { 
  5665.             return new WP_Error( 'cannot_parse_url', sprintf( esc_html__( 'Cannot parse URL %s', 'jetpack' ), $url ) ); 
  5666.         } 
  5667.  
  5668.         // Strip www and protocols 
  5669.         $url = preg_replace( '/^www\./i', '', $parsed_url['host'] . $parsed_url['path'] ); 
  5670.         return $url; 
  5671.     } 
  5672.  
  5673.     /** 
  5674.      * Gets the value that is to be saved in the jetpack_sync_error_idc option. 
  5675.      * 
  5676.      * @since 4.4.0 
  5677.      * 
  5678.      * @param array $response 
  5679.      * @return array Array of the local urls, wpcom urls, and error code 
  5680.      */ 
  5681.     public static function get_sync_error_idc_option( $response = array() ) { 
  5682.         $local_options = array( 
  5683.             'home' => get_home_url(),  
  5684.             'siteurl' => get_site_url(),  
  5685.  ); 
  5686.  
  5687.         $options = array_merge( $local_options, $response ); 
  5688.  
  5689.         $returned_values = array(); 
  5690.         foreach( $options as $key => $option ) { 
  5691.             if ( 'error_code' === $key ) { 
  5692.                 $returned_values[ $key ] = $option; 
  5693.                 continue; 
  5694.             } 
  5695.  
  5696.             if ( is_wp_error( $normalized_url = self::normalize_url_protocol_agnostic( $option ) ) ) { 
  5697.                 continue; 
  5698.             } 
  5699.  
  5700.             $returned_values[ $key ] = $normalized_url; 
  5701.         } 
  5702.  
  5703.         return $returned_values; 
  5704.     } 
  5705.  
  5706.     /** 
  5707.      * Returns the value of the jetpack_sync_idc_optin filter, or constant. 
  5708.      * If set to true, the site will be put into staging mode. 
  5709.      * 
  5710.      * @since 4.3.2 
  5711.      * @return bool 
  5712.      */ 
  5713.     public static function sync_idc_optin() { 
  5714.         if ( Jetpack_Constants::is_defined( 'JETPACK_SYNC_IDC_OPTIN' ) ) { 
  5715.             $default = Jetpack_Constants::get_constant( 'JETPACK_SYNC_IDC_OPTIN' ); 
  5716.         } else { 
  5717.             $default = ! Jetpack_Constants::is_defined( 'SUNRISE' ) && ! is_multisite(); 
  5718.         } 
  5719.  
  5720.         /** 
  5721.          * Allows sites to optin to IDC mitigation which blocks the site from syncing to WordPress.com when the home 
  5722.          * URL or site URL do not match what WordPress.com expects. The default value is either false, or the value of 
  5723.          * JETPACK_SYNC_IDC_OPTIN constant if set. 
  5724.          * 
  5725.          * @since 4.3.2 
  5726.          * 
  5727.          * @param bool $default Whether the site is opted in to IDC mitigation. 
  5728.          */ 
  5729.         return (bool) apply_filters( 'jetpack_sync_idc_optin', $default ); 
  5730.     } 
  5731.  
  5732.     /** 
  5733.      * Maybe Use a .min.css stylesheet, maybe not. 
  5734.      * 
  5735.      * Hooks onto `plugins_url` filter at priority 1, and accepts all 3 args. 
  5736.      */ 
  5737.     public static function maybe_min_asset( $url, $path, $plugin ) { 
  5738.         // Short out on things trying to find actual paths. 
  5739.         if ( ! $path || empty( $plugin ) ) { 
  5740.             return $url; 
  5741.         } 
  5742.  
  5743.         // Strip out the abspath. 
  5744.         $base = dirname( plugin_basename( $plugin ) ); 
  5745.  
  5746.         // Short out on non-Jetpack assets. 
  5747.         if ( 'jetpack/' !== substr( $base, 0, 8 ) ) { 
  5748.             return $url; 
  5749.         } 
  5750.  
  5751.         // File name parsing. 
  5752.         $file = "{$base}/{$path}"; 
  5753.         $full_path = JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . substr( $file, 8 ); 
  5754.         $file_name = substr( $full_path, strrpos( $full_path, '/' ) + 1 ); 
  5755.         $file_name_parts_r = array_reverse( explode( '.', $file_name ) ); 
  5756.         $extension = array_shift( $file_name_parts_r ); 
  5757.  
  5758.         if ( in_array( strtolower( $extension ), array( 'css', 'js' ) ) ) { 
  5759.             // Already pointing at the minified version. 
  5760.             if ( 'min' === $file_name_parts_r[0] ) { 
  5761.                 return $url; 
  5762.             } 
  5763.  
  5764.             $min_full_path = preg_replace( "#\.{$extension}$#", ".min.{$extension}", $full_path ); 
  5765.             if ( file_exists( $min_full_path ) ) { 
  5766.                 $url = preg_replace( "#\.{$extension}$#", ".min.{$extension}", $url ); 
  5767.             } 
  5768.         } 
  5769.  
  5770.         return $url; 
  5771.     } 
  5772.  
  5773.     /** 
  5774.      * Maybe inlines a stylesheet. 
  5775.      * 
  5776.      * If you'd like to inline a stylesheet instead of printing a link to it,  
  5777.      * wp_style_add_data( 'handle', 'jetpack-inline', true ); 
  5778.      * 
  5779.      * Attached to `style_loader_tag` filter. 
  5780.      * 
  5781.      * @param string $tag The tag that would link to the external asset. 
  5782.      * @param string $handle The registered handle of the script in question. 
  5783.      * 
  5784.      * @return string 
  5785.      */ 
  5786.     public static function maybe_inline_style( $tag, $handle ) { 
  5787.         global $wp_styles; 
  5788.         $item = $wp_styles->registered[ $handle ]; 
  5789.  
  5790.         if ( ! isset( $item->extra['jetpack-inline'] ) || ! $item->extra['jetpack-inline'] ) { 
  5791.             return $tag; 
  5792.         } 
  5793.  
  5794.         if ( preg_match( '# href=\'([^\']+)\' #i', $tag, $matches ) ) { 
  5795.             $href = $matches[1]; 
  5796.             // Strip off query string 
  5797.             if ( $pos = strpos( $href, '?' ) ) { 
  5798.                 $href = substr( $href, 0, $pos ); 
  5799.             } 
  5800.             // Strip off fragment 
  5801.             if ( $pos = strpos( $href, '#' ) ) { 
  5802.                 $href = substr( $href, 0, $pos ); 
  5803.             } 
  5804.         } else { 
  5805.             return $tag; 
  5806.         } 
  5807.  
  5808.         $plugins_dir = plugin_dir_url( JETPACK__PLUGIN_FILE ); 
  5809.         if ( $plugins_dir !== substr( $href, 0, strlen( $plugins_dir ) ) ) { 
  5810.             return $tag; 
  5811.         } 
  5812.  
  5813.         // If this stylesheet has a RTL version, and the RTL version replaces normal... 
  5814.         if ( isset( $item->extra['rtl'] ) && 'replace' === $item->extra['rtl'] && is_rtl() ) { 
  5815.             // And this isn't the pass that actually deals with the RTL version... 
  5816.             if ( false === strpos( $tag, " id='$handle-rtl-css' " ) ) { 
  5817.                 // Short out, as the RTL version will deal with it in a moment. 
  5818.                 return $tag; 
  5819.             } 
  5820.         } 
  5821.  
  5822.         $file = JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . substr( $href, strlen( $plugins_dir ) ); 
  5823.         $css = Jetpack::absolutize_css_urls( file_get_contents( $file ), $href ); 
  5824.         if ( $css ) { 
  5825.             $tag = "<!-- Inline {$item->handle} -->\r\n"; 
  5826.             if ( empty( $item->extra['after'] ) ) { 
  5827.                 wp_add_inline_style( $handle, $css ); 
  5828.             } else { 
  5829.                 array_unshift( $item->extra['after'], $css ); 
  5830.                 wp_style_add_data( $handle, 'after', $item->extra['after'] ); 
  5831.             } 
  5832.         } 
  5833.  
  5834.         return $tag; 
  5835.     } 
  5836.  
  5837.     /** 
  5838.      * Loads a view file from the views 
  5839.      * 
  5840.      * Data passed in with the $data parameter will be available in the 
  5841.      * template file as $data['value'] 
  5842.      * 
  5843.      * @param string $template - Template file to load 
  5844.      * @param array $data - Any data to pass along to the template 
  5845.      * @return boolean - If template file was found 
  5846.      **/ 
  5847.     public function load_view( $template, $data = array() ) { 
  5848.         $views_dir = JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'views/'; 
  5849.  
  5850.         if( file_exists( $views_dir . $template ) ) { 
  5851.             require_once( $views_dir . $template ); 
  5852.             return true; 
  5853.         } 
  5854.  
  5855.         error_log( "Jetpack: Unable to find view file $views_dir$template" ); 
  5856.         return false; 
  5857.     } 
  5858.  
  5859.     /** 
  5860.      * Throws warnings for deprecated hooks to be removed from Jetpack 
  5861.      */ 
  5862.     public function deprecated_hooks() { 
  5863.         global $wp_filter; 
  5864.  
  5865.         /** 
  5866.          * Format: 
  5867.          * deprecated_filter_name => replacement_name 
  5868.          * 
  5869.          * If there is no replacement, use null for replacement_name 
  5870.          */ 
  5871.         $deprecated_list = array( 
  5872.             'jetpack_bail_on_shortcode' => 'jetpack_shortcodes_to_include',  
  5873.             'wpl_sharing_2014_1' => null,  
  5874.             'jetpack-tools-to-include' => 'jetpack_tools_to_include',  
  5875.             'jetpack_identity_crisis_options_to_check' => null,  
  5876.             'update_option_jetpack_single_user_site' => null,  
  5877.             'audio_player_default_colors' => null,  
  5878.             'add_option_jetpack_featured_images_enabled' => null,  
  5879.             'add_option_jetpack_update_details' => null,  
  5880.             'add_option_jetpack_updates' => null,  
  5881.             'add_option_jetpack_network_name' => null,  
  5882.             'add_option_jetpack_network_allow_new_registrations' => null,  
  5883.             'add_option_jetpack_network_add_new_users' => null,  
  5884.             'add_option_jetpack_network_site_upload_space' => null,  
  5885.             'add_option_jetpack_network_upload_file_types' => null,  
  5886.             'add_option_jetpack_network_enable_administration_menus' => null,  
  5887.             'add_option_jetpack_is_multi_site' => null,  
  5888.             'add_option_jetpack_is_main_network' => null,  
  5889.             'add_option_jetpack_main_network_site' => null,  
  5890.             'jetpack_sync_all_registered_options' => null,  
  5891.             'jetpack_has_identity_crisis' => 'jetpack_sync_error_idc_validation',  
  5892.             'jetpack_is_post_mailable' => null,  
  5893.  ); 
  5894.  
  5895.         // This is a silly loop depth. Better way? 
  5896.         foreach( $deprecated_list AS $hook => $hook_alt ) { 
  5897.             if ( has_action( $hook ) ) { 
  5898.                 foreach( $wp_filter[ $hook ] AS $func => $values ) { 
  5899.                     foreach( $values AS $hooked ) { 
  5900.                         if ( is_callable( $hooked['function'] ) ) { 
  5901.                             $function_name = 'an anonymous function'; 
  5902.                         } else { 
  5903.                             $function_name = $hooked['function']; 
  5904.                         } 
  5905.                         _deprecated_function( $hook . ' used for ' . $function_name, null, $hook_alt ); 
  5906.                     } 
  5907.                 } 
  5908.             } 
  5909.         } 
  5910.     } 
  5911.  
  5912.     /** 
  5913.      * Converts any url in a stylesheet, to the correct absolute url. 
  5914.      * 
  5915.      * Considerations: 
  5916.      *  - Normal, relative URLs     `feh.png` 
  5917.      *  - Data URLs                 `data:image/gif;base64, eh129ehiuehjdhsa==` 
  5918.      *  - Schema-agnostic URLs      `//domain.com/feh.png` 
  5919.      *  - Absolute URLs             `http://domain.com/feh.png` 
  5920.      *  - Domain root relative URLs `/feh.png` 
  5921.      * 
  5922.      * @param $css string: The raw CSS -- should be read in directly from the file. 
  5923.      * @param $css_file_url : The URL that the file can be accessed at, for calculating paths from. 
  5924.      * 
  5925.      * @return mixed|string 
  5926.      */ 
  5927.     public static function absolutize_css_urls( $css, $css_file_url ) { 
  5928.         $pattern = '#url\((?P<path>[^)]*)\)#i'; 
  5929.         $css_dir = dirname( $css_file_url ); 
  5930.         $p = parse_url( $css_dir ); 
  5931.         $domain = sprintf( 
  5932.                     '%1$s//%2$s%3$s%4$s',  
  5933.                     isset( $p['scheme'] )           ? "{$p['scheme']}:" : '',  
  5934.                     isset( $p['user'], $p['pass'] ) ? "{$p['user']}:{$p['pass']}@" : '',  
  5935.                     $p['host'],  
  5936.                     isset( $p['port'] )             ? ":{$p['port']}" : '' 
  5937.  ); 
  5938.  
  5939.         if ( preg_match_all( $pattern, $css, $matches, PREG_SET_ORDER ) ) { 
  5940.             $find = $replace = array(); 
  5941.             foreach ( $matches as $match ) { 
  5942.                 $url = trim( $match['path'], "'\" \t" ); 
  5943.  
  5944.                 // If this is a data url, we don't want to mess with it. 
  5945.                 if ( 'data:' === substr( $url, 0, 5 ) ) { 
  5946.                     continue; 
  5947.                 } 
  5948.  
  5949.                 // If this is an absolute or protocol-agnostic url,  
  5950.                 // we don't want to mess with it. 
  5951.                 if ( preg_match( '#^(https?:)?//#i', $url ) ) { 
  5952.                     continue; 
  5953.                 } 
  5954.  
  5955.                 switch ( substr( $url, 0, 1 ) ) { 
  5956.                     case '/': 
  5957.                         $absolute = $domain . $url; 
  5958.                         break; 
  5959.                     default: 
  5960.                         $absolute = $css_dir . '/' . $url; 
  5961.                 } 
  5962.  
  5963.                 $find[] = $match[0]; 
  5964.                 $replace[] = sprintf( 'url("%s")', $absolute ); 
  5965.             } 
  5966.             $css = str_replace( $find, $replace, $css ); 
  5967.         } 
  5968.  
  5969.         return $css; 
  5970.     } 
  5971.  
  5972.     /** 
  5973.      * This methods removes all of the registered css files on the front end 
  5974.      * from Jetpack in favor of using a single file. In effect "imploding" 
  5975.      * all the files into one file. 
  5976.      * 
  5977.      * Pros: 
  5978.      * - Uses only ONE css asset connection instead of 15 
  5979.      * - Saves a minimum of 56k 
  5980.      * - Reduces server load 
  5981.      * - Reduces time to first painted byte 
  5982.      * 
  5983.      * Cons: 
  5984.      * - Loads css for ALL modules. However all selectors are prefixed so it 
  5985.      *        should not cause any issues with themes. 
  5986.      * - Plugins/themes dequeuing styles no longer do anything. See 
  5987.      *        jetpack_implode_frontend_css filter for a workaround 
  5988.      * 
  5989.      * For some situations developers may wish to disable css imploding and 
  5990.      * instead operate in legacy mode where each file loads seperately and 
  5991.      * can be edited individually or dequeued. This can be accomplished with 
  5992.      * the following line: 
  5993.      * 
  5994.      * add_filter( 'jetpack_implode_frontend_css', '__return_false' ); 
  5995.      * 
  5996.      * @since 3.2 
  5997.      **/ 
  5998.     public function implode_frontend_css( $travis_test = false ) { 
  5999.         $do_implode = true; 
  6000.         if ( defined( 'SCRIPT_DEBUG' ) && SCRIPT_DEBUG ) { 
  6001.             $do_implode = false; 
  6002.         } 
  6003.  
  6004.         /** 
  6005.          * Allow CSS to be concatenated into a single jetpack.css file. 
  6006.          * 
  6007.          * @since 3.2.0 
  6008.          * 
  6009.          * @param bool $do_implode Should CSS be concatenated? Default to true. 
  6010.          */ 
  6011.         $do_implode = apply_filters( 'jetpack_implode_frontend_css', $do_implode ); 
  6012.  
  6013.         // Do not use the imploded file when default behaviour was altered through the filter 
  6014.         if ( ! $do_implode ) { 
  6015.             return; 
  6016.         } 
  6017.  
  6018.         // We do not want to use the imploded file in dev mode, or if not connected 
  6019.         if ( Jetpack::is_development_mode() || ! self::is_active() ) { 
  6020.             if ( ! $travis_test ) { 
  6021.                 return; 
  6022.             } 
  6023.         } 
  6024.  
  6025.         // Do not use the imploded file if sharing css was dequeued via the sharing settings screen 
  6026.         if ( get_option( 'sharedaddy_disable_resources' ) ) { 
  6027.             return; 
  6028.         } 
  6029.  
  6030.         /** 
  6031.          * Now we assume Jetpack is connected and able to serve the single 
  6032.          * file. 
  6033.          * 
  6034.          * In the future there will be a check here to serve the file locally 
  6035.          * or potentially from the Jetpack CDN 
  6036.          * 
  6037.          * For now: 
  6038.          * - Enqueue a single imploded css file 
  6039.          * - Zero out the style_loader_tag for the bundled ones 
  6040.          * - Be happy, drink scotch 
  6041.          */ 
  6042.  
  6043.         add_filter( 'style_loader_tag', array( $this, 'concat_remove_style_loader_tag' ), 10, 2 ); 
  6044.  
  6045.         $version = Jetpack::is_development_version() ? filemtime( JETPACK__PLUGIN_DIR . 'css/jetpack.css' ) : JETPACK__VERSION; 
  6046.  
  6047.         wp_enqueue_style( 'jetpack_css', plugins_url( 'css/jetpack.css', __FILE__ ), array(), $version ); 
  6048.         wp_style_add_data( 'jetpack_css', 'rtl', 'replace' ); 
  6049.     } 
  6050.  
  6051.     function concat_remove_style_loader_tag( $tag, $handle ) { 
  6052.         if ( in_array( $handle, $this->concatenated_style_handles ) ) { 
  6053.             $tag = ''; 
  6054.             if ( defined( 'WP_DEBUG' ) && WP_DEBUG ) { 
  6055.                 $tag = "<!-- `" . esc_html( $handle ) . "` is included in the concatenated jetpack.css -->\r\n"; 
  6056.             } 
  6057.         } 
  6058.  
  6059.         return $tag; 
  6060.     } 
  6061.  
  6062.     /** 
  6063.      * Check the heartbeat data 
  6064.      * 
  6065.      * Organizes the heartbeat data by severity.  For example, if the site 
  6066.      * is in an ID crisis, it will be in the $filtered_data['bad'] array. 
  6067.      * 
  6068.      * Data will be added to "caution" array, if it either: 
  6069.      *  - Out of date Jetpack version 
  6070.      *  - Out of date WP version 
  6071.      *  - Out of date PHP version 
  6072.      * 
  6073.      * $return array $filtered_data 
  6074.      */ 
  6075.     public static function jetpack_check_heartbeat_data() { 
  6076.         $raw_data = Jetpack_Heartbeat::generate_stats_array(); 
  6077.  
  6078.         $good = array(); 
  6079.         $caution = array(); 
  6080.         $bad = array(); 
  6081.  
  6082.         foreach ( $raw_data as $stat => $value ) { 
  6083.  
  6084.             // Check jetpack version 
  6085.             if ( 'version' == $stat ) { 
  6086.                 if ( version_compare( $value, JETPACK__VERSION, '<' ) ) { 
  6087.                     $caution[ $stat ] = $value . " - min supported is " . JETPACK__VERSION; 
  6088.                     continue; 
  6089.                 } 
  6090.             } 
  6091.  
  6092.             // Check WP version 
  6093.             if ( 'wp-version' == $stat ) { 
  6094.                 if ( version_compare( $value, JETPACK__MINIMUM_WP_VERSION, '<' ) ) { 
  6095.                     $caution[ $stat ] = $value . " - min supported is " . JETPACK__MINIMUM_WP_VERSION; 
  6096.                     continue; 
  6097.                 } 
  6098.             } 
  6099.  
  6100.             // Check PHP version 
  6101.             if ( 'php-version' == $stat ) { 
  6102.                 if ( version_compare( PHP_VERSION, '5.2.4', '<' ) ) { 
  6103.                     $caution[ $stat ] = $value . " - min supported is 5.2.4"; 
  6104.                     continue; 
  6105.                 } 
  6106.             } 
  6107.  
  6108.             // Check ID crisis 
  6109.             if ( 'identitycrisis' == $stat ) { 
  6110.                 if ( 'yes' == $value ) { 
  6111.                     $bad[ $stat ] = $value; 
  6112.                     continue; 
  6113.                 } 
  6114.             } 
  6115.  
  6116.             // The rest are good :) 
  6117.             $good[ $stat ] = $value; 
  6118.         } 
  6119.  
  6120.         $filtered_data = array( 
  6121.             'good' => $good,  
  6122.             'caution' => $caution,  
  6123.             'bad' => $bad 
  6124.  ); 
  6125.  
  6126.         return $filtered_data; 
  6127.     } 
  6128.  
  6129.  
  6130.     /** 
  6131.      * This method is used to organize all options that can be reset 
  6132.      * without disconnecting Jetpack. 
  6133.      * 
  6134.      * It is used in class.jetpack-cli.php to reset options 
  6135.      * 
  6136.      * @return array of options to delete. 
  6137.      */ 
  6138.     public static function get_jetpack_options_for_reset() { 
  6139.         $jetpack_options = Jetpack_Options::get_option_names(); 
  6140.         $jetpack_options_non_compat = Jetpack_Options::get_option_names( 'non_compact' ); 
  6141.         $jetpack_options_private = Jetpack_Options::get_option_names( 'private' ); 
  6142.  
  6143.         $all_jp_options = array_merge( $jetpack_options, $jetpack_options_non_compat, $jetpack_options_private ); 
  6144.  
  6145.         // A manual build of the wp options 
  6146.         $wp_options = array( 
  6147.             'sharing-options',  
  6148.             'disabled_likes',  
  6149.             'disabled_reblogs',  
  6150.             'jetpack_comments_likes_enabled',  
  6151.             'wp_mobile_excerpt',  
  6152.             'wp_mobile_featured_images',  
  6153.             'wp_mobile_app_promos',  
  6154.             'stats_options',  
  6155.             'stats_dashboard_widget',  
  6156.             'safecss_preview_rev',  
  6157.             'safecss_rev',  
  6158.             'safecss_revision_migrated',  
  6159.             'nova_menu_order',  
  6160.             'jetpack_portfolio',  
  6161.             'jetpack_portfolio_posts_per_page',  
  6162.             'jetpack_testimonial',  
  6163.             'jetpack_testimonial_posts_per_page',  
  6164.             'wp_mobile_custom_css',  
  6165.             'sharedaddy_disable_resources',  
  6166.             'sharing-options',  
  6167.             'sharing-services',  
  6168.             'site_icon_temp_data',  
  6169.             'featured-content',  
  6170.             'site_logo',  
  6171.             'jetpack_dismissed_notices',  
  6172.  ); 
  6173.  
  6174.         // Flag some Jetpack options as unsafe 
  6175.         $unsafe_options = array( 
  6176.             'id', // (int)    The Client ID/WP.com Blog ID of this site. 
  6177.             'master_user', // (int)    The local User ID of the user who connected this site to jetpack.wordpress.com. 
  6178.             'version', // (string) Used during upgrade procedure to auto-activate new modules. version:time 
  6179.             'jumpstart', // (string) A flag for whether or not to show the Jump Start.  Accepts: new_connection, jumpstart_activated, jetpack_action_taken, jumpstart_dismissed. 
  6180.  
  6181.             // non_compact 
  6182.             'activated',  
  6183.  
  6184.             // private 
  6185.             'register',  
  6186.             'blog_token', // (string) The Client Secret/Blog Token of this site. 
  6187.             'user_token', // (string) The User Token of this site. (deprecated) 
  6188.             'user_tokens' 
  6189.  ); 
  6190.  
  6191.         // Remove the unsafe Jetpack options 
  6192.         foreach ( $unsafe_options as $unsafe_option ) { 
  6193.             if ( false !== ( $key = array_search( $unsafe_option, $all_jp_options ) ) ) { 
  6194.                 unset( $all_jp_options[ $key ] ); 
  6195.             } 
  6196.         } 
  6197.  
  6198.         $options = array( 
  6199.             'jp_options' => $all_jp_options,  
  6200.             'wp_options' => $wp_options 
  6201.  ); 
  6202.  
  6203.         return $options; 
  6204.     } 
  6205.  
  6206.     /** 
  6207.      * Check if an option of a Jetpack module has been updated. 
  6208.      * 
  6209.      * If any module option has been updated before Jump Start has been dismissed,  
  6210.      * update the 'jumpstart' option so we can hide Jump Start. 
  6211.      * 
  6212.      * @param string $option_name 
  6213.      * 
  6214.      * @return bool 
  6215.      */ 
  6216.     public static function jumpstart_has_updated_module_option( $option_name = '' ) { 
  6217.         // Bail if Jump Start has already been dismissed 
  6218.         if ( 'new_connection' !== Jetpack_Options::get_option( 'jumpstart' ) ) { 
  6219.             return false; 
  6220.         } 
  6221.  
  6222.         $jetpack = Jetpack::init(); 
  6223.  
  6224.         // Manual build of module options 
  6225.         $option_names = self::get_jetpack_options_for_reset(); 
  6226.  
  6227.         if ( in_array( $option_name, $option_names['wp_options'] ) ) { 
  6228.             Jetpack_Options::update_option( 'jumpstart', 'jetpack_action_taken' ); 
  6229.  
  6230.             //Jump start is being dismissed send data to MC Stats 
  6231.             $jetpack->stat( 'jumpstart', 'manual, '.$option_name ); 
  6232.  
  6233.             $jetpack->do_stats( 'server_side' ); 
  6234.         } 
  6235.  
  6236.     } 
  6237.  
  6238.     /** 
  6239.      * Strip http:// or https:// from a url, replaces forward slash with ::,  
  6240.      * so we can bring them directly to their site in calypso. 
  6241.      * 
  6242.      * @param string | url 
  6243.      * @return string | url without the guff 
  6244.      */ 
  6245.     public static function build_raw_urls( $url ) { 
  6246.         $strip_http = '/.*?:\/\//i'; 
  6247.         $url = preg_replace( $strip_http, '', $url ); 
  6248.         $url = str_replace( '/', '::', $url ); 
  6249.         return $url; 
  6250.     } 
  6251.  
  6252.     /** 
  6253.      * Stores and prints out domains to prefetch for page speed optimization. 
  6254.      * 
  6255.      * @param mixed $new_urls 
  6256.      */ 
  6257.     public static function dns_prefetch( $new_urls = null ) { 
  6258.         static $prefetch_urls = array(); 
  6259.         if ( empty( $new_urls ) && ! empty( $prefetch_urls ) ) { 
  6260.             echo "\r\n"; 
  6261.             foreach ( $prefetch_urls as $this_prefetch_url ) { 
  6262.                 printf( "<link rel='dns-prefetch' href='%s'>\r\n", esc_attr( $this_prefetch_url ) ); 
  6263.             } 
  6264.         } elseif ( ! empty( $new_urls ) ) { 
  6265.             if ( ! has_action( 'wp_head', array( __CLASS__, __FUNCTION__ ) ) ) { 
  6266.                 add_action( 'wp_head', array( __CLASS__, __FUNCTION__ ) ); 
  6267.             } 
  6268.             foreach ( (array) $new_urls as $this_new_url ) { 
  6269.                 $prefetch_urls[] = strtolower( untrailingslashit( preg_replace( '#^https?://#i', '//', $this_new_url ) ) ); 
  6270.             } 
  6271.             $prefetch_urls = array_unique( $prefetch_urls ); 
  6272.         } 
  6273.     }

  6275.     public function wp_dashboard_setup() { 
  6276.         if ( self::is_active() ) { 
  6277.             add_action( 'jetpack_dashboard_widget', array( __CLASS__, 'dashboard_widget_footer' ), 999 ); 
  6278.             $widget_title = __( 'Site Stats', 'jetpack' ); 
  6279.         } elseif ( ! self::is_development_mode() && current_user_can( 'jetpack_connect' ) ) { 
  6280.             add_action( 'jetpack_dashboard_widget', array( $this, 'dashboard_widget_connect_to_wpcom' ) ); 
  6281.             $widget_title = __( 'Please Connect Jetpack', 'jetpack' ); 
  6282.         } 
  6283.  
  6284.         if ( has_action( 'jetpack_dashboard_widget' ) ) { 
  6285.             wp_add_dashboard_widget( 
  6286.                 'jetpack_summary_widget',  
  6287.                 $widget_title,  
  6288.                 array( __CLASS__, 'dashboard_widget' ) 
  6289.  ); 
  6290.             wp_enqueue_style( 'jetpack-dashboard-widget', plugins_url( 'css/dashboard-widget.css', JETPACK__PLUGIN_FILE ), array(), JETPACK__VERSION ); 
  6291.  
  6292.             // If we're inactive and not in development mode, sort our box to the top. 
  6293.             if ( ! self::is_active() && ! self::is_development_mode() ) { 
  6294.                 global $wp_meta_boxes; 
  6295.  
  6296.                 $dashboard = $wp_meta_boxes['dashboard']['normal']['core']; 
  6297.                 $ours = array( 'jetpack_summary_widget' => $dashboard['jetpack_summary_widget'] ); 
  6298.  
  6299.                 $wp_meta_boxes['dashboard']['normal']['core'] = array_merge( $ours, $dashboard ); 
  6300.             } 
  6301.         } 
  6302.     }

  6304.     /** 
  6305.      * @param mixed $result Value for the user's option 
  6306.      * @return mixed 
  6307.      */ 
  6308.     function get_user_option_meta_box_order_dashboard( $sorted ) { 
  6309.         if ( ! is_array( $sorted ) ) { 
  6310.             return $sorted; 
  6311.         } 
  6312.  
  6313.         foreach ( $sorted as $box_context => $ids ) { 
  6314.             if ( false === strpos( $ids, 'dashboard_stats' ) ) { 
  6315.                 // If the old id isn't anywhere in the ids, don't bother exploding and fail out. 
  6316.                 continue; 
  6317.             } 
  6318.  
  6319.             $ids_array = explode( ', ', $ids ); 
  6320.             $key = array_search( 'dashboard_stats', $ids_array ); 
  6321.  
  6322.             if ( false !== $key ) { 
  6323.                 // If we've found that exact value in the option (and not `google_dashboard_stats` for example) 
  6324.                 $ids_array[ $key ] = 'jetpack_summary_widget'; 
  6325.                 $sorted[ $box_context ] = implode( ', ', $ids_array ); 
  6326.                 // We've found it, stop searching, and just return. 
  6327.                 break; 
  6328.             } 
  6329.         } 
  6330.  
  6331.         return $sorted; 
  6332.     }

  6411.     /**

  6413.      */ 
  6414.     function jetpack_icon_user_connected( $columns ) {

  6419.     /** 
  6420.      * Show Jetpack icon if the user is linked. 
  6421.      */ 
  6422.     function jetpack_show_user_connected_icon( $val, $col, $user_id ) { 
  6423.         if ( 'user_jetpack' == $col && Jetpack::is_user_connected( $user_id ) ) { 
  6424.             $emblem_html = sprintf( 
  6425.                 '<a title="%1$s" class="jp-emblem-user-admin">%2$s</a>',  
  6426.                 esc_attr__( 'This user is linked and ready to fly with Jetpack.', 'jetpack' ),  
  6427.                 Jetpack::get_jp_emblem() 
  6428.  ); 
  6429.             return $emblem_html; 
  6430.         } 
  6431.  
  6432.         return $val; 
  6433.     }
